Generative Models in Decision Making: A Survey
Authors: Xinyu Shao, Jianping Zhang, Haozhi Wang, Leo Maxime Brunswic, Kaiwen Zhou, Jiqian Dong, Kaiyang Guo, Zhitang Chen, Jun Wang, Jianye Hao, Xiu Li, Yinchuan Li
First: 2025-02-24T12:31:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T10:16:35+00:00
Comments: Project page:https://github.com/xyshao23/Awesome-Generative-Models-for-Decision-Making-Taxonomy
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Generative models have fundamentally reshaped the landscape of decision-making, reframing the problem from pure scalar reward maximization to high-fidelity trajectory generation and distribution matching. This paradigm shift addresses intrinsic limitations in classical Reinforcement Learning (RL), particularly the limited expressivity of standard unimodal policy distributions in capturing complex, multi-modal behaviors embedded in diverse datasets. However, current literature often treats these models as isolated algorithmic improvements, rarely synthesizing them into a single comprehensive framework. This survey proposes a principled taxonomy grounding generative decision-making within the probabilistic framework of Control as Inference. By performing a variational factorization of the trajectory posterior, we conceptualize four distinct functional roles: Controllers for amortized policy inference, Modelers for dynamics priors, Optimizers for iterative trajectory refinement, and Evaluators for trajectory guidance and value assessment. Unlike existing architecture-centric reviews, this function-centric framework allows us to critically analyze representative generative families across distinct dimensions. Furthermore, we examine deployment in high-stakes domains, specifically Embodied AI, Autonomous Driving, and AI for Science, highlighting systemic risks such as dynamics hallucination in world models and proxy exploitation. Finally, we chart the path toward Generalist Physical Intelligence, identifying pivotal challenges in inference efficiency, trustworthiness, and the emergence of Physical Foundation Models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：决策中的生成模型：综述
生成模型从根本上重塑了决策领域，将问题从纯粹的标量奖励最大化重构为高保真轨迹生成与分布匹配。这一范式转变解决了经典强化学习的内在局限，尤其是标准单峰策略分布在捕捉多样化数据集中蕴含的复杂多模态行为时表达能力有限的问题。然而，现有文献常将这些模型视为孤立的算法改进，鲜少将其整合为统一框架。本综述提出一种原则性分类法，将生成式决策置于'控制即推理'的概率框架中。通过对轨迹后验进行变分分解，我们概念化了四种功能角色：用于摊销策略推理的控制器、用于动力学先验的建模器、用于迭代轨迹优化的优化器，以及用于轨迹引导与价值评估的评估器。与现有以架构为中心的综述不同，这种以功能为中心的框架使我们能批判性分析不同维度的代表性生成模型族。此外，我们考察了高风险领域的部署，特别是具身人工智能、自动驾驶与科学人工智能，揭示了世界模型中的动力学幻觉与代理利用等系统性风险。最后，我们规划了通向通用物理智能的路径，指出了推理效率、可信度及物理基础模型涌现等关键挑战。
Summary / 总结
This survey is motivated by the paradigm shift in decision-making from reward maximization to trajectory generation, aiming to address the limited expressivity of classical RL policies and synthesize disparate generative models into a unified framework. The method proposes a principled taxonomy based on Control as Inference, categorizing models into four functional roles—Controllers, Modelers, Optimizers, and Evaluators—through variational factorization of the trajectory posterior, enabling a function-centric analysis across dimensions. Key experimental insights highlight applications in high-stakes domains like Embodied AI and Autonomous Driving, revealing systemic risks such as dynamics hallucination, while charting future challenges toward Generalist Physical Intelligence in inference efficiency and trustworthiness.
本综述的动机在于决策范式从奖励最大化转向轨迹生成，旨在解决经典强化学习中策略表达能力有限的问题，并将分散的生成模型整合为统一框架。方法上，基于“控制即推理”的概率框架提出了一种原则性分类法，通过对轨迹后验进行变分分解，将模型划分为控制器、建模器、优化器和评估器四个功能角色，实现了跨维度的功能中心分析。主要实验成果聚焦于具身人工智能和自动驾驶等高风险领域的应用，揭示了动态幻觉等系统性风险，并展望了迈向通用物理智能过程中在推理效率和可信度等方面的关键挑战。
BioLLMAgent: A Hybrid Framework with Enhanced Structural Interpretability for Simulating Human Decision-Making in Computational Psychiatry
Authors: Zuo Fei, Kezhi Wang, Xiaomin Chen, Yizhou Huang
First: 2026-03-05T10:04:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T10:04:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Computational psychiatry faces a fundamental trade-off: traditional reinforcement learning (RL) models offer interpretability but lack behavioral realism, while large language model (LLM) agents generate realistic behaviors but lack structural interpretability. We introduce BioLLMAgent, a novel hybrid framework that combines validated cognitive models with the generative capabilities of LLMs. The framework comprises three core components: (i) an Internal RL Engine for experience-driven value learning; (ii) an External LLM Shell for high-level cognitive strategies and therapeutic interventions; and (iii) a Decision Fusion Mechanism for integrating components via weighted utility. Comprehensive experiments on the Iowa Gambling Task (IGT) across six clinical and healthy datasets demonstrate that BioLLMAgent accurately reproduces human behavioral patterns while maintaining excellent parameter identifiability (correlations $>0.67$). Furthermore, the framework successfully simulates cognitive behavioral therapy (CBT) principles and reveals, through multi-agent dynamics, that community-wide educational interventions may outperform individual treatments. Validated across reward-punishment learning and temporal discounting tasks, BioLLMAgent provides a structurally interpretable "computational sandbox" for testing mechanistic hypotheses and intervention strategies in psychiatric research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BioLLMAgent：一种具有增强结构可解释性的混合框架，用于模拟计算精神病学中的人类决策
计算精神病学面临一个根本性权衡：传统强化学习（RL）模型具有可解释性但缺乏行为真实性，而大型语言模型（LLM）智能体能生成真实行为却缺乏结构可解释性。我们提出了BioLLMAgent，一种新颖的混合框架，将经过验证的认知模型与LLM的生成能力相结合。该框架包含三个核心组件：（i）用于经验驱动价值学习的内部RL引擎；（ii）用于高层认知策略与治疗干预的外部LLM外壳；（iii）通过加权效用整合组件的决策融合机制。在爱荷华赌博任务（IGT）上对六个临床与健康数据集进行的综合实验表明，BioLLMAgent能准确复现人类行为模式，同时保持优异的参数可识别性（相关性>0.67）。此外，该框架成功模拟了认知行为疗法（CBT）原则，并通过多智能体动力学揭示，社区范围的教育干预可能优于个体治疗。在奖赏-惩罚学习与时间折扣任务中的验证表明，BioLLMAgent为精神病学研究的机制假设和干预策略测试提供了一个结构可解释的“计算沙箱”。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the trade-off in computational psychiatry between the interpretability of traditional reinforcement learning models and the behavioral realism of large language model agents, this paper introduces BioLLMAgent, a hybrid framework combining cognitive models with LLMs. The method integrates an internal RL engine for value learning, an external LLM shell for high-level strategies, and a decision fusion mechanism, enabling simulation of human decision-making. Experimental results on the Iowa Gambling Task across clinical and healthy datasets show that BioLLMAgent accurately reproduces human behavior with high parameter identifiability (correlations >0.67), simulates cognitive behavioral therapy, and suggests community-wide interventions may outperform individual treatments, validated across multiple tasks.
本研究针对计算精神病学中传统强化学习模型可解释性强但行为真实性不足、而大语言模型智能体行为真实但结构可解释性差的权衡问题，提出了BioLLMAgent这一结合认知模型与大语言模型的混合框架。该方法通过内部强化学习引擎进行价值学习、外部大语言模型外壳处理高级认知策略与治疗干预、以及决策融合机制进行加权整合，以模拟人类决策过程。在爱荷华赌博任务上对临床和健康数据集的实验表明，BioLLMAgent能准确复现人类行为模式且参数可识别性优异（相关性>0.67），成功模拟了认知行为治疗原则，并通过多智能体动态揭示社区教育干预可能优于个体治疗，该框架在奖赏惩罚学习和时间折扣任务中均得到验证。
Competitive Multi-Operator Reinforcement Learning for Joint Pricing and Fleet Rebalancing in AMoD Systems
Authors: Emil Kragh Toft, Carolin Schmidt, Daniele Gammelli, Filipe Rodrigues
First: 2026-03-05T09:44:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T09:44:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous Mobility-on-Demand (AMoD) systems promise to revolutionize urban transportation by providing affordable on-demand services to meet growing travel demand. However, realistic AMoD markets will be competitive, with multiple operators competing for passengers through strategic pricing and fleet deployment. While reinforcement learning has shown promise in optimizing single-operator AMoD control, existing work fails to capture competitive market dynamics. We investigate the impact of competition on policy learning by introducing a multi-operator reinforcement learning framework where two operators simultaneously learn pricing and fleet rebalancing policies. By integrating discrete choice theory, we enable passenger allocation and demand competition to emerge endogenously from utility-maximizing decisions. Experiments using real-world data from multiple cities demonstrate that competition fundamentally alters learned behaviors, leading to lower prices and distinct fleet positioning patterns compared to monopolistic settings. Notably, we demonstrate that learning-based approaches are robust to the additional stochasticity of competition, with competitive agents successfully converging to effective policies while accounting for partially unobserved competitor strategies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：竞争性多运营商强化学习在AMoD系统中联合定价与车队再平衡的应用
自主按需出行（AMoD）系统有望通过提供经济实惠的按需服务来满足日益增长的出行需求，从而彻底改变城市交通。然而，现实的AMoD市场将充满竞争，多个运营商通过战略性定价和车队部署争夺乘客。尽管强化学习在优化单运营商AMoD控制方面显示出潜力，但现有研究未能捕捉竞争性市场动态。我们通过引入一个多运营商强化学习框架，研究竞争对策略学习的影响，其中两个运营商同时学习定价和车队再平衡策略。通过整合离散选择理论，我们使乘客分配和需求竞争从效用最大化的决策中内生地产生。利用来自多个城市的真实数据进行的实验表明，与垄断环境相比，竞争从根本上改变了学习到的行为，导致价格降低和独特的车队布局模式。值得注意的是，我们证明了基于学习的方法对竞争带来的额外随机性具有鲁棒性，竞争智能体能够成功收敛到有效策略，同时考虑到部分未观察到的竞争对手策略。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to model competitive dynamics in Autonomous Mobility-on-Demand (AMoD) markets, where existing single-operator reinforcement learning approaches fail to capture strategic interactions between multiple firms. The method introduces a multi-operator reinforcement learning framework where two competing operators simultaneously learn joint pricing and fleet rebalancing policies, integrating discrete choice theory to endogenously model passenger allocation based on utility maximization. Experimental results using real-world city data show that competition fundamentally alters learned behaviors, leading to lower prices and distinct fleet positioning compared to monopolistic settings, and that the learning-based agents robustly converge to effective policies despite the stochasticity and partial observability of competitor strategies.
本文的研究动机在于需要对自动驾驶按需出行（AMoD）市场中的竞争动态进行建模，因为现有的单运营商强化学习方法无法捕捉多个企业间的战略互动。该方法提出了一个多运营商强化学习框架，其中两个竞争运营商同时学习联合定价和车队再平衡策略，并整合离散选择理论，以基于效用最大化内生地模拟乘客分配。使用多个城市的真实数据进行的实验表明，竞争从根本上改变了学习到的行为，与垄断环境相比，导致了更低的价格和独特的车队布局模式，并且基于学习的智能体能够稳健地收敛到有效策略，尽管面临竞争对手策略的随机性和部分可观测性。
Learn Hard Problems During RL with Reference Guided Fine-tuning
Authors: Yangzhen Wu, Shanda Li, Zixin Wen, Xin Zhou, Ameet Talwalkar, Yiming Yang, Wenhao Huang, Tianle Cai
First: 2026-03-01T18:41:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T09:33:10+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) for mathematical reasoning can suffer from reward sparsity: for challenging problems, LLM fails to sample any correct trajectories, preventing RL from receiving meaningful positive feedback. At the same time, there often exist human-written reference solutions along with the problem (e.g., problems from AoPS), but directly fine-tuning on these solutions offers no benefit because models often cannot imitate human proofs that lie outside their own reasoning distribution. We introduce Reference-Guided Fine-Tuning (ReGFT), a simple and effective method that utilizes human-written reference solutions to synthesize positive trajectories on hard problems and train on them before RL. For each problem, we provide the model with a partial reference solution and let it generate its own reasoning trace, ensuring the resulting trajectories remain in the model's reasoning space while still benefiting from reference guidance. Fine-tuning on these reference-guided trajectories increases the number of solvable problems and produces a checkpoint that receives more positive rewards during RL. Across three benchmarks (AIME24, AIME25, BeyondAIME), ReGFT consistently improves supervised accuracy, accelerates DAPO training, and raises the final performance plateau of RL. Our results show that ReGFT effectively overcomes reward sparsity and unlocks stronger RL-based mathematical reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于参考引导微调在强化学习中攻克难题
数学推理的强化学习（RL）常面临奖励稀疏问题：面对难题时，大语言模型（LLM）无法采样到任何正确轨迹，导致RL无法获得有效的正向反馈。同时，题目常附有人工撰写的参考答案（如AoPS题库），但直接对这些解答进行微调收效甚微，因为模型往往难以模仿超出其自身推理分布的人类证明过程。 我们提出参考引导微调（ReGFT），这是一种简单有效的方法：在RL训练前，利用人工参考答案为难题合成正向轨迹进行训练。针对每个问题，我们向模型提供部分参考答案，并让其生成自身的推理轨迹，确保所得轨迹既保持在模型的推理空间内，又能受益于参考引导。 基于这些参考引导轨迹的微调，可提升模型可解问题的数量，并产生能在RL过程中获得更多正向奖励的检查点。在三个基准测试（AIME24、AIME25、BeyondAIME）中，ReGFT持续提升监督学习准确率，加速DAPO训练，并提高RL的最终性能上限。实验结果表明，ReGFT能有效克服奖励稀疏问题，释放基于RL的数学推理更强潜力。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of reward sparsity in reinforcement learning (RL) for mathematical reasoning, where large language models often fail to generate correct solutions to hard problems, leaving RL without positive feedback. The authors propose Reference-Guided Fine-Tuning (ReGFT), a method that leverages human-written reference solutions to synthesize positive training trajectories: for each problem, the model is given a partial reference and generates its own reasoning trace, ensuring the trajectory stays within its reasoning distribution while benefiting from guidance. Experimental results on benchmarks including AIME24, AIME25, and BeyondAIME demonstrate that ReGFT increases solvable problems, accelerates DAPO training, and raises the final performance plateau of RL, effectively overcoming reward sparsity and enhancing mathematical reasoning.
本文针对数学推理中强化学习的奖励稀疏性问题，即大语言模型在解决难题时难以生成正确解，导致强化学习缺乏正向反馈。作者提出了参考引导微调方法，利用人工编写的参考答案合成正向训练轨迹：针对每个问题，模型接收部分参考答案并生成自己的推理轨迹，确保轨迹保持在模型推理分布内同时获得引导。在AIME24、AIME25和BeyondAIME等基准测试上的实验结果表明，该方法增加了可解问题数量，加速了DAPO训练，并提升了强化学习的最终性能上限，有效克服了奖励稀疏性并增强了数学推理能力。
Achieving Olympia-Level Geometry Large Language Model Agent via Complexity Boosting Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Haiteng Zhao, Junhao Shen, Yiming Zhang, Songyang Gao, Kuikun Liu, Tianyou Ma, Fan Zheng, Dahua Lin, Wenwei Zhang, Kai Chen
First: 2025-12-11T11:05:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T09:33:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents exhibit strong mathematical problem-solving abilities and can even solve International Mathematical Olympiad (IMO) level problems with the assistance of formal proof systems. However, due to weak heuristics for auxiliary constructions, AI for geometry problem solving remains dominated by expert models such as AlphaGeometry 2, which rely heavily on large-scale data synthesis and search for both training and evaluation. In this work, we make the first attempt to build a medalist-level LLM agent for geometry and present InternGeometry. InternGeometry overcomes the heuristic limitations in geometry by iteratively proposing propositions and auxiliary constructions, verifying them with a symbolic engine, and reflecting on the engine's feedback to guide subsequent proposals. A dynamic memory mechanism enables InternGeometry to conduct more than two hundred interactions with the symbolic engine per problem. To further accelerate learning, we introduce Complexity-Boosting Reinforcement Learning (CBRL), which gradually increases the complexity of synthesized problems across training stages. Built on InternThinker-32B, InternGeometry solves 44 of 50 IMO geometry problems (2000-2024), exceeding the average gold medalist score (40.9), using only 13K training examples, just 0.004% of the data used by AlphaGeometry 2, demonstrating the potential of LLM agents on expert-level geometry tasks. InternGeometry can also propose novel auxiliary constructions for IMO problems that do not appear in human solutions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过复杂度提升强化学习实现奥林匹克几何大语言模型智能体
大语言模型（LLM）智能体展现出强大的数学解题能力，甚至能在形式化证明系统辅助下解决国际数学奥林匹克（IMO）级别的问题。然而，由于辅助构造的启发式能力较弱，几何解题领域仍由AlphaGeometry 2等依赖大规模数据合成与搜索训练的专家模型主导。本研究首次尝试构建奖牌级几何LLM智能体InternGeometry，通过迭代提出命题与辅助构造、使用符号引擎验证并反思反馈来克服几何启发式局限。动态记忆机制使InternGeometry能在每个问题中与符号引擎进行超过两百次交互。为进一步加速学习，我们提出复杂度提升强化学习（CBRL），在训练阶段逐步增加合成问题的复杂度。基于InternThinker-32B构建的InternGeometry仅使用1.3万训练样本（仅为AlphaGeometry 2数据量的0.004%），便在2000-2024年的50道IMO几何题中解出44道，超越金牌得主平均分（40.9），证明了LLM智能体在专家级几何任务上的潜力。InternGeometry还能为IMO问题提出人类解法中未出现过的新型辅助构造。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing large language model (LLM) agents in geometry, which struggle with heuristic auxiliary constructions and rely on massive synthetic data like AlphaGeometry 2, this work introduces InternGeometry, a medalist-level LLM agent. The method employs an iterative process where the agent proposes propositions and auxiliary constructions, verifies them with a symbolic engine, and uses feedback for reflection, supported by a dynamic memory mechanism enabling hundreds of interactions per problem. To enhance learning efficiency, Complexity-Boosting Reinforcement Learning (CBRL) is introduced, progressively increasing problem complexity during training. Experimental results show that InternGeometry, built on InternThinker-32B and trained with only 13K examples (0.004% of AlphaGeometry 2's data), solves 44 out of 50 IMO geometry problems (2000-2024), surpassing the average gold medalist score of 40.9, and can propose novel auxiliary constructions not found in human solutions.
针对现有大语言模型（LLM）智能体在几何问题中启发式辅助构造能力不足、严重依赖大规模合成数据（如AlphaGeometry 2）的局限，本研究提出了InternGeometry，一个达到国际数学奥林匹克奖牌水平的LLM智能体。其方法采用迭代过程：智能体提出命题和辅助构造，通过符号引擎验证，并利用反馈进行反思，辅以动态记忆机制实现每个问题数百次交互。为提升学习效率，引入了复杂度提升强化学习（CBRL），在训练阶段逐步增加合成问题的复杂度。实验结果表明，基于InternThinker-32B构建、仅用1.3万训练样本（相当于AlphaGeometry 2数据量的0.004%）的InternGeometry，在2000年至2024年的50道IMO几何题中解决了44道，超过了平均金牌得分40.9，并能提出人类解法中未出现的新颖辅助构造。
3D-RFT: Reinforcement Fine-Tuning for Video-based 3D Scene Understanding
Authors: Xiongkun Linghu, Jiangyong Huang, Baoxiong Jia, Siyuan Huang
First: 2026-03-05T09:15:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T09:15:16+00:00
Comments: Project page: https://3d-rft.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards ( RLVR ) has emerged as a transformative paradigm for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models ( LLMs), yet its potential in 3D scene understanding remains under-explored. Existing approaches largely rely on Supervised Fine-Tuning ( SFT), where the token-level cross-entropy loss acts as an indirect proxy for optimization, leading to a misalignment between training objectives and task performances. To bridge this gap, we present Reinforcement Fine-Tuning for Video-based 3D Scene Understanding (3D-RFT ), the first framework to extend RLVR to video-based 3D perception and reasoning. 3D-RFT shifts the paradigm by directly optimizing the model towards evaluation metrics. 3D-RFT first activates 3D-aware Multi-modal Large Language Models ( MLLM s) via SFT, followed by reinforcement fine-tuning using Group Relative Policy Optimization ( GRPO) with strictly verifiable reward functions. We design task-specific reward functions directly from metrics like 3D IoU and F1-Score to provide more effective signals to guide model training. Extensive experiments demonstrate that 3D-RFT-4B achieves state-of-the-art performance on various video-based 3D scene understanding tasks. Notably, 3D-RFT-4B significantly outperforms larger models (e.g., VG LLM-8B) on 3D video detection, 3D visual grounding, and spatial reasoning benchmarks. We further reveal good properties of 3D-RFT such as robust efficacy, and valuable insights into training strategies and data impact. We hope 3D-RFT can serve as a robust and promising paradigm for future development of 3D scene understanding.
中文标题/摘要
标题：3D-RFT：面向视频三维场景理解的强化微调框架
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为增强大语言模型推理能力的变革性范式，但其在三维场景理解领域的潜力尚未充分探索。现有方法主要依赖监督微调（SFT），其词元级交叉熵损失仅作为优化的间接代理，导致训练目标与任务性能间存在偏差。为弥合此差距，我们提出面向视频三维场景理解的强化微调框架（3D-RFT），这是首个将RLVR扩展至视频三维感知与推理的框架。3D-RFT通过直接针对评估指标优化模型实现范式转换：先通过SFT激活三维感知多模态大语言模型（MLLM），再采用具备严格可验证奖励函数的组相对策略优化（GRPO）进行强化微调。我们基于三维交并比和F1分数等指标设计任务专属奖励函数，为模型训练提供更有效的引导信号。大量实验表明，3D-RFT-4B在各类视频三维场景理解任务中达到最先进性能。值得注意的是，在三维视频检测、三维视觉定位和空间推理基准测试中，3D-RFT-4B显著优于更大规模模型（如VG LLM-8B）。我们进一步揭示了3D-RFT的优良特性，包括鲁棒效能，以及对训练策略与数据影响的深刻洞见。期待3D-RFT能为三维场景理解的未来发展提供稳健且前景广阔的范式。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the misalignment between standard supervised fine-tuning objectives and actual task performance in 3D scene understanding, this paper introduces 3D-RFT, a framework that applies reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards to video-based 3D perception. The method first activates a 3D-aware multimodal large language model via supervised fine-tuning and then performs reinforcement fine-tuning using Group Relative Policy Optimization with task-specific reward functions derived directly from metrics like 3D IoU and F1-Score. Experimental results show that the 3D-RFT-4B model achieves state-of-the-art performance on various benchmarks for 3D video detection, visual grounding, and spatial reasoning, significantly outperforming larger models such as VG-LLM-8B, while also demonstrating robust efficacy and providing insights into training strategies.
本文的动机是解决传统监督微调目标与三维场景理解任务实际性能之间的错位问题，提出了3D-RFT框架，将基于可验证奖励的强化学习应用于视频三维感知。该方法首先通过监督微调激活三维感知的多模态大语言模型，然后使用组相对策略优化进行强化微调，其奖励函数直接源自3D IoU和F1-Score等评估指标。主要实验结果表明，3D-RFT-4B模型在三维视频检测、视觉定位和空间推理等多个基准测试中取得了最先进的性能，显著超越了如VG-LLM-8B等更大模型，同时展现了良好的鲁棒性，并为训练策略和数据影响提供了有价值的见解。
Pessimistic Auxiliary Policy for Offline Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Fan Zhang, Baoru Huang, Xin Zhang
First: 2026-02-27T12:34:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T09:03:30+00:00
Comments: Withdrawn due to a crucial mistake
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline reinforcement learning aims to learn an agent from pre-collected datasets, avoiding unsafe and inefficient real-time interaction. However, inevitable access to out-ofdistribution actions during the learning process introduces approximation errors, causing the error accumulation and considerable overestimation. In this paper, we construct a new pessimistic auxiliary policy for sampling reliable actions. Specifically, we develop a pessimistic auxiliary strategy by maximizing the lower confidence bound of the Q-function. The pessimistic auxiliary strategy exhibits a relatively high value and low uncertainty in the vicinity of the learned policy, avoiding the learned policy sampling high-value actions with potentially high errors during the learning process. Less approximation error introduced by sampled action from pessimistic auxiliary strategy leads to the alleviation of error accumulation. Extensive experiments on offline reinforcement learning benchmarks reveal that utilizing the pessimistic auxiliary strategy can effectively improve the efficacy of other offline RL approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：离线强化学习的悲观辅助策略
离线强化学习旨在从预收集的数据集中学习智能体，避免不安全且低效的实时交互。然而，学习过程中不可避免地接触到分布外动作会引入近似误差，导致误差累积和显著高估。本文构建了一种新的悲观辅助策略以采样可靠动作。具体而言，我们通过最大化Q函数的下置信界来构建悲观辅助策略。该策略在学习策略附近表现出较高价值和较低不确定性，避免学习过程采样具有潜在高误差的高价值动作。由悲观辅助策略采样的动作引入的近似误差更小，从而缓解误差累积。在离线强化学习基准上的大量实验表明，利用悲观辅助策略能有效提升其他离线强化学习方法的性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge in offline reinforcement learning where out-of-distribution actions during training lead to approximation errors, error accumulation, and overestimation. To mitigate this, the authors propose a pessimistic auxiliary policy that samples reliable actions by maximizing the lower confidence bound of the Q-function, ensuring high value and low uncertainty near the learned policy to reduce error introduction. Experimental results on offline RL benchmarks demonstrate that this approach effectively enhances the performance of existing offline RL methods.
该论文针对离线强化学习中因训练期间访问分布外动作而导致的近似误差、误差累积和过高估计问题，提出了一种悲观辅助策略。该方法通过最大化Q函数的置信下界来采样可靠动作，确保在学习策略附近具有较高价值和较低不确定性，从而减少误差引入。在离线强化学习基准测试上的实验结果表明，该策略能有效提升现有离线RL方法的性能。
$\nabla$-Reasoner: LLM Reasoning via Test-Time Gradient Descent in Latent Space
Authors: Peihao Wang, Ruisi Cai, Zhen Wang, Hongyuan Mei, Qiang Liu, Pan Li, Zhangyang Wang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-05T08:42:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T08:42:54+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Scaling inference-time compute for Large Language Models (LLMs) has unlocked unprecedented reasoning capabilities. However, existing inference-time scaling methods typically rely on inefficient and suboptimal discrete search algorithms or trial-and-error prompting to improve the online policy. In this paper, we propose $\nabla$-Reasoner, an iterative generation framework that integrates differentiable optimization over token logits into the decoding loop to refine the policy on the fly. Our core component, Differentiable Textual Optimization (DTO), leverages gradient signals from both the LLM's likelihood and a reward model to refine textual representations. $\nabla$-Reasoner further incorporates rejection sampling and acceleration design to robustify and speed up decoding. Theoretically, we show that performing inference-time gradient descent in the sample space to maximize reward is dual to aligning an LLM policy via KL-regularized reinforcement learning. Empirically, $\nabla$-Reasoner achieves over 20% accuracy improvement on a challenging mathematical reasoning benchmark, while reducing number of model calls by approximately 10-40% compared to strong baselines. Overall, our work introduces a paradigm shift from zeroth-order search to first-order optimization at test time, offering a cost-effective path to amplify LLM reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：∇-Reasoner：基于潜在空间测试时梯度下降的大语言模型推理框架
通过扩展大语言模型（LLMs）的推理时计算，已释放出前所未有的推理能力。然而，现有的推理时扩展方法通常依赖低效且次优的离散搜索算法或试错式提示来改进在线策略。本文提出∇-Reasoner——一种迭代生成框架，将词元对数概率的可微分优化集成至解码循环中，实现策略的实时优化。其核心组件“可微分文本优化（DTO）”利用来自LLM似然函数与奖励模型的双重梯度信号优化文本表示。∇-Reasoner进一步结合拒绝采样与加速设计以增强解码鲁棒性并提升速度。理论层面，我们证明在样本空间执行推理时梯度下降以最大化奖励，等价于通过KL正则化强化学习对齐LLM策略。实证层面，∇-Reasoner在具有挑战性的数学推理基准上实现超过20%的准确率提升，同时相较于强基线方法减少约10-40%的模型调用次数。总体而言，本研究实现了从零阶搜索到一阶优化的范式转变，为增强LLM推理能力提供了高效路径。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces $\nabla$-Reasoner, motivated by the need to move beyond inefficient discrete search or trial-and-error prompting for scaling inference-time compute in LLMs. The method proposes an iterative generation framework that performs test-time gradient descent in latent space, using a core component called Differentiable Textual Optimization (DTO) to refine token logits by leveraging gradients from both the LLM's likelihood and an external reward model, augmented with rejection sampling and acceleration techniques. The main experimental results demonstrate that this approach achieves over 20% accuracy improvement on a challenging mathematical reasoning benchmark while reducing the number of required model calls by approximately 10-40% compared to strong baselines, establishing a shift from zeroth-order to first-order optimization during inference.
本文提出了$\nabla$-Reasoner，其动机是超越低效的离散搜索或试错提示方法，以扩展大语言模型在推理时的计算能力。该方法采用一种迭代生成框架，在潜在空间中进行测试时梯度下降，其核心组件“可微分文本优化”利用来自大语言模型似然和外部奖励模型的梯度来优化词元逻辑值，并结合拒绝采样与加速设计以增强解码的鲁棒性和速度。主要实验结果表明，该方法在一个具有挑战性的数学推理基准上实现了超过20%的准确率提升，同时与强基线相比，所需模型调用次数减少了约10-40%，从而实现了从零阶搜索到一阶优化的范式转变。
Balancing Progress and Safety: A Novel Risk-Aware Objective for RL in Autonomous Driving
Authors: Ahmed Abouelazm, Jonas Michel, Helen Gremmelmaier, Tim Joseph, Philip Schörner, J. Marius Zöllner
First: 2025-05-10T19:05:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T08:32:45+00:00
Comments: Accepted in the 36th IEEE Intelligent vehicles Symposium (IV 2025)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) is a promising approach for achieving autonomous driving due to robust decision-making capabilities. RL learns a driving policy through trial and error in traffic scenarios, guided by a reward function that combines the driving objectives. The design of such reward function has received insufficient attention, yielding ill-defined rewards with various pitfalls. Safety, in particular, has long been regarded only as a penalty for collisions. This leaves the risks associated with actions leading up to a collision unaddressed, limiting the applicability of RL in real-world scenarios. To address these shortcomings, our work focuses on enhancing the reward formulation by defining a set of driving objectives and structuring them hierarchically. Furthermore, we discuss the formulation of these objectives in a normalized manner to transparently determine their contribution to the overall reward. Additionally, we introduce a novel risk-aware objective for various driving interactions based on a two-dimensional ellipsoid function and an extension of Responsibility-Sensitive Safety (RSS) concepts. We evaluate the efficacy of our proposed reward in unsignalized intersection scenarios with varying traffic densities. The approach decreases collision rates by 21\% on average compared to baseline rewards and consistently surpasses them in route progress and cumulative reward, demonstrating its capability to promote safer driving behaviors while maintaining high-performance levels.
中文标题/摘要
标题：平衡进展与安全：自动驾驶强化学习的新型风险感知目标
强化学习因其强大的决策能力，是实现自动驾驶的一种有前景的方法。它通过在交通场景中试错来学习驾驶策略，并由结合了驾驶目标的奖励函数引导。此类奖励函数的设计未得到足够重视，导致定义模糊的奖励存在多种缺陷。特别是安全性，长期以来仅被视为碰撞惩罚。这使得导致碰撞的行为所伴随的风险未被解决，限制了强化学习在现实场景中的适用性。为解决这些不足，我们的工作重点是通过定义一组驾驶目标并对其进行分层结构设计来增强奖励公式。此外，我们讨论了以归一化方式表述这些目标，以透明地确定其对总奖励的贡献。另外，我们基于二维椭球函数和责任敏感安全概念的扩展，为各种驾驶交互引入了一种新型风险感知目标。我们在不同交通密度的无信号交叉口场景中评估了所提奖励的有效性。与基线奖励相比，该方法平均降低碰撞率21%，并在路线进展和累积奖励方面持续超越基线，证明了其在保持高性能水平的同时促进更安全驾驶行为的能力。

This paper addresses the limitations of traditional reward functions in reinforcement learning (RL) for autonomous driving, which often treat safety merely as a collision penalty and fail to account for risks preceding collisions, thereby hindering real-world applicability. The authors propose a novel reward formulation that hierarchically structures driving objectives, normalizes them for transparent contribution, and introduces a risk-aware objective based on a two-dimensional ellipsoid function and an extension of Responsibility-Sensitive Safety (RSS) concepts to better capture interactive risks. Experimental evaluation in unsignalized intersection scenarios with varying traffic densities shows that this approach reduces collision rates by an average of 21% compared to baseline rewards while consistently outperforming them in route progress and cumulative reward, demonstrating improved safety without compromising performance.

Automatic Curriculum Learning for Driving Scenarios: Towards Robust and Efficient Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ahmed Abouelazm, Tim Weinstein, Tim Joseph, Philip Schörner, J. Marius Zöllner
First: 2025-05-13T06:26:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T08:22:50+00:00
Comments: Accepted in the 36th IEEE Intelligent Vehicles Symposium (IV 2025)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper addresses the challenges of training end-to-end autonomous driving agents using Reinforcement Learning (RL). RL agents are typically trained in a fixed set of scenarios and nominal behavior of surrounding road users in simulations, limiting their generalization and real-life deployment. While domain randomization offers a potential solution by randomly sampling driving scenarios, it frequently results in inefficient training and sub-optimal policies due to the high variance among training scenarios. To address these limitations, we propose an automatic curriculum learning framework that dynamically generates driving scenarios with adaptive complexity based on the agent's evolving capabilities. Unlike manually designed curricula that introduce expert bias and lack scalability, our framework incorporates a ``teacher'' that automatically generates and mutates driving scenarios based on their learning potential -- an agent-centric metric derived from the agent's current policy -- eliminating the need for expert design. The framework enhances training efficiency by excluding scenarios the agent has mastered or finds too challenging. We evaluate our framework in a reinforcement learning setting where the agent learns a driving policy from camera images. Comparative results against baseline methods, including fixed scenario training and domain randomization, demonstrate that our approach leads to enhanced generalization, achieving higher success rates: +9% in low traffic density, +21% in high traffic density, and faster convergence with fewer training steps. Our findings highlight the potential of ACL in improving the robustness and efficiency of RL-based autonomous driving agents.

Adaptive Rollout Allocation for Online Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards
Authors: Hieu Trung Nguyen, Bao Nguyen, Wenao Ma, Yuzhi Zhao, Ruifeng She, Viet Anh Nguyen
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-02-02T03:50:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T08:17:02+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sampling efficiency is a key bottleneck in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards. Existing group-based policy optimization methods, such as GRPO, allocate a fixed number of rollouts for all training prompts. This uniform allocation implicitly treats all prompts as equally informative, and could lead to inefficient computational budget usage and impede training progress. We introduce VIP, a Variance-Informed Predictive allocation strategy that allocates a given rollout budget to the prompts in the incumbent batch to minimize the expected gradient variance of the policy update. At each iteration, VIP uses a lightweight Gaussian process model to predict per-prompt success probabilities based on recent rollouts. These probability predictions are translated into variance estimates, which are then fed into a convex optimization problem to determine the optimal rollout allocations under a hard compute budget constraint. Empirical results show that VIP consistently improves sampling efficiency and achieves higher performance than uniform or heuristic allocation strategies in multiple benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：可验证奖励在线强化学习的自适应轨迹分配策略
采样效率是可验证奖励强化学习的关键瓶颈。现有基于分组的策略优化方法（如GRPO）为所有训练提示分配固定数量的轨迹。这种均匀分配隐含地将所有提示视为同等信息量，可能导致计算预算使用效率低下并阻碍训练进展。本文提出VIP（方差感知预测分配策略），将给定轨迹预算分配给当前批次中的提示，以最小化策略更新的期望梯度方差。在每次迭代中，VIP使用轻量级高斯过程模型基于近期轨迹预测每个提示的成功概率。这些概率预测被转化为方差估计，随后输入凸优化问题，在严格计算预算约束下确定最优轨迹分配。实验结果表明，VIP在多个基准测试中持续提升采样效率，并比均匀或启发式分配策略获得更高性能。

Motivated by the sampling inefficiency in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, where fixed uniform rollout allocation treats all prompts as equally informative, this paper introduces VIP, a Variance-Informed Predictive allocation strategy. The method employs a lightweight Gaussian process model to predict per-prompt success probabilities from recent rollouts, translates these into variance estimates, and solves a convex optimization problem to optimally allocate a given rollout budget to minimize expected gradient variance in policy updates. Experimental results across multiple benchmarks demonstrate that VIP consistently improves sampling efficiency and achieves higher performance compared to uniform or heuristic allocation strategies.
本文针对可验证奖励强化学习中采样效率低下的问题，提出了一种方差感知预测分配策略VIP。该方法通过轻量级高斯过程模型基于近期轨迹预测每个提示的成功概率，将其转化为方差估计，并求解凸优化问题以在计算预算约束下分配轨迹来最小化策略更新的梯度方差。在多个基准测试中的实验结果表明，VIP相比均匀或启发式分配策略，能持续提升采样效率并获得更高的性能。
BandPO: Bridging Trust Regions and Ratio Clipping via Probability-Aware Bounds for LLM Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yuan Li, Bo Wang, Yufei Gao, Yuqian Yao, Xinyuan Wang, Zhangyue Yin, Xipeng Qiu
First: 2026-03-05T08:03:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T08:03:05+00:00
Comments: Code available at https://github.com/OpenMOSS/BandPO.git
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Proximal constraints are fundamental to the stability of the Large Language Model reinforcement learning. While the canonical clipping mechanism in PPO serves as an efficient surrogate for trust regions, we identify a critical bottleneck: fixed bounds strictly constrain the upward update margin of low-probability actions, disproportionately suppressing high-advantage tail strategies and inducing rapid entropy collapse. To address this, we introduce Band-constrained Policy Optimization (BandPO). BandPO replaces canonical clipping with Band, a unified theoretical operator that projects trust regions defined by f-divergences into dynamic, probability-aware clipping intervals. Theoretical analysis confirms that Band effectively resolves this exploration bottleneck. We formulate this mapping as a convex optimization problem, guaranteeing a globally optimal numerical solution while deriving closed-form solutions for specific divergences. Extensive experiments across diverse models and datasets demonstrate that BandPO consistently outperforms canonical clipping and Clip-Higher, while robustly mitigating entropy collapse.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BandPO：通过概率感知边界桥接信任域与比率裁剪以优化大语言模型强化学习
近端约束对大语言模型强化学习的稳定性至关重要。虽然PPO中的标准裁剪机制可作为信任域的有效替代方案，但我们发现一个关键瓶颈：固定边界严格限制了低概率动作的向上更新空间，不成比例地抑制了高优势的尾部策略，并导致熵值快速崩溃。为解决此问题，我们提出带约束策略优化（BandPO）。BandPO用Band算子替代标准裁剪机制——这是一个统一的理论算子，可将由f散度定义的信任域映射至动态的、概率感知的裁剪区间。理论分析证实Band能有效解决这一探索瓶颈。我们将此映射构建为凸优化问题，在保证获得全局最优数值解的同时，为特定散度推导出闭式解。跨多种模型与数据集的广泛实验表明，BandPO在持续优于标准裁剪与Clip-Higher方法的同时，能稳健缓解熵值崩溃现象。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the limitation of fixed clipping bounds in PPO, which restrict upward updates for low-probability actions, suppress high-advantage strategies, and cause entropy collapse in LLM reinforcement learning. The method introduces BandPO, which replaces standard clipping with a unified operator called Band that projects trust regions defined by f-divergences into dynamic, probability-aware clipping intervals, theoretically resolving the exploration bottleneck; this mapping is formulated as a convex optimization problem with guaranteed optimal solutions. Experimental results across various models and datasets show that BandPO consistently outperforms canonical clipping and Clip-Higher while effectively mitigating entropy collapse.

Distilling Privileged Information for Dubins Traveling Salesman Problems with Neighborhoods
Authors: Min Kyu Shin, Su-Jeong Park, Seung-Keol Ryu, Heeyeon Kim, Han-Lim Choi
First: 2024-04-25T16:33:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T06:44:22+00:00
Comments: Results have severe errors
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper presents a novel learning approach for Dubins Traveling Salesman Problems(DTSP) with Neighborhood (DTSPN) to quickly produce a tour of a non-holonomic vehicle passing through neighborhoods of given task points. The method involves two learning phases: initially, a model-free reinforcement learning approach leverages privileged information to distill knowledge from expert trajectories generated by the LinKernighan heuristic (LKH) algorithm. Subsequently, a supervised learning phase trains an adaptation network to solve problems independently of privileged information. Before the first learning phase, a parameter initialization technique using the demonstration data was also devised to enhance training efficiency. The proposed learning method produces a solution about 50 times faster than LKH and substantially outperforms other imitation learning and RL with demonstration schemes, most of which fail to sense all the task points.
中文标题/摘要
标题：针对带邻域Dubins旅行商问题的特权信息蒸馏方法
本文提出一种新颖的学习方法，用于解决带邻域的Dubins旅行商问题，旨在快速生成非完整车辆通过给定任务点邻域的路径。该方法包含两个学习阶段：首先，采用无模型强化学习，利用特权信息从LinKernighan启发式算法生成的专家轨迹中蒸馏知识；随后，通过监督学习训练一个自适应网络，使其能够独立于特权信息解决问题。在第一学习阶段前，还设计了基于演示数据的参数初始化技术以提升训练效率。所提出的学习方法求解速度比LinKernighan启发式算法快约50倍，显著优于其他模仿学习及结合演示的强化学习方法，且后者大多无法感知所有任务点。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to rapidly generate efficient tours for non-holonomic vehicles in Dubins Traveling Salesman Problems with Neighborhoods (DTSPN). The method employs a two-phase learning approach: first, a model-free reinforcement learning phase distills knowledge from expert trajectories generated by the LinKernighan heuristic, utilizing privileged information; second, a supervised learning phase trains an adaptation network to operate without that privileged data, aided by a parameter initialization technique from demonstrations to boost training efficiency. Experimentally, the proposed method produces solutions approximately 50 times faster than the LKH algorithm and significantly outperforms other imitation learning and RL-with-demonstration baselines, which often fail to cover all task points, though the results are noted to contain severe errors.
本文旨在快速为非完整车辆在带有邻域的Dubins旅行商问题中生成高效路径。该方法采用两阶段学习策略：首先，利用无模型强化学习，通过特权信息从LinKernighan启发式算法生成的专家轨迹中提炼知识；随后，通过监督学习训练一个适应网络，使其能够独立于特权信息解决问题，并辅以基于演示数据的参数初始化技术以提高训练效率。实验结果表明，所提出的学习方法求解速度比LKH算法快约50倍，且显著优于其他模仿学习和演示强化学习方案，这些方案大多无法感知所有任务点，但需注意其结果存在严重错误。
SCoUT: Scalable Communication via Utility-Guided Temporal Grouping in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Manav Vora, Gokul Puthumanaillam, Hiroyasu Tsukamoto, Melkior Ornik
First: 2026-03-05T05:33:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T05:33:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Communication can improve coordination in partially observed multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), but learning \emph{when} and \emph{who} to communicate with requires choosing among many possible sender-recipient pairs, and the effect of any single message on future reward is hard to isolate. We introduce \textbf{SCoUT} (\textbf{S}calable \textbf{Co}mmunication via \textbf{U}tility-guided \textbf{T}emporal grouping), which addresses both these challenges via temporal and agent abstraction within traditional MARL. During training, SCoUT resamples \textit{soft} agent groups every \(K\) environment steps (macro-steps) via Gumbel-Softmax; these groups are latent clusters that induce an affinity used as a differentiable prior over recipients. Using the same assignments, a group-aware critic predicts values for each agent group and maps them to per-agent baselines through the same soft assignments, reducing critic complexity and variance. Each agent is trained with a three-headed policy: environment action, send decision, and recipient selection. To obtain precise communication learning signals, we derive counterfactual communication advantages by analytically removing each sender's contribution from the recipient's aggregated messages. This counterfactual computation enables precise credit assignment for both send and recipient-selection decisions. At execution time, all centralized training components are discarded and only the per-agent policy is run, preserving decentralized execution. Project website, videos and code: \hyperlink{https://scout-comm.github.io/}{https://scout-comm.github.io/}
中文标题/摘要
标题：SCoUT：基于效用引导时序分组的可扩展通信多智能体强化学习方法
通信能提升部分可观测多智能体强化学习（MARL）中的协作效率，但学习通信时机与对象需在大量可能的发送-接收对中进行选择，且单一信息对远期奖励的影响难以分离。本文提出SCoUT（基于效用引导时序分组的可扩展通信），通过在传统MARL框架中引入时序与智能体抽象解决这两大挑战：训练阶段每K步环境步（宏步骤）通过Gumbel-Softmax重采样软智能体分组，这些潜在聚类产生的亲和度构成接收者的可微分先验；基于相同分组，群体感知评价器预测各智能体组价值并通过相同软分配映射至个体基线，降低评价器复杂度与方差。每个智能体采用三头策略：环境动作、发送决策、接收者选择。为获取精确通信学习信号，通过解析移除发送者对接收者聚合信息的贡献推导反事实通信优势，该计算实现发送与接收选择决策的精准信用分配。执行阶段仅保留去中心化的个体策略网络。项目网站、视频与代码：https://scout-comm.github.io/
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces SCoUT, a method to address the challenges of learning when and with whom to communicate in partially observed multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), where the large number of potential sender-recipient pairs and difficulty in isolating message impact hinder effective coordination. The method employs temporal and agent abstraction by resampling soft agent groups periodically using Gumbel-Softmax, which creates latent clusters that guide recipient selection as a differentiable prior, and uses a group-aware critic to reduce complexity and variance. Experimental results demonstrate that SCoUT enables precise credit assignment for communication decisions through counterfactual advantages, leading to improved coordination and performance in decentralized execution settings compared to baseline methods.
本文提出了SCoUT方法，旨在解决部分可观察多智能体强化学习（MARL）中学习何时与谁通信的挑战，其中大量潜在的发送者-接收者对以及难以隔离消息影响阻碍了有效协调。该方法通过使用Gumbel-Softmax定期重采样软智能体分组，引入时间和智能体抽象，形成潜在聚类以作为可微先验指导接收者选择，并采用分组感知评论家降低复杂性和方差。实验结果表明，SCoUT通过反事实优势实现了对通信决策的精确信用分配，在分散执行环境中相比基线方法提高了协调性和性能。
Traceable Evidence Enhanced Visual Grounded Reasoning: Evaluation and Methodology
Authors: Haochen Wang, Xiangtai Li, Zilong Huang, Anran Wang, Jiacong Wang, Tao Zhang, Jiani Zheng, Sule Bai, Zijian Kang, Jiashi Feng, Zhuochen Wang, Zhaoxiang Zhang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-07-10T17:59:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T05:24:46+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026 Camera Ready Version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Models like OpenAI-o3 pioneer visual grounded reasoning by dynamically referencing visual regions, just like human "thinking with images". However, no benchmark exists to evaluate these capabilities holistically. To bridge this gap, we propose TreeBench (Traceable Evidence Evaluation Benchmark), a diagnostic benchmark built on three principles: (1) focused visual perception of subtle targets in complex scenes, (2) traceable evidence via bounding box evaluation, and (3) second-order reasoning to test object interactions and spatial hierarchies beyond simple object localization. Prioritizing images with dense objects, we initially sample 1K high-quality images from SA-1B, and incorporate eight LMM experts to manually annotate questions, candidate options, and answers for each image. After three stages of quality control, TreeBench consists of 405 challenging visual question-answering pairs, even the most advanced models struggle with this benchmark, where none of them reach 60% accuracy, e.g., OpenAI-o3 scores only 54.87. Furthermore, we introduce TreeVGR (Traceable Evidence Enhanced Visual Grounded Reasoning), a training paradigm to supervise localization and reasoning jointly with reinforcement learning, enabling accurate localizations and explainable reasoning pathways. Initialized from Qwen2.5-VL-7B, it improves V* Bench (+16.8), MME-RealWorld (+12.6), and TreeBench (+13.4), proving traceability is key to advancing vision-grounded reasoning. The code is available at https://github.com/Haochen-Wang409/TreeVGR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：可追溯证据增强的视觉基础推理：评估与方法论
以OpenAI-o3为代表的模型通过动态引用视觉区域开创了视觉基础推理，类似人类的“图像化思考”。然而目前缺乏全面评估此类能力的基准。为填补这一空白，我们提出TreeBench（可追溯证据评估基准），该诊断基准基于三项原则构建：（1）对复杂场景中细微目标的聚焦视觉感知；（2）通过边界框评估实现可追溯证据；（3）二阶推理以测试超越简单目标定位的物体交互与空间层级关系。我们优先选取密集物体图像，从SA-1B中初步采样1K张高质量图像，并组织八位LMM专家对每张图像人工标注问题、候选选项及参考答案。经过三轮质量控制，TreeBench最终包含405组具有挑战性的视觉问答对，即使最先进的模型在该基准上也表现不佳——无一达到60%准确率（如OpenAI-o3仅获54.87分）。此外，我们提出TreeVGR（可追溯证据增强的视觉基础推理），这是一种通过强化学习联合监督定位与推理的训练范式，能实现精准定位与可解释的推理路径。该方法基于Qwen2.5-VL-7B初始化，在V*Bench（+16.8）、MME-RealWorld（+12.6）和TreeBench（+13.4）上均取得显著提升，证明可追溯性是推进视觉基础推理的关键。代码已开源：https://github.com/Haochen-Wang409/TreeVGR。

Additionally, the authors propose TreeVGR, a training paradigm using reinforcement learning to jointly supervise localization and reasoning, which, when initialized from Qwen2.5-VL-7B, significantly improves performance on benchmarks like V* Bench, MME-RealWorld, and TreeBench, demonstrating that traceability is crucial for advancing vision-grounded reasoning.
本文针对当前缺乏全面评估视觉基础推理能力的基准问题展开研究，这类能力要求模型像人类一样动态参考视觉区域。为填补这一空白，作者提出了TreeBench诊断基准，其构建基于三个原则：复杂场景中对细微目标的聚焦视觉感知、通过边界框评估实现可追溯证据，以及测试物体交互和空间层次关系的二阶推理。该基准从SA-1B数据集中选取1K张图像，并借助八位专家进行人工标注，经过严格质量控制后包含405个具有挑战性的视觉问答对，即使最先进的模型也难以应对，例如OpenAI-o3的准确率仅为54.87%。此外，作者还提出了TreeVGR训练范式，利用强化学习联合监督定位与推理，基于Qwen2.5-VL-7B初始化后，在V* Bench、MME-RealWorld和TreeBench等基准上性能显著提升，证明了可追溯性是推动视觉基础推理发展的关键。
VISA: Value Injection via Shielded Adaptation for Personalized LLM Alignment
Authors: Jiawei Chen, Tianzhuo Yang, Guoxi Zhang, Jiaming Ji, Yaodong Yang, Juntao Dai
First: 2026-03-05T05:12:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T05:12:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligning Large Language Models (LLMs) with nuanced human values remains a critical challenge, as existing methods like Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) often handle only coarse-grained attributes. In practice, fine-tuning LLMs on task-specific datasets to optimize value alignment inevitably incurs an alignment tax: the model's pre-calibrated value system drifts significantly due to latent bias absorption from training data, while the fine-tuning process also causes severe hallucinations and semantic information loss in generated responses. To address this, we propose VISA (Value Injection via Shielded Adaptation), a closed-loop framework designed to navigate this trade-off. VISA's architecture features a high-precision value detector, a semantic-to-value translator, and a core value-rewriter. The value-rewriter is trained via Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) with a composite reward function that simultaneously optimizes for fine-grained value precision, and the preservation of semantic integrity. By learning an optimal policy to balance these competing objectives, VISA effectively mitigates the alignment tax while staying loyal to the original knowledge. Our experiments demonstrate that this approach enables precise control over a model's value expression while maintaining its factual consistency and general capabilities, significantly outperforming both standard fine-tuning methods and prompting-based baselines, including GPT-4o.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VISA：基于屏蔽式自适应的价值注入实现个性化大语言模型对齐
将大语言模型（LLMs）与细致的人类价值观对齐仍是一个关键挑战，现有方法如基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）通常只能处理粗粒度属性。实践中，针对任务特定数据集微调LLMs以优化价值对齐时，不可避免地会产生对齐代价：模型预校准的价值体系因训练数据中的潜在偏见吸收而发生显著漂移，同时微调过程还会导致生成响应中出现严重幻觉和语义信息丢失。为解决此问题，我们提出VISA（基于屏蔽式自适应的价值注入），这是一个旨在权衡此矛盾的闭环框架。VISA架构包含高精度价值检测器、语义-价值转换器和核心价值重写器。价值重写器通过群体相对策略优化（GRPO）进行训练，采用复合奖励函数同时优化细粒度价值精度和语义完整性保持。通过学习平衡这些竞争目标的最优策略，VISA在保持对原始知识忠诚度的同时，有效缓解了对齐代价。实验表明，该方法能在保持事实一致性和通用能力的前提下，实现对模型价值表达的精准控制，显著优于标准微调方法和基于提示的基线（包括GPT-4o）。

To mitigate this, the authors propose VISA, a closed-loop framework comprising a value detector, semantic-to-value translator, and a value-rewriter trained via Group Relative Policy Optimization with a composite reward function to balance value precision and semantic integrity. Experimental results show that VISA enables precise control over value expression while maintaining factual consistency and general capabilities, outperforming standard fine-tuning and prompting-based baselines including GPT-4o.
本文针对大型语言模型与细微人类价值观对齐的挑战，指出现有方法如RLHF常导致粗粒度对齐并产生'对齐税'，即微调引发价值观漂移、幻觉和语义损失。为此，作者提出VISA框架，它包含价值检测器、语义到价值转换器和价值重写器，通过组相对策略优化和复合奖励函数训练，以平衡价值精度与语义完整性。实验结果表明，VISA能精确控制模型的价值表达，同时保持事实一致性和通用能力，显著优于标准微调方法和基于提示的基线模型，包括GPT-4o。
Interleaved Tool-Call Reasoning for Protein Function Understanding
Authors: Chuanliu Fan, Zicheng Ma, Huanran Meng, Aijia Zhang, Wenjie Du, Jun Zhang, Yi Qin Gao, Ziqiang Cao, Guohong Fu
First: 2026-01-07T05:34:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T04:51:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have highlighted the effectiveness of chain-of-thought reasoning in symbolic domains such as mathematics and programming. However, our study shows that directly transferring such text-based reasoning paradigms to protein function understanding is ineffective: reinforcement learning mainly amplifies superficial keyword patterns while failing to introduce new biological knowledge, resulting in limited generalization. We argue that protein function prediction is a knowledge-intensive scientific task that fundamentally relies on external biological priors and computational tools rather than purely internal reasoning. To address this gap, we propose PFUA, a tool-augmented protein reasoning agent that unifies problem decomposition, tool invocation, and grounded answer generation. Instead of relying on long unconstrained reasoning traces, PFUA integrates domain-specific tools to produce verifiable intermediate evidence. Experiments on four benchmarks demonstrate that PFUA consistently outperforms text-only reasoning models with an average performance improvement of 103%.
中文标题/摘要
标题：交错式工具调用推理用于蛋白质功能理解
近期大语言模型（LLMs）的进展突显了思维链推理在数学和编程等符号领域的有效性。然而，我们的研究表明，直接将此类基于文本的推理范式迁移到蛋白质功能理解中是无效的：强化学习主要放大了表面的关键词模式，而未能引入新的生物学知识，导致泛化能力有限。我们认为蛋白质功能预测是一项知识密集型的科学任务，其根本上依赖于外部生物学先验知识和计算工具，而非纯粹的内部推理。为弥补这一差距，我们提出了PFUA——一种工具增强的蛋白质推理智能体，它统一了问题分解、工具调用和基于证据的答案生成。PFUA不依赖冗长无约束的推理轨迹，而是整合领域专用工具以生成可验证的中间证据。在四个基准测试上的实验表明，PFUA始终优于纯文本推理模型，平均性能提升达103%。

To address this, the authors propose PFUA, a method that integrates domain-specific computational tools into a unified reasoning agent, which decomposes problems, invokes tools for verifiable evidence, and generates grounded answers. Experimental results on four benchmarks show that PFUA consistently outperforms text-only reasoning models, achieving an average performance improvement of 103%.
本研究的动机是观察到直接将基于文本的思维链推理应用于蛋白质功能理解效果不佳，因为这种方法往往强化表面关键词模式而未能引入新的生物学知识，导致泛化能力有限。为此，作者提出了PFUA方法，该方法将领域特定的计算工具整合到一个统一的推理代理中，通过问题分解、工具调用和基于证据的答案生成来应对挑战。在四个基准测试上的实验结果表明，PFUA始终优于纯文本推理模型，平均性能提升了103%。
Diffusion Policy through Conditional Proximal Policy Optimization
Authors: Ben Liu, Shunpeng Yang, Hua Chen
First: 2026-03-05T04:12:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T04:12:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has been extensively employed in a wide range of decision-making problems, such as games and robotics. Recently, diffusion policies have shown strong potential in modeling multi-modal behaviors, enabling more diverse and flexible action generation compared to the conventional Gaussian policy. Despite various attempts to combine RL with diffusion, a key challenge is the difficulty of computing action log-likelihood under the diffusion model. This greatly hinders the direct application of diffusion policies in on-policy reinforcement learning. Most existing methods calculate or approximate the log-likelihood through the entire denoising process in the diffusion model, which can be memory- and computationally inefficient. To overcome this challenge, we propose a novel and efficient method to train a diffusion policy in an on-policy setting that requires only evaluating a simple Gaussian probability. This is achieved by aligning the policy iteration with the diffusion process, which is a distinct paradigm compared to previous work. Moreover, our formulation can naturally handle entropy regularization, which is often difficult to incorporate into diffusion policies. Experiments demonstrate that the proposed method produces multimodal policy behaviors and achieves superior performance on a variety of benchmark tasks in both IsaacLab and MuJoCo Playground.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于条件近端策略优化的扩散策略
强化学习（RL）已广泛应用于游戏和机器人等决策问题。近年来，扩散策略在建模多模态行为方面展现出强大潜力，相比传统高斯策略能生成更多样灵活的动作。尽管已有多种尝试将RL与扩散模型结合，但核心挑战在于难以计算扩散模型下的动作对数似然，这严重阻碍了扩散策略在在线强化学习中的直接应用。现有方法大多通过扩散模型的完整去噪过程计算或近似对数似然，存在内存和计算效率低下的问题。为克服这一挑战，我们提出一种新颖高效的在线扩散策略训练方法，仅需评估简单高斯概率即可实现。该方法通过将策略迭代与扩散过程对齐，形成了与先前工作截然不同的范式。此外，我们的公式能自然处理熵正则化——这一特性在扩散策略中通常难以实现。实验表明，所提方法能产生多模态策略行为，并在IsaacLab和MuJoCo Playground的多种基准任务中取得优越性能。

The paper addresses the challenge of integrating diffusion policies into on-policy reinforcement learning, where computing action log-likelihood under diffusion models is typically inefficient due to the need to evaluate the entire denoising process. To overcome this, the authors propose a novel method that aligns policy iteration with the diffusion process, enabling training with only a simple Gaussian probability evaluation and naturally incorporating entropy regularization. Experimental results on IsaacLab and MuJoCo Playground benchmarks show that the method generates multimodal behaviors and achieves superior performance across various tasks.

Breaking Contextual Inertia: Reinforcement Learning with Single-Turn Anchors for Stable Multi-Turn Interaction
Authors: Xingwu Chen, Zhanqiu Zhang, Yiwen Guo, Difan Zou
First: 2026-03-05T04:04:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T04:04:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While LLMs demonstrate strong reasoning capabilities when provided with full information in a single turn, they exhibit substantial vulnerability in multi-turn interactions. Specifically, when information is revealed incrementally or requires updates, models frequently fail to integrate new constraints, leading to a collapse in performance compared to their single-turn baselines. We term the root cause as \emph{Contextual Inertia}: a phenomenon where models rigidly adhere to previous reasoning traces. Even when users explicitly provide corrections or new data in later turns, the model ignores them, preferring to maintain consistency with its previous (incorrect) reasoning path. To address this, we introduce \textbf{R}einforcement \textbf{L}earning with \textbf{S}ingle-\textbf{T}urn \textbf{A}nchors (\textbf{RLSTA}), a generalizable training approach designed to stabilize multi-turn interaction across diverse scenarios and domains. RLSTA leverages the model's superior single-turn capabilities as stable internal anchors to provide reward signals. By aligning multi-turn responses with these anchors, RLSTA empowers models to break contextual inertia and self-calibrate their reasoning based on the latest information. Experiments show that RLSTA significantly outperforms standard fine-tuning and abstention-based methods. Notably, our method exhibits strong cross-domain generalization (e.g., math to code) and proves effective even without external verifiers, highlighting its potential for general-domain applications.
中文标题/摘要
标题：打破情境惯性：基于单轮锚点的强化学习实现稳定多轮交互
尽管大语言模型在单轮完整信息输入时展现出强大的推理能力，但在多轮交互中却表现出显著脆弱性。具体而言，当信息逐步揭示或需要更新时，模型往往无法整合新约束，导致性能相比单轮基线大幅下降。我们将根本原因定义为\emph{情境惯性}：即模型僵化遵循先前推理轨迹的现象。即使用户在后续轮次明确提供修正或新数据，模型仍会忽略这些信息，倾向于维持与先前（错误）推理路径的一致性。为此，我们提出\textbf{基于单轮锚点的强化学习}方法，这是一种可泛化的训练框架，旨在稳定跨场景与跨领域的多轮交互。该方法利用模型优越的单轮能力作为稳定的内部锚点来提供奖励信号，通过将多轮响应与这些锚点对齐，使模型能够打破情境惯性，根据最新信息进行自校准推理。实验表明，该方法显著优于标准微调与基于弃权的方法，尤其展现出强大的跨领域泛化能力，且无需外部验证器即可生效，凸显了其在通用领域应用的潜力。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the observation that large language models (LLMs) often fail to integrate new information in multi-turn interactions, a problem termed Contextual Inertia, where models rigidly stick to earlier reasoning even when corrected. To address this, the authors propose RLSTA, a reinforcement learning method that uses the model's own reliable single-turn outputs as anchors to provide reward signals, encouraging the model to align multi-turn responses with these anchors and self-calibrate based on the latest input. Experimental results demonstrate that RLSTA significantly outperforms standard fine-tuning and abstention-based methods, showing strong cross-domain generalization and effectiveness without external verifiers.

Parameter Stress Analysis in Reinforcement Learning: Applying Synaptic Filtering to Policy Networks
Authors: Zain ul Abdeen, Ming Jin
First: 2025-06-28T23:28:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T03:38:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper explores reinforcement learning (RL) policy robustness by systematically analyzing network parameters under internal and external stresses. \textcolor{black}{We apply synaptic filtering methods using high-pass, low-pass, and pulse-wave filters from} \citep{pravin2024fragility}, as an internal stress by selectively perturbing parameters, while adversarial attacks apply external stress through modified agent observations. This dual approach enables the classification of parameters as \textit{fragile}, \textit{robust}, or \textit{antifragile}, based on their influence on policy performance in clean and adversarial settings. Parameter scores are defined to quantify these characteristics, and the framework is validated on proximal policy optimization (PPO)-trained agents in Mujoco continuous control environments. The results highlight the presence of antifragile parameters that enhance policy performance under stress, demonstrating the potential of targeted filtering techniques to improve RL policy adaptability. These insights provide a foundation for future advancements in the design of robust and antifragile RL systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习中的参数应力分析：在策略网络中应用突触滤波
本文通过系统分析网络参数在内部与外部应力下的表现，探讨强化学习策略的鲁棒性。我们采用来自\citep{pravin2024fragility}的高通、低通及脉冲波滤波器等突触滤波方法作为内部应力，通过选择性扰动参数施加影响；同时利用对抗性攻击通过修改智能体观测施加外部应力。这种双重方法依据参数在正常与对抗环境下对策略性能的影响，将其分类为脆弱、鲁棒或反脆弱。通过定义参数评分量化这些特性，并在Mujoco连续控制环境中基于近端策略优化训练的智能体上验证了该框架。结果揭示了反脆弱参数在应力下能提升策略性能，表明定向滤波技术有潜力增强强化学习策略的适应性。这些发现为未来设计鲁棒且反脆弱的强化学习系统奠定了基础。
Summary / 总结
This study investigates the robustness of reinforcement learning policies by analyzing how network parameters respond to internal and external stresses. The method applies synaptic filtering techniques, including high-pass, low-pass, and pulse-wave filters, to selectively perturb parameters as an internal stress, while adversarial attacks on observations serve as an external stress. This dual approach classifies parameters as fragile, robust, or antifragile based on their impact on policy performance in both clean and adversarial settings, with scores defined to quantify these traits. Experimental validation using PPO-trained agents in Mujoco environments reveals the existence of antifragile parameters that actually improve performance under stress, indicating that targeted filtering can enhance policy adaptability and robustness.

Distributional Reinforcement Learning with Information Bottleneck for Uncertainty-Aware DRAM Equalization
Authors: Muhammad Usama, Dong Eui Chang
First: 2026-03-05T03:34:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T03:34:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Equalizer parameter optimization is critical for signal integrity in high-speed memory systems operating at multi-gigabit data rates. However, existing methods suffer from computationally expensive eye diagram evaluation, optimization of expected rather than worst-case performance, and absence of uncertainty quantification for deployment decisions. In this paper, we propose a distributional risk-sensitive reinforcement learning framework integrating Information Bottleneck latent representations with Conditional Value-at-Risk optimization. We introduce rate-distortion optimal signal compression achieving 51 times speedup over eye diagrams while quantifying epistemic uncertainty through Monte Carlo dropout. Distributional reinforcement learning with quantile regression enables explicit worst-case optimization, while PAC-Bayesian regularization certifies generalization bounds. Experimental validation on 2.4 million waveforms from eight memory units demonstrated mean improvements of 37.1\% and 41.5\% for 4-tap and 8-tap equalizer configurations with worst-case guarantees of 33.8\% and 38.2\%, representing 80.7\% and 89.1\% improvements over Q-learning baselines. The framework achieved 62.5\% high-reliability classification eliminating manual validation for most configurations. These results suggest the proposed framework provides a practical solution for production-scale equalizer optimization with certified worst-case guarantees.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于信息瓶颈的分布强化学习用于不确定性感知的DRAM均衡优化
均衡器参数优化对多千兆比特数据速率高速存储系统的信号完整性至关重要。然而，现有方法存在计算开销大的眼图评估、优化期望性能而非最坏情况性能，以及缺乏部署决策的不确定性量化等问题。本文提出一种分布风险敏感强化学习框架，将信息瓶颈潜在表示与条件风险价值优化相结合。通过率失真最优信号压缩实现比眼图快51倍的加速，并利用蒙特卡洛丢弃量化认知不确定性。基于分位数回归的分布强化学习实现显式最坏情况优化，而PAC-贝叶斯正则化提供泛化界保证。在八个存储单元的240万个波形上的实验验证表明：4抽头和8抽头均衡器配置的平均性能分别提升37.1%和41.5%，最坏情况保证达到33.8%和38.2%，较Q学习基线提升80.7%和89.1%。该框架实现62.5%的高可靠性分类，免除了多数配置的人工验证。结果表明，所提框架为具备最坏情况保证的生产级均衡器优化提供了实用解决方案。

Experimental results on 2.4 million waveforms showed mean performance improvements of 37.1% and 41.5% for different equalizer configurations, with certified worst-case guarantees and an 80.7% to 89.1% improvement over baselines, alongside a 62.5% high-reliability classification rate that reduces manual validation.

Yukthi Opus: A Multi-Chain Hybrid Metaheuristic for Large-Scale NP-Hard Optimization
Authors: SB Danush Vikraman, Hannah Abigail, Prasanna Kesavraj, Gajanan V Honnavar
First: 2026-01-05T06:51:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T03:33:08+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 9 figures, includes extensive ablation studies and benchmark comparisons
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present Yukthi Opus (YO), a multi-chain hybrid metaheuristic designed for NP-hard optimization under explicit evaluation budget constraints. YO integrates three complementary mechanisms in a structured two-phase architecture: Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) for global exploration, greedy local search for exploitation, and simulated annealing with adaptive reheating to enable controlled escape from local minima. A dedicated burn-in phase allocates evaluations to probabilistic exploration, after which a hybrid optimization loop refines promising candidates. YO further incorporates a spatial blacklist mechanism to avoid repeated evaluation of poor regions and a multi-chain execution strategy to improve robustness and reduce sensitivity to initialization. We evaluate YO on three benchmarks: the Rastrigin function (5D) with ablation studies, the Traveling Salesman Problem with 50 to 200 cities, and the Rosenbrock function (5D) with comparisons against established optimizers including CMA-ES, Bayesian optimization, and accelerated particle swarm optimization. Results show that MCMC exploration and greedy refinement are critical for solution quality, while simulated annealing and multi-chain execution primarily improve stability and variance reduction. Overall, YO achieves competitive performance on large and multimodal problems while maintaining predictable evaluation budgets, making it suitable for expensive black-box optimization settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Yukthi Opus：一种面向大规模NP难优化问题的多链混合元启发式算法
本文提出Yukthi Opus（YO），一种在显式评估预算约束下针对NP难优化问题设计的多链混合元启发式算法。YO采用结构化的两阶段架构集成三种互补机制：马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）实现全局探索，贪婪局部搜索进行开发，以及带自适应重加热的模拟退火以实现可控的局部极小值逃逸。专用预热阶段将评估资源分配给概率探索，随后混合优化循环对潜力候选解进行精细化。YO进一步引入空间黑名单机制以避免重复评估劣质区域，并采用多链执行策略提升鲁棒性、降低对初始化的敏感性。 我们在三个基准测试中评估YO：含消融研究的Rastrigin函数（5维）、50至200城市的旅行商问题，以及与CMA-ES、贝叶斯优化、加速粒子群优化等成熟优化器对比的Rosenbrock函数（5维）。结果表明MCMC探索与贪婪精细化对解质量至关重要，而模拟退火与多链执行主要提升稳定性并降低方差。总体而言，YO在保持可预测评估预算的同时，于大规模多模态问题上取得具有竞争力的性能，适用于高成本黑箱优化场景。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Yukthi Opus (YO), a multi-chain hybrid metaheuristic motivated by the need to solve large-scale NP-hard optimization problems under strict evaluation budget constraints, such as in expensive black-box settings. The method employs a structured two-phase architecture integrating Markov Chain Monte Carlo for global exploration, greedy local search for exploitation, and simulated annealing with adaptive reheating to escape local minima, alongside a spatial blacklist and multi-chain execution for robustness. Experimental results on benchmarks including the Rastrigin function, Traveling Salesman Problem (50-200 cities), and Rosenbrock function demonstrate that YO achieves competitive performance, with MCMC and greedy refinement being key to solution quality, while simulated annealing and multi-chain strategies enhance stability and reduce variance compared to optimizers like CMA-ES and Bayesian optimization.

Position: Beyond Model-Centric Prediction -- Agentic Time Series Forecasting
Authors: Mingyue Cheng, Xiaoyu Tao, Qi Liu, Ze Guo, Enhong Chen
First: 2026-02-02T08:01:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T02:16:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Time series forecasting has traditionally been formulated as a model-centric, static, and single-pass prediction problem that maps historical observations to future values. While this paradigm has driven substantial progress, it proves insufficient in adaptive and multi-turn settings where forecasting requires informative feature extraction, reasoning-driven inference, iterative refinement, and continual adaptation over time. In this paper, we argue for agentic time series forecasting (ATSF), which reframes forecasting as an agentic process composed of perception, planning, action, reflection, and memory. Rather than focusing solely on predictive models, ATSF emphasizes organizing forecasting as an agentic workflow that can interact with tools, incorporate feedback from outcomes, and evolve through experience accumulation. We outline three representative implementation paradigms -- workflow-based design, agentic reinforcement learning, and a hybrid agentic workflow paradigm -- and discuss the opportunities and challenges that arise when shifting from model-centric prediction to agentic forecasting. Together, this position aims to establish agentic forecasting as a foundation for future research at the intersection of time series forecasting.
中文标题/摘要
标题：观点：超越模型中心预测——智能体时间序列预测
时间序列预测传统上被构建为一个模型中心、静态、单次执行的预测问题，即将历史观测值映射为未来值。尽管这一范式推动了显著进展，但在需要信息特征提取、推理驱动推断、迭代优化以及持续时域适应的自适应多轮场景中，其局限性日益凸显。本文提出智能体时间序列预测（ATSF）框架，将预测重构为由感知、规划、行动、反思与记忆构成的智能体过程。ATSF不仅关注预测模型，更强调将预测组织为可与工具交互、整合结果反馈、通过经验积累进化的智能体工作流。我们概述了三种典型实现范式——基于工作流的设计、智能体强化学习及混合智能体工作流范式，并探讨了从模型中心预测转向智能体预测所面临的机遇与挑战。本观点旨在将智能体预测确立为时间序列预测交叉领域未来研究的基石。

The paper argues that traditional model-centric time series forecasting is inadequate for adaptive, multi-turn scenarios requiring iterative reasoning and refinement. It proposes Agentic Time Series Forecasting (ATSF), which frames forecasting as an agentic process involving perception, planning, action, reflection, and memory, enabling interaction with tools, feedback incorporation, and experiential learning. The authors outline three implementation paradigms—workflow-based design, agentic reinforcement learning, and a hybrid approach—and discuss the opportunities and challenges of this shift, aiming to establish ATSF as a foundation for future research.
本文认为传统以模型为中心的时间序列预测方法难以适应需要迭代推理和优化的自适应、多轮场景。为此，它提出了智能体时间序列预测（ATSF），将预测重构为包含感知、规划、行动、反思和记忆的智能体过程，使其能够与工具交互、整合反馈并通过经验积累不断演进。作者概述了三种实现范式——基于工作流的设计、智能体强化学习和混合智能体工作流范式，并讨论了从模型中心预测转向智能体预测的机遇与挑战，旨在为未来研究奠定基础。
VidGuard-R1: AI-Generated Video Detection and Explanation via Reasoning MLLMs and RL
Authors: Kyoungjun Park, Yifan Yang, Juheon Yi, Shicheng Zheng, Yifei Shen, Dongqi Han, Caihua Shan, Muhammad Muaz, Lili Qiu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-02T17:55:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-05T01:56:33+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
The rapid proliferation of AI-generated video necessitates robust detection tools that offer both high accuracy and human-interpretable explanations. While existing MLLM-based detectors rely on supervised fine-tuning (SFT) or direct preference optimization (DPO), these methods are often bottlenecked by static, pre-labeled datasets that fail to capture the evolving, multi-step physical inconsistencies of modern generative models. To bridge this gap, we introduce VidGuard-R1, the first video authenticity detector to utilize group relative policy optimization (GRPO). Moving beyond passive preference matching, VidGuard-R1 employs a reinforcement learning framework that encourages the model to explore and rank multiple reasoning paths. By introducing specialized reward models for temporal stability and diffusion-aware complexity, we incentivize the model to discover 'physics-grounded' artifacts. Our contributions include: (1) a curated dataset of 140,000 challenging real/fake video pairs; (2) a GRPO-based training paradigm that achieves state-of-the-art zero-shot performance; and (3) a reasoning-first architecture that provides precise, verifiable rationales for its forensic judgments. Project website: https://vidguard-r1.github.io/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VidGuard-R1：基于推理型多模态大语言模型与强化学习的AI生成视频检测与解释系统
AI生成视频的快速扩散亟需兼具高准确性与人类可解释性的鲁棒检测工具。现有基于多模态大语言模型的检测器依赖监督微调或直接偏好优化，这些方法受限于静态预标注数据集，难以捕捉现代生成模型动态演进的多步骤物理不一致性。为填补这一空白，我们提出首个采用群体相对策略优化的视频真实性检测器VidGuard-R1。该方法突破被动偏好匹配的局限，通过强化学习框架引导模型探索并排序多重推理路径，并引入针对时序稳定性与扩散感知复杂度的专用奖励模型，激励模型发现‘基于物理规律’的伪影特征。主要贡献包括：（1）包含14万对高难度真实/伪造视频的精选数据集；（2）实现零样本性能最优的GRPO训练范式；（3）提供可验证精准判据的推理优先架构。项目网站：https://vidguard-r1.github.io/。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for robust and explainable detection of AI-generated videos, this paper introduces VidGuard-R1, a novel detector that moves beyond supervised fine-tuning and direct preference optimization by employing group relative policy optimization (GRPO) within a reinforcement learning framework. The method encourages the model to explore and rank multiple reasoning paths, using specialized reward models for temporal stability and diffusion-aware complexity to identify physics-grounded inconsistencies. Experimental results demonstrate state-of-the-art zero-shot performance on a curated dataset of 140,000 challenging video pairs, with the reasoning-first architecture providing precise, verifiable rationales for its forensic judgments.

Optimizing Language Models for Crosslingual Knowledge Consistency
Authors: Tianyu Liu, Jirui Qi, Mrinmaya Sachan, Ryan Cotterell, Raquel Fernández, Arianna Bisazza
First: 2026-03-04T23:36:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T23:36:55+00:00
Comments: Under review. The first two authors contributed equally
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language models are known to often exhibit inconsistent knowledge. This is particularly problematic in multilingual scenarios, where models are likely to be asked similar questions in different languages, and inconsistent responses can undermine their reliability. In this work, we show that this issue can be mitigated using reinforcement learning with a structured reward function, which leads to an optimal policy with consistent crosslingual responses. We introduce Direct Consistency Optimization (DCO), a DPO-inspired method that requires no explicit reward model and is derived directly from the LLM itself. Comprehensive experiments show that DCO significantly improves crosslingual consistency across diverse LLMs and outperforms existing methods when training with samples of multiple languages, while complementing DPO when gold labels are available. Extra experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of DCO in bilingual settings, significant out-of-domain generalizability, and controllable alignment via direction hyperparameters. Taken together, these results establish DCO as a robust and efficient solution for improving knowledge consistency across languages in multilingual LLMs. All code, training scripts, and evaluation benchmarks are released at https://github.com/Betswish/ConsistencyRL.

标题：优化语言模型以实现跨语言知识一致性

This paper addresses the problem of inconsistent knowledge in multilingual large language models, where similar questions in different languages can yield contradictory answers, undermining reliability. The authors propose Direct Consistency Optimization (DCO), a reinforcement learning method inspired by DPO that uses a structured reward function derived directly from the LLM itself, eliminating the need for an explicit reward model. Experimental results demonstrate that DCO significantly enhances crosslingual consistency across various LLMs, outperforms existing methods when trained on multilingual samples, complements DPO when gold labels are available, and shows strong out-of-domain generalization and controllable alignment via hyperparameters.

Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning in Intelligent Transportation Systems: A Comprehensive Survey
Authors: Rexcharles Donatus, Kumater Ter, Daniel Udekwe
First: 2025-08-27T23:04:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T23:12:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The growing complexity of urban mobility and the demand for efficient, sustainable, and adaptive solutions have positioned Intelligent Transportation Systems (ITS) at the forefront of modern infrastructure innovation. At the core of ITS lies the challenge of autonomous decision-making across dynamic, large scale, and uncertain environments where multiple agents traffic signals, autonomous vehicles, or fleet units must coordinate effectively. Multi Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) offers a promising paradigm for addressing these challenges by enabling distributed agents to jointly learn optimal strategies that balance individual objectives with system wide efficiency. This paper presents a comprehensive survey of MARL applications in ITS. We introduce a structured taxonomy that categorizes MARL approaches according to coordination models and learning algorithms, spanning value based, policy based, actor critic, and communication enhanced frameworks. Applications are reviewed across key ITS domains, including traffic signal control, connected and autonomous vehicle coordination, logistics optimization, and mobility on demand systems. Furthermore, we highlight widely used simulation platforms such as SUMO, CARLA, and CityFlow that support MARL experimentation, along with emerging benchmarks. The survey also identifies core challenges, including scalability, non stationarity, credit assignment, communication constraints, and the sim to real transfer gap, which continue to hinder real world deployment.

标题：智能交通系统中的多智能体强化学习：全面综述
城市交通日益复杂，对高效、可持续和自适应解决方案的需求，使智能交通系统（ITS）成为现代基础设施创新的前沿。ITS的核心挑战在于动态、大规模和不确定环境中的自主决策，其中多个智能体（如交通信号、自动驾驶车辆或车队单元）必须有效协调。多智能体强化学习（MARL）通过使分布式智能体共同学习平衡个体目标与系统整体效率的最优策略，为解决这些挑战提供了有前景的范式。本文全面综述了MARL在ITS中的应用。我们提出了一个结构化分类法，根据协调模型和学习算法对MARL方法进行分类，涵盖基于价值、基于策略、演员-评论家以及通信增强框架。综述涵盖了ITS关键领域的应用，包括交通信号控制、网联与自动驾驶车辆协调、物流优化和按需出行系统。此外，我们重点介绍了支持MARL实验的常用仿真平台（如SUMO、CARLA和CityFlow）以及新兴基准测试。本文还指出了核心挑战，包括可扩展性、非平稳性、信用分配、通信约束以及仿真到现实的迁移差距，这些仍是实际部署的主要障碍。

Main experimental results and applications are reviewed across domains like traffic signal control and autonomous vehicle coordination, using simulation platforms like SUMO and CARLA, while highlighting persistent challenges including scalability and the sim-to-real transfer gap.
