CoRPO: Adding a Correctness Bias to GRPO Improves Generalization
Authors: Anisha Garg, Claire Zhang, Nishit Neema, David Bick, Ganesh Venkatesh, Joel Hestness
First: 2025-11-06T15:12:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T23:06:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Group-Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) has emerged as the standard for training reasoning capabilities in large language models through reinforcement learning. By estimating advantages using group-mean rewards rather than a learned critic, GRPO has enabled efficient scaling of reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR). However, we identify a fundamental limitation: GRPO's mean baseline can assign positive advantages to incorrect solutions simply because they outperform a poorly-performing group average. It leads to overestimation of advantages and reinforcement of incorrect behaviours. To address this, we propose Correctness-Relative Policy Optimization (CoRPO), a simple modification to the GRPO objective that clips the minimum baseline to a fixed correctness threshold. We show that baseline clipping introduces a protective bias to advantage estimation that mitigates overfitting while preserving effective exploration. Empirically, CoRPO-trained models improve cross-domain reasoning, generalizing more consistently to out-of-domain (OOD) tasks. When trained on coding tasks, CoRPO outperforms GRPO on math, and vice-versa, indicating that CoRPO learns robust, transferable reasoning patterns rather than task-specific solutions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CoRPO：为GRPO引入正确性偏置以提升泛化能力
组相对策略优化（GRPO）已成为通过强化学习训练大语言模型推理能力的标准方法。该方法通过组平均奖励而非学习型评价器来估计优势值，实现了可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）的高效扩展。然而，我们发现其存在根本性局限：GRPO的均值基线可能仅因错误解优于低性能组平均值而为其分配正优势值，导致优势值高估并强化错误行为。为此，我们提出正确性相对策略优化（CoRPO），通过对GRPO目标函数进行简单修正，将基线最小值限制在固定正确性阈值。研究表明，基线截断机制为优势估计引入了保护性偏置，在保持有效探索的同时缓解过拟合问题。实证表明，经CoRPO训练的模型提升了跨领域推理能力，在域外（OOD）任务中表现出更稳定的泛化性能。在代码任务训练中，CoRPO在数学领域表现优于GRPO，反之亦然，这表明CoRPO学习到的是鲁棒、可迁移的推理模式，而非任务特定解法。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from identifying a fundamental limitation in Group-Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), a standard method for training reasoning in large language models via reinforcement learning, where its mean-reward baseline can assign positive advantages to incorrect solutions if they merely outperform a low group average, leading to overestimated advantages and reinforcement of incorrect behaviors. To address this, the method introduces Correctness-Relative Policy Optimization (CoRPO), a simple modification that clips the minimum baseline to a fixed correctness threshold, thereby adding a protective bias to advantage estimation to mitigate overfitting while preserving exploration. The main experimental results show that CoRPO-trained models improve cross-domain reasoning, generalizing more consistently to out-of-domain tasks; for instance, when trained on coding, CoRPO outperforms GRPO on math tasks, and vice-versa, indicating it learns robust, transferable reasoning patterns rather than task-specific solutions.
本研究的动机源于发现群体相对策略优化（GRPO）——一种通过强化学习训练大语言模型推理能力的标准方法——存在根本性局限：其基于群体平均奖励的基线可能仅仅因为错误解的表现优于较差的群体平均值，就为其分配正优势值，导致优势值高估并强化错误行为。为解决此问题，方法提出了正确性相对策略优化（CoRPO），这是一种简单的修改，通过将最小基线裁剪至固定的正确性阈值，从而为优势估计引入保护性偏置，以减轻过拟合同时保持有效探索。主要实验结果表明，经CoRPO训练的模型提升了跨领域推理能力，在域外任务上表现更一致；例如，在编码任务上训练时，CoRPO在数学任务上优于GRPO，反之亦然，这表明CoRPO学习到的是鲁棒、可迁移的推理模式，而非任务特定的解决方案。
VTool-R1: VLMs Learn to Think with Images via Reinforcement Learning on Multimodal Tool Use
Authors: Mingyuan Wu, Jingcheng Yang, Jize Jiang, Meitang Li, Kaizhuo Yan, Hanchao Yu, Minjia Zhang, Chengxiang Zhai, Klara Nahrstedt
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-05-25T18:23:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T22:28:47+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning Finetuning (RFT) has significantly advanced the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs) by enabling long chains of thought, self-correction, and effective tool use. While recent works attempt to extend RFT to vision-language models (VLMs), these efforts largely produce text-only reasoning conditioned on static image inputs, falling short of true multimodal reasoning in the response. In contrast, test-time methods like Visual Sketchpad incorporate visual steps but lack training mechanisms. We introduce VTool-R1, the first framework that trains VLMs to generate multimodal chains of thought by interleaving text and intermediate visual reasoning steps. VTool-R1 integrates Python-based visual editing tools into the RFT process, enabling VLMs to learn when and how to generate visual reasoning steps that benefit final reasoning. Trained with outcome-based rewards tied to task accuracy, our approach elicits strategic visual tool use for reasoning without relying on process-based supervision. Experiments on structured visual question answering over charts and tables show that VTool-R1 enhances reasoning performance by teaching VLMs to "think with images" and generate multimodal chain of thoughts with tools. To support future research in multi-turn multi-modal reasoning, we open-source our code at https://github.com/VTOOL-R1/vtool-r1
中文标题/摘要
标题：VTool-R1：视觉语言模型通过多模态工具使用的强化学习实现图像化思考
强化学习微调（RFT）通过实现长链思维、自我修正和有效工具使用，显著提升了大型语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力。尽管近期研究尝试将RFT扩展至视觉语言模型（VLMs），但这些工作主要生成基于静态图像输入的纯文本推理，未能实现响应中真正的多模态推理。相比之下，如Visual Sketchpad等测试时方法虽包含视觉步骤，但缺乏训练机制。 我们提出VTool-R1——首个通过交错文本与中间视觉推理步骤来训练VLMs生成多模态思维链的框架。VTool-R1将基于Python的视觉编辑工具集成到RFT过程中，使VLMs能够学习何时及如何生成有益于最终推理的视觉推理步骤。通过基于任务准确度的结果奖励进行训练，我们的方法无需依赖过程监督即可激发策略性视觉工具使用。在图表结构化视觉问答任务上的实验表明，VTool-R1通过教导VLMs“用图像思考”并生成带工具的多模态思维链，有效提升了推理性能。为支持多轮多模态推理的未来研究，我们在https://github.com/VTOOL-R1/vtool-r1开源代码。

When Sensors Fail: Temporal Sequence Models for Robust PPO under Sensor Drift
Authors: Kevin Vogt-Lowell, Theodoros Tsiligkaridis, Rodney Lafuente-Mercado, Surabhi Ghatti, Shanghua Gao, Marinka Zitnik, Daniela Rus
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-04T22:21:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T22:21:54+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026 CAO Workshop
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Real-world reinforcement learning systems must operate under distributional drift in their observation streams, yet most policy architectures implicitly assume fully observed and noise-free states. We study robustness of Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) under temporally persistent sensor failures that induce partial observability and representation shift. To respond to this drift, we augment PPO with temporal sequence models, including Transformers and State Space Models (SSMs), to enable policies to infer missing information from history and maintain performance. Under a stochastic sensor failure process, we prove a high-probability bound on infinite-horizon reward degradation that quantifies how robustness depends on policy smoothness and failure persistence. Empirically, on MuJoCo continuous-control benchmarks with severe sensor dropout, we show Transformer-based sequence policies substantially outperform MLP, RNN, and SSM baselines in robustness, maintaining high returns even when large fractions of sensors are unavailable. These results demonstrate that temporal sequence reasoning provides a principled and practical mechanism for reliable operation under observation drift caused by sensor unreliability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：传感器失效时的应对策略：基于时序序列模型的鲁棒PPO算法应对传感器漂移
现实世界的强化学习系统必须在观测流存在分布漂移的条件下运行，然而大多数策略架构隐式假设状态完全可观测且无噪声。本研究针对导致部分可观测性和表征偏移的持续性传感器故障，探究近端策略优化（PPO）的鲁棒性。为应对此类漂移，我们通过集成Transformer和状态空间模型（SSM）等时序序列模型来增强PPO，使策略能够从历史信息推断缺失数据并保持性能。在随机传感器故障过程中，我们证明了无限时域奖励衰减的高概率边界，该边界量化了鲁棒性对策略平滑度与故障持续性的依赖关系。在MuJoCo连续控制基准测试中，面对严重的传感器丢失情况，基于Transformer的序列策略在鲁棒性上显著优于MLP、RNN和SSM基线模型，即使大部分传感器不可用时仍能保持高回报。这些结果表明，时序序列推理为传感器不可靠性导致的观测漂移提供了原理清晰且实用的可靠运行机制。

Motivated by the need for reinforcement learning systems to handle real-world sensor drift and failures, which induce partial observability and distributional shift, this paper proposes augmenting Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) with temporal sequence models like Transformers and State Space Models to infer missing information from historical observations. The method involves integrating these models into policy architectures to enhance robustness under persistent sensor dropout. Experimental results on MuJoCo continuous-control benchmarks demonstrate that Transformer-based sequence policies significantly outperform MLP, RNN, and SSM baselines, maintaining high returns even with severe sensor unavailability, while theoretical analysis provides a high-probability bound on reward degradation linked to policy smoothness and failure persistence.
本文针对强化学习系统在现实世界中需应对传感器漂移和故障导致的局部可观测性与分布偏移问题，提出将时序序列模型（如Transformer和状态空间模型）与近端策略优化（PPO）结合，以从历史观测中推断缺失信息。该方法通过将这些模型集成到策略架构中，提升在持续传感器失效情况下的鲁棒性。在MuJoCo连续控制基准测试中，实验结果表明基于Transformer的序列策略显著优于MLP、RNN和SSM基线，即使在传感器严重不可用时仍能保持高性能，同时理论分析给出了与策略平滑性和故障持续性相关的奖励衰减的高概率界限。
GRAND: Guidance, Rebalancing, and Assignment for Networked Dispatch in Multi-Agent Path Finding
Authors: Johannes Gaber, Meshal Alharbi, Daniele Gammelli, Gioele Zardini
First: 2025-12-02T19:44:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T22:19:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large robot fleets are now common in warehouses and other logistics settings, where small control gains translate into large operational impacts. In this article, we address task scheduling for lifelong Multi-Agent Pickup-and-Delivery (MAPD) and propose a hybrid method that couples learning-based global guidance with lightweight optimization. A graph neural network policy trained via reinforcement learning outputs a desired distribution of free agents over an aggregated warehouse graph. This signal is converted into region-to-region rebalancing through a minimum-cost flow, and finalized by small, local assignment problems, preserving accuracy while keeping per-step latency within a 1 s compute budget. We call this approach GRAND: a hierarchical algorithm that relies on Guidance, Rebalancing, and Assignment to explicitly leverage the workspace Network structure and Dispatch agents to tasks. On congested warehouse benchmarks from the League of Robot Runners (LoRR) with up to 500 agents, our approach improves throughput by up to 10% over the 2024 winning scheduler while maintaining real-time execution. The results indicate that coupling graph-structured learned guidance with tractable solvers reduces congestion and yields a practical, scalable blueprint for high-throughput scheduling in large fleets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GRAND：多智能体路径规划中网络化调度的引导、再平衡与分配
大型机器人车队在仓库等物流场景中日益普及，微小的控制优化即可带来显著的运营效益。本文针对终身多智能体取送任务（MAPD）的调度问题，提出一种融合学习型全局引导与轻量优化的混合方法。通过强化学习训练的图神经网络策略，在聚合仓库图上输出空闲智能体的期望分布；该信号经最小成本流转换为区域间再平衡，最终通过局部小规模分配问题完成调度，在保持精度的同时将单步计算延迟控制在1秒内。该方法被命名为GRAND：一种依赖引导、再平衡与分配的层次化算法，显式利用工作空间网络结构并将任务分派至智能体。在包含多达500个智能体的“机器人跑者联盟”（LoRR）拥堵仓库基准测试中，本方法在保持实时执行的同时，较2024年优胜调度器提升吞吐量最高达10%。结果表明，结合图结构学习引导与可求解优化器能有效缓解拥堵，为大规模车队的高吞吐调度提供了实用且可扩展的解决方案。
Summary / 总结
The motivation is to enhance task scheduling for large robot fleets in warehouses, where small efficiency gains have major operational impacts. The method, called GRAND, is a hybrid approach that combines a graph neural network policy trained via reinforcement learning for global guidance with lightweight optimization; it first outputs a desired distribution of free agents over an aggregated graph, then uses minimum-cost flow for region-to-region rebalancing, and finally solves small local assignment problems to preserve accuracy while keeping per-step latency under 1 second. Main experimental results on congested warehouse benchmarks from the League of Robot Runners with up to 500 agents show that GRAND improves throughput by up to 10% over the 2024 winning scheduler while maintaining real-time execution, indicating that coupling learned guidance with tractable solvers reduces congestion and offers a scalable blueprint for high-throughput scheduling.
该研究的动机是优化仓库等物流场景中大型机器人车队的任务调度，因为微小的控制提升能带来显著的运营效益。方法上提出了名为GRAND的混合算法，它结合了基于强化学习训练的图神经网络策略进行全局引导与轻量级优化；首先在聚合的仓库图上输出空闲机器人的期望分布，然后通过最小成本流实现区域间再平衡，最后解决小型局部分配问题，在保持精度的同时将每步计算延迟控制在1秒内。主要实验结果在多达500个智能体的拥堵仓库基准测试（来自League of Robot Runners）中显示，GRAND相比2024年获胜调度器将吞吐量提升了高达10%，同时保持实时执行，这表明将图结构学习引导与可处理求解器结合能减少拥堵，为大规模车队的高吞吐调度提供了实用且可扩展的方案。
SPEED-RL: Faster Training of Reasoning Models via Online Curriculum Learning
Authors: Ruiqi Zhang, Daman Arora, Song Mei, Andrea Zanette
First: 2025-06-10T17:42:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T21:31:21+00:00
Comments: There are some bugs in the experiments, and we cannot fix them to make it satisfactory to us
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Training large language models with reinforcement learning (RL) against verifiable rewards significantly enhances their reasoning abilities, yet remains computationally expensive due to inefficient uniform prompt sampling. We introduce Selective Prompting with Efficient Estimation of Difficulty (SPEED), an adaptive online RL curriculum that selectively chooses training examples of intermediate difficulty to maximize learning efficiency. Theoretically, we establish that intermediate-difficulty prompts improve the gradient estimator's signal-to-noise ratio, accelerating convergence. Empirically, our efficient implementation leads to 2x to 6x faster training without degrading accuracy, requires no manual tuning, and integrates seamlessly into standard RL algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPEED-RL：基于在线课程学习的推理模型快速训练方法
通过强化学习（RL）结合可验证奖励训练大语言模型能显著提升其推理能力，但均匀提示采样的低效性导致计算成本高昂。本文提出基于难度高效估计的选择性提示方法（SPEED），这是一种自适应在线RL课程策略，通过选择性选取中等难度训练样本来最大化学习效率。理论上，我们证明中等难度提示能提升梯度估计器的信噪比，从而加速收敛。实证表明，本方法的高效实现可在不降低准确性的前提下将训练速度提升2至6倍，无需人工调参，并能无缝集成至标准RL算法中。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high computational cost of training large language models with reinforcement learning due to inefficient uniform prompt sampling, this paper introduces SPEED, an adaptive online curriculum learning method that selectively chooses training examples of intermediate difficulty to maximize learning efficiency. The method is theoretically grounded in improving the gradient estimator's signal-to-noise ratio for faster convergence. Experimentally, it achieves 2x to 6x faster training without accuracy degradation, requires no manual tuning, and integrates seamlessly into standard RL algorithms, though the authors note unresolved bugs in the experiments.
本文的动机在于，由于低效的均匀提示采样，使用强化学习训练大型语言模型的计算成本高昂，因此提出了SPEED，一种自适应在线课程学习方法，选择中等难度的训练样本来最大化学习效率。该方法在理论上基于提高梯度估计器的信噪比以实现更快收敛。实验结果表明，它实现了2到6倍的训练加速且不降低准确性，无需手动调参，并能无缝集成到标准强化学习算法中，但作者指出实验中存在未解决的缺陷。
Bootstrapping Exploration with Group-Level Natural Language Feedback in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Lei Huang, Xiang Cheng, Chenxiao Zhao, Guobin Shen, Junjie Yang, Xiaocheng Feng, Yuxuan Gu, Xing Yu, Bing Qin
First: 2026-03-04T20:53:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T20:53:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) typically receive diverse natural language (NL) feedback through interaction with the environment. However, current reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms rely solely on scalar rewards, leaving the rich information in NL feedback underutilized and leading to inefficient exploration. In this work, we propose GOLF, an RL framework that explicitly exploits group-level language feedback to guide targeted exploration through actionable refinements. GOLF aggregates two complementary feedback sources: (i) external critiques that pinpoint errors or propose targeted fixes, and (ii) intra-group attempts that supply alternative partial ideas and diverse failure patterns. These group-level feedbacks are aggregated to produce high-quality refinements, which are adaptively injected into training as off-policy scaffolds to provide targeted guidance in sparse-reward regions. Meanwhile, GOLF jointly optimizes generation and refinement within a unified RL loop, creating a virtuous cycle that continuously improves both capabilities. Experiments on both verifiable and non-verifiable benchmarks show that GOLF achieves superior performance and exploration efficiency, achieving 2.2$\times$ improvements in sample efficiency compared to RL methods trained solely on scalar rewards. Code is available at https://github.com/LuckyyySTA/GOLF.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习中基于群体自然语言反馈的探索引导方法
大型语言模型（LLMs）通常通过与环境的交互获得多样化的自然语言（NL）反馈。然而，当前强化学习（RL）算法仅依赖标量奖励，导致NL反馈中的丰富信息未被充分利用，探索效率低下。本研究提出GOLF框架，通过可操作的改进策略显式利用群体层面的语言反馈来引导定向探索。GOLF聚合两种互补反馈源：（1）指出错误或提出针对性修正的外部批评；（2）提供替代性局部想法与多样化失败模式的组内尝试。这些群体反馈经聚合生成高质量改进方案，作为离策略脚手架自适应注入训练过程，为稀疏奖励区域提供定向指导。同时，GOLF在统一RL循环中联合优化生成与改进能力，形成持续提升双重能力的良性循环。在可验证与不可验证基准上的实验表明，GOLF实现了卓越的性能与探索效率，相比仅依赖标量奖励的RL方法，样本效率提升2.2倍。代码发布于https://github.com/LuckyyySTA/GOLF。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the underutilization of rich natural language feedback in reinforcement learning, which typically relies only on scalar rewards, this paper introduces GOLF, a framework that leverages group-level language feedback to enhance exploration. The method aggregates external critiques and intra-group attempts to produce actionable refinements, which are injected as off-policy scaffolds to guide training in sparse-reward scenarios, while jointly optimizing generation and refinement in a unified loop. Experimental results on verifiable and non-verifiable benchmarks demonstrate that GOLF achieves superior performance and exploration efficiency, with a 2.2× improvement in sample efficiency over RL methods using only scalar rewards.
针对强化学习中仅依赖标量奖励而未能充分利用自然语言反馈丰富信息的问题，本文提出了GOLF框架，利用群体层面的语言反馈来增强探索。该方法通过聚合外部批评和组内尝试生成可操作的改进建议，并将其作为离策略支架注入训练，以在稀疏奖励区域提供针对性指导，同时在统一循环中联合优化生成和细化过程。在可验证和不可验证基准上的实验结果表明，GOLF实现了更优的性能和探索效率，样本效率相比仅使用标量奖励的强化学习方法提升了2.2倍。
Composition-Grounded Data Synthesis for Visual Reasoning
Authors: Xinyi Gu, Jiayuan Mao, Zhang-Wei Hong, Zhuoran Yu, Pengyuan Li, Dhiraj Joshi, Rogerio Feris, Zexue He
First: 2025-10-16T18:00:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T18:45:57+00:00
Comments: ICLR2026 camera-ready version. Project page: https://cogsynthesis.github.io
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Pretrained multi-modal large language models (MLLMs) demonstrate strong performance on diverse multimodal tasks, but remain limited in reasoning capabilities for domains where annotations are difficult to collect. In this work, we focus on artificial image domains such as charts, rendered documents, and webpages, which are abundant in practice yet lack large-scale human annotated reasoning datasets. We introduce COGS (COmposition-Grounded data Synthesis), a data-efficient framework for equipping MLLMs with advanced reasoning abilities from a small set of seed questions. The key idea is to decompose each seed question into primitive perception and reasoning factors, which can then be systematically recomposed with new images to generate large collections of synthetic question-answer pairs. Each generated question is paired with subquestions and intermediate answers, enabling reinforcement learning with factor-level process rewards. Experiments on chart reasoning show that COGS substantially improves performance on unseen questions, with the largest gains on reasoning-heavy and compositional questions. Moreover, training with a factor-level mixture of different seed data yields better transfer across multiple datasets, suggesting that COGS induces generalizable capabilities rather than dataset-specific overfitting. We further demonstrate that the framework extends beyond charts to other domains such as webpages.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向视觉推理的构图式数据合成方法
预训练多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在多样化多模态任务中展现出强大性能，但在标注数据难以获取的领域，其推理能力仍存在局限。本研究聚焦图表、渲染文档和网页等人工图像领域——这些领域在实践中数据丰富，却缺乏大规模人工标注的推理数据集。我们提出COGS（构图式数据合成框架），这是一个数据高效框架，旨在通过少量种子问题赋予MLLMs高级推理能力。其核心思想是将每个种子问题解构为基本感知因子与推理因子，进而系统性地与新图像重组，生成大规模合成问答对。每个生成的问题均附带子问题与中间答案，支持通过因子级过程奖励进行强化学习。图表推理实验表明，COGS显著提升了对未见问题的处理性能，在强推理与组合式问题上提升尤为显著。此外，采用不同种子数据的因子级混合训练能实现更好的跨数据集迁移效果，表明COGS诱导的是泛化能力而非数据集特异性过拟合。我们进一步验证了该框架可扩展至网页等其他领域。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to enhance the reasoning capabilities of pretrained multi-modal large language models (MLLMs) in artificial image domains like charts and webpages, where large-scale human-annotated reasoning datasets are scarce. The method introduces COGS, a data-efficient framework that decomposes a small set of seed questions into primitive perception and reasoning factors, then systematically recomposes these factors with new images to generate synthetic question-answer pairs, each accompanied by subquestions and intermediate answers for reinforcement learning with factor-level process rewards. Experimental results on chart reasoning demonstrate that COGS significantly boosts performance on unseen questions, particularly for reasoning-heavy and compositional ones, and training with a factor-level mixture of seed data improves cross-dataset transfer, indicating generalizable capabilities; the framework also extends effectively to other domains such as webpages.
本研究旨在提升预训练多模态大语言模型在图表和网页等人工图像领域的推理能力，这些领域缺乏大规模人工标注的推理数据集。方法上提出了COGS框架，通过将少量种子问题分解为基本感知和推理因子，并系统性地将这些因子与新图像重组，生成合成问答对，每个问题都配有子问题和中间答案，以支持基于因子级过程奖励的强化学习。实验结果表明，在图表推理任务中，COGS显著提高了对未见问题的性能，尤其在推理密集和组合型问题上效果突出，且通过因子级混合种子数据训练能增强跨数据集的泛化能力，表明其诱导了可推广的推理技能；该框架还成功扩展至网页等其他领域。
Dual-Modality Multi-Stage Adversarial Safety Training: Robustifying Multimodal Web Agents Against Cross-Modal Attacks
Authors: Haoyu Liu, Dingcheng Li, Lukas Rutishauser, Zeyu Zheng
First: 2026-03-04T18:29:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T18:29:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal web agents that process both screenshots and accessibility trees are increasingly deployed to interact with web interfaces, yet their dual-stream architecture opens an underexplored attack surface: an adversary who injects content into the webpage DOM simultaneously corrupts both observation channels with a consistent deceptive narrative. Our vulnerability analysis on MiniWob++ reveals that attacks including a visual component far outperform text-only injections, exposing critical gaps in text-centric VLM safety training. Motivated by this finding, we propose Dual-Modality Multi-Stage Adversarial Safety Training (DMAST), a framework that formalizes the agent-attacker interaction as a two-player zero-sum Markov game and co-trains both players through a three-stage pipeline: (1) imitation learning from a strong teacher model, (2) oracle-guided supervised fine-tuning that uses a novel zero-acknowledgment strategy to instill task-focused reasoning under adversarial noise, and (3) adversarial reinforcement learning via Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) self-play. On out-of-distribution tasks, DMAST substantially mitigates adversarial risks while simultaneously doubling task completion efficiency. Our approach significantly outperforms established training-based and prompt-based defenses, demonstrating genuine co-evolutionary progress and robust generalization to complex, unseen environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：双模态多阶段对抗安全训练：增强多模态网络代理抵御跨模态攻击的鲁棒性
处理屏幕截图和可访问性树的多模态网络代理正日益广泛地应用于网页界面交互，但其双流架构暴露了一个尚未充分探索的攻击面：攻击者通过向网页DOM注入内容，可同时污染两个观测通道，形成一致的欺骗性叙述。我们在MiniWob++上的漏洞分析表明，包含视觉组件的攻击效果远超纯文本注入，揭示了以文本为中心的视觉语言模型安全训练存在关键缺陷。基于此发现，我们提出双模态多阶段对抗安全训练框架，将代理与攻击者的交互形式化为双人零和马尔可夫博弈，并通过三阶段流程协同训练双方：（1）基于强教师模型的模仿学习；（2）采用新型零确认策略的预言机引导监督微调，使模型在对抗噪声中保持任务聚焦推理；（3）通过群组相对策略优化的对抗性强化学习自博弈。在分布外任务中，该框架显著降低对抗风险的同时将任务完成效率提升一倍。本方法明显优于现有基于训练和提示的防御方案，展现出真正的协同进化能力及对复杂未知环境的强泛化性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the vulnerability of multimodal web agents, which process both screenshots and accessibility trees, to cross-modal adversarial attacks where injected content corrupts both observation channels simultaneously. Motivated by the finding that attacks with a visual component are far more effective than text-only injections, the authors propose Dual-Modality Multi-Stage Adversarial Safety Training (DMAST), a framework that formalizes the agent-attacker interaction as a two-player zero-sum Markov game and co-trains both players through a three-stage pipeline involving imitation learning, oracle-guided supervised fine-tuning with a zero-acknowledgment strategy, and adversarial reinforcement learning via Group Relative Policy Optimization self-play. Experimental results on out-of-distribution tasks show that DMAST substantially mitigates adversarial risks while simultaneously doubling task completion efficiency, significantly outperforming established training-based and prompt-based defenses and demonstrating robust generalization to complex, unseen environments.
本文针对处理截图和可访问性树的多模态网络代理易受跨模态对抗攻击的漏洞展开研究，这种攻击通过注入内容同时破坏两个观察通道。受视觉攻击远比纯文本注入更有效的发现启发，作者提出了双模态多阶段对抗安全训练框架，将代理与攻击者的交互形式化为两人零和马尔可夫博弈，并通过三阶段流程协同训练双方：模仿学习、采用零确认策略的预言机引导监督微调，以及基于群体相对策略优化的对抗强化学习自博弈。在分布外任务上的实验结果表明，该框架显著降低了对抗风险，同时将任务完成效率提升了一倍，明显优于现有的基于训练和提示的防御方法，并展现出对复杂未知环境的强大泛化能力。
A Constrained RL Approach for Cost-Efficient Delivery of Latency-Sensitive Applications
Authors: Ozan Aygün, Vincenzo Norman Vitale, Antonia M. Tulino, Hao Feng, Elza Erkip, Jaime Llorca
First: 2026-03-04T18:19:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T18:19:35+00:00
Comments: 7 pages, 4 figures, accepted for publication in 2025 59th Asilomar Conference on Signals, Systems, and Computers
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Next-generation networks aim to provide performance guarantees to real-time interactive services that require timely and cost-efficient packet delivery. In this context, the goal is to reliably deliver packets with strict deadlines imposed by the application while minimizing overall resource allocation cost. A large body of work has leveraged stochastic optimization techniques to design efficient dynamic routing and scheduling solutions under average delay constraints; however, these methods fall short when faced with strict per-packet delay requirements. We formulate the minimum-cost delay-constrained network control problem as a constrained Markov decision process and utilize constrained deep reinforcement learning (CDRL) techniques to effectively minimize total resource allocation cost while maintaining timely throughput above a target reliability level. Results indicate that the proposed CDRL-based solution can ensure timely packet delivery even when existing baselines fall short, and it achieves lower cost compared to other throughput-maximizing methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种面向低延迟应用成本高效传输的约束强化学习方法
下一代网络旨在为需要及时且经济高效数据包传输的实时交互服务提供性能保障。在此背景下，目标是在满足应用层严格截止时限的前提下可靠传输数据包，同时最小化总体资源分配成本。现有研究多采用随机优化技术设计平均延迟约束下的动态路由与调度方案，但这些方法难以满足严格的逐包延迟要求。本文将最小成本延迟约束网络控制问题建模为约束马尔可夫决策过程，运用约束深度强化学习技术，在保持及时吞吐量高于目标可靠水平的同时有效降低总资源分配成本。实验表明，所提出的基于约束深度强化学习的解决方案能在现有基线方法失效时仍确保数据包及时传输，且相比其他吞吐量最大化方法具有更低的成本。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to guarantee strict per-packet deadlines for latency-sensitive applications in next-generation networks while minimizing resource costs, this paper formulates the problem as a constrained Markov decision process and employs constrained deep reinforcement learning (CDRL) to dynamically control routing and scheduling. The method aims to minimize total allocation cost while maintaining timely throughput above a target reliability threshold. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed CDRL solution reliably ensures timely packet delivery where existing baselines fail and achieves lower cost compared to throughput-maximizing alternatives.
本文针对下一代网络中延迟敏感型应用需在严格每包时限内保证传输并最小化资源成本的需求，将问题建模为约束马尔可夫决策过程，采用约束深度强化学习方法动态控制路由与调度。该方法在维持及时吞吐量高于目标可靠性的同时，最小化总资源分配成本。实验结果表明，所提出的约束深度强化学习方案能在现有基线方法失效时仍确保数据包及时送达，且相比专注于最大化吞吐量的方法实现了更低的成本。
LadderSym: A Multimodal Interleaved Transformer for Music Practice Error Detection
Authors: Benjamin Shiue-Hal Chou, Purvish Jajal, Nick John Eliopoulos, James C. Davis, George K. Thiruvathukal, Kristen Yeon-Ji Yun, Yung-Hsiang Lu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-16T02:15:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T18:04:43+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Music learners can greatly benefit from tools that accurately detect errors in their practice. Existing approaches typically compare audio recordings to music scores using heuristics or learnable models. This paper introduces LadderSym, a novel Transformer-based method for music error detection. LadderSym is guided by two key observations about the state-of-the-art approaches: (1) late fusion limits inter-stream alignment and cross-modality comparison capability; and (2) reliance on score audio introduces ambiguity in the frequency spectrum, degrading performance in music with concurrent notes. To address these limitations, LadderSym introduces (1) a two-stream encoder with inter-stream alignment modules to improve audio comparison capabilities and error detection F1 scores, and (2) a multimodal strategy that leverages both audio and symbolic scores by incorporating symbolic representations as decoder prompts, reducing ambiguity and improving F1 scores. We evaluate our method on the MAESTRO-E and CocoChorales-E datasets by measuring the F1 score for each note category. Compared to the previous state of the art, LadderSym more than doubles F1 for missed notes on MAESTRO-E (26.8% -> 56.3%) and improves extra note detection by 14.4 points (72.0% -> 86.4%). Similar gains are observed on CocoChorales-E. Furthermore, we also evaluate our models on real data we curated. This work introduces insights about comparison models that could inform sequence evaluation tasks for reinforcement learning, human skill assessment, and model evaluation. Code: https://github.com/ben2002chou/LadderSYM

标题：LadderSym：用于音乐练习错误检测的多模态交错Transformer

Motivated by the need for accurate tools to assist music learners in practice, this paper introduces LadderSym, a Transformer-based method for detecting errors like missed or extra notes. What Does Flow Matching Bring To TD Learning?
Authors: Bhavya Agrawalla, Michal Nauman, Aviral Kumar
First: 2026-03-04T17:51:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T17:51:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent work shows that flow matching can be effective for scalar Q-value function estimation in reinforcement learning (RL), but it remains unclear why or how this approach differs from standard critics. Contrary to conventional belief, we show that their success is not explained by distributional RL, as explicitly modeling return distributions can reduce performance. Instead, we argue that the use of integration for reading out values and dense velocity supervision at each step of this integration process for training improves TD learning via two mechanisms. First, it enables robust value prediction through \emph{test-time recovery}, whereby iterative computation through integration dampens errors in early value estimates as more integration steps are performed. This recovery mechanism is absent in monolithic critics. Second, supervising the velocity field at multiple interpolant values induces more \emph{plastic} feature learning within the network, allowing critics to represent non-stationary TD targets without discarding previously learned features or overfitting to individual TD targets encountered during training. We formalize these effects and validate them empirically, showing that flow-matching critics substantially outperform monolithic critics (2$\times$ in final performance and around 5$\times$ in sample efficiency) in settings where loss of plasticity poses a challenge e.g., in high-UTD online RL problems, while remaining stable during learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：流匹配为时序差分学习带来什么？
近期研究表明，流匹配在强化学习的标量Q值函数估计中具有显著效果，但其与标准评论家方法的差异机制尚不明确。与传统观点相反，我们发现其成功并非源于分布强化学习——显式建模回报分布反而可能降低性能。我们提出，该方法通过积分过程读取值函数，并在积分每一步施加密集速度监督，通过两种机制改进时序差分学习：首先，通过\emph{测试时恢复}实现稳健值预测——积分迭代计算能随着步数增加抑制早期估计误差，而传统单一评论家缺乏此机制；其次，在多个插值点监督速度场能诱导网络进行更\emph{可塑性}的特征学习，使评论家既能表征非平稳时序差分目标，又不会丢弃已学特征或对训练中单个目标过拟合。我们形式化论证了这些效应并通过实验验证：在可塑性缺失场景（如高UTD在线强化学习问题）中，流匹配评论家性能远超单一评论家（最终性能提升2倍，样本效率提升约5倍），且在学习过程中保持稳定。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates why flow matching, a technique for estimating Q-value functions via integration and velocity supervision, outperforms standard monolithic critics in reinforcement learning, challenging the prior attribution to distributional RL. The method's success is attributed to two mechanisms: test-time recovery, where iterative integration corrects early estimation errors, and enhanced plasticity in feature learning, allowing the critic to adapt to non-stationary TD targets without overfitting. Experimental results demonstrate that flow-matching critics achieve roughly double the final performance and five times the sample efficiency of monolithic critics, particularly in high-update-to-data online RL scenarios where plasticity loss is critical, while maintaining stable learning throughout.
本文探讨了流匹配技术通过积分和速度监督估计Q值函数时，为何优于标准的单体批评器，并反驳了先前将其成功归因于分布强化学习的观点。该方法的核心在于两个机制：测试时恢复，即通过迭代积分修正早期估计误差；以及增强的特征学习可塑性，使批评器能适应非平稳的TD目标而不过拟合。实验结果表明，流匹配批评器在最终性能上约提升两倍，样本效率提高约五倍，尤其在更新数据比高的在线强化学习场景中，有效应对了可塑性丧失的挑战，同时保持了学习过程的稳定性。
Unraveling the Complexity of Memory in RL Agents: an Approach for Classification and Evaluation
Authors: Egor Cherepanov, Nikita Kachaev, Artem Zholus, Alexey K. Kovalev, Aleksandr I. Panov
First: 2024-12-09T14:34:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T17:39:28+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 6 figures, 9 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The incorporation of memory into agents is essential for numerous tasks within the domain of Reinforcement Learning (RL). In particular, memory is paramount for tasks that require the use of past information, adaptation to novel environments, and improved sample efficiency. However, the term "memory" encompasses a wide range of concepts, which, coupled with the lack of a unified methodology for validating an agent's memory, leads to erroneous judgments about agents' memory capabilities and prevents objective comparison with other memory-enhanced agents. This paper aims to streamline the concept of memory in RL by providing practical precise definitions of agent memory types, such as long-term vs. short-term memory and declarative vs. procedural memory, inspired by cognitive science. Using these definitions, we categorize different classes of agent memory, propose a robust experimental methodology for evaluating the memory capabilities of RL agents, and standardize evaluations. Furthermore, we empirically demonstrate the importance of adhering to the proposed methodology when evaluating different types of agent memory by conducting experiments with different RL agents and what its violation leads to.

Low-Rank Contextual Reinforcement Learning from Heterogeneous Human Feedback
Authors: Seong Jin Lee, Will Wei Sun, Yufeng Liu
First: 2024-12-27T04:02:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T17:21:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) has become a cornerstone for aligning large language models with human preferences. However, the heterogeneity of human feedback, driven by diverse individual contexts and preferences, poses significant challenges for reward learning. To address this, we propose a Low-rank Contextual RLHF (LoCo-RLHF) framework that integrates contextual information to better model heterogeneous feedback while maintaining computational efficiency. Our approach builds on a contextual preference model, leveraging the intrinsic low-rank structure of the interaction between user contexts and query-answer pairs to mitigate the high dimensionality of feature representations. Furthermore, we address the challenge of distributional shifts in feedback through our Pessimism in Reduced Subspace (PRS) policy, inspired by pessimistic offline reinforcement learning techniques. We theoretically demonstrate that our policy achieves a tighter sub-optimality gap compared to existing methods. Extensive experiments validate the effectiveness of LoCo-RLHF, showcasing its superior performance in personalized RLHF settings and its robustness to distribution shifts.

Experimental results demonstrate that LoCo-RLHF outperforms existing methods in personalized settings, showing superior performance and robustness to distribution shifts, while theoretical analysis confirms a tighter sub-optimality gap for the proposed policy.
针对人类反馈强化学习中因个体背景和偏好差异导致的反馈异质性挑战，本文提出了低秩上下文RLHF（LoCo-RLHF）框架。该方法通过将上下文信息整合到偏好模型中，利用用户上下文与查询-回答对交互的内在低秩结构来高效处理高维特征表示，并引入基于悲观离线强化学习的“降维子空间悲观”（PRS）策略以应对反馈分布偏移。实验验证了LoCo-RLHF在个性化RLHF设置中的有效性，其性能优于现有方法，且对分布偏移具有鲁棒性，理论分析也表明该策略实现了更紧的次优性差距。
Memory, Benchmark & Robots: A Benchmark for Solving Complex Tasks with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Egor Cherepanov, Nikita Kachaev, Alexey K. Kovalev, Aleksandr I. Panov
First: 2025-02-14T20:46:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T17:15:30+00:00
Comments: 57 pages, 29 figures, 11 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Memory is crucial for enabling agents to tackle complex tasks with temporal and spatial dependencies. While many reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms incorporate memory, the field lacks a universal benchmark to assess an agent's memory capabilities across diverse scenarios. This gap is particularly evident in tabletop robotic manipulation, where memory is essential for solving tasks with partial observability and ensuring robust performance, yet no standardized benchmarks exist. To address this, we introduce MIKASA (Memory-Intensive Skills Assessment Suite for Agents), a comprehensive benchmark for memory RL, with three key contributions: (1) we propose a comprehensive classification framework for memory-intensive RL tasks, (2) we collect MIKASA-Base -- a unified benchmark that enables systematic evaluation of memory-enhanced agents across diverse scenarios, and (3) we develop MIKASA-Robo (pip install mikasa-robo-suite) -- a novel benchmark of 32 carefully designed memory-intensive tasks that assess memory capabilities in tabletop robotic manipulation. Our work introduces a unified framework to advance memory RL research, enabling more robust systems for real-world use. MIKASA is available at https://tinyurl.com/membenchrobots.

IPD: Boosting Sequential Policy with Imaginary Planning Distillation in Offline Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yihao Qin, Yuanfei Wang, Hang Zhou, Peiran Liu, Hao Dong, Yiding Ji
First: 2026-03-04T17:05:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T17:05:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Decision transformer based sequential policies have emerged as a powerful paradigm in offline reinforcement learning (RL), yet their efficacy remains constrained by the quality of static datasets and inherent architectural limitations. Specifically, these models often struggle to effectively integrate suboptimal experiences and fail to explicitly plan for an optimal policy. To bridge this gap, we propose \textbf{Imaginary Planning Distillation (IPD)}, a novel framework that seamlessly incorporates offline planning into data generation, supervised training, and online inference. Our framework first learns a world model equipped with uncertainty measures and a quasi-optimal value function from the offline data. These components are utilized to identify suboptimal trajectories and augment them with reliable, imagined optimal rollouts generated via Model Predictive Control (MPC). A Transformer-based sequential policy is then trained on this enriched dataset, complemented by a value-guided objective that promotes the distillation of the optimal policy. By replacing the conventional, manually-tuned return-to-go with the learned quasi-optimal value function, IPD improves both decision-making stability and performance during inference. Empirical evaluations on the D4RL benchmark demonstrate that IPD significantly outperforms several state-of-the-art value-based and transformer-based offline RL methods across diverse tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：IPD：通过虚拟规划蒸馏提升离线强化学习中的序列策略
基于决策变换器的序列策略已成为离线强化学习的重要范式，但其效能仍受限于静态数据集质量与固有架构缺陷。这类模型常难以有效整合次优经验，且无法显式规划最优策略。为弥补这一差距，我们提出\textbf{虚拟规划蒸馏（IPD）}——一种将离线规划无缝融入数据生成、监督训练与在线推理的新框架。该框架首先从离线数据中学习具备不确定性度量的世界模型和准最优价值函数，进而识别次优轨迹并通过模型预测控制生成可靠的虚拟最优轨迹进行增强。随后基于Transformer的序列策略在此增强数据集上进行训练，辅以促进最优策略蒸馏的价值引导目标。通过用习得的准最优价值函数替代传统人工调整的回报目标，IPD显著提升了推理阶段的决策稳定性与性能。在D4RL基准测试中的实证研究表明，IPD在多样化任务上均显著优于当前最先进的基于价值和基于变换器的离线强化学习方法。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limitations of decision transformer-based sequential policies in offline reinforcement learning, which are constrained by static dataset quality and an inability to effectively integrate suboptimal experiences or explicitly plan for optimal policies. The proposed method, Imaginary Planning Distillation (IPD), incorporates offline planning into data generation, training, and inference by first learning a world model with uncertainty measures and a quasi-optimal value function from offline data, then using Model Predictive Control to augment suboptimal trajectories with imagined optimal rollouts, and finally training a Transformer-based policy on this enriched dataset with a value-guided objective. Experimental results on the D4RL benchmark show that IPD significantly outperforms state-of-the-art value-based and transformer-based offline RL methods across diverse tasks, improving decision-making stability and performance.

Recurrent Action Transformer with Memory
Authors: Egor Cherepanov, Alexey Staroverov, Alexey K. Kovalev, Aleksandr I. Panov
First: 2023-06-15T19:29:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T17:00:23+00:00
Comments: 29 pages, 22 figures, 13 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Transformers have become increasingly popular in offline reinforcement learning (RL) due to their ability to treat agent trajectories as sequences, reframing policy learning as a sequence modeling task. However, in partially observable environments (POMDPs), effective decision-making depends on retaining information about past events -- something that standard transformers struggle with due to the quadratic complexity of self-attention, which limits their context length. One solution to this problem is to extend transformers with memory mechanisms. We propose the Recurrent Action Transformer with Memory (RATE), a novel transformer-based architecture for offline RL that incorporates a recurrent memory mechanism designed to regulate information retention. We evaluate RATE across a diverse set of environments: memory-intensive tasks (ViZDoom-Two-Colors, T-Maze, Memory Maze, Minigrid-Memory, and POPGym), as well as standard Atari and MuJoCo benchmarks. Our comprehensive experiments demonstrate that RATE significantly improves performance in memory-dependent settings while remaining competitive on standard tasks across a broad range of baselines. These findings underscore the pivotal role of integrated memory mechanisms in offline RL and establish RATE as a unified, high-capacity architecture for effective decision-making over extended horizons. Code: https://sites.google.com/view/rate-model/.

标题：带记忆的循环动作Transformer
Transformer因其能够将智能体轨迹视为序列、将策略学习重构为序列建模任务，在离线强化学习（RL）中日益普及。然而，在部分可观测环境（POMDPs）中，有效决策依赖于保留历史事件信息——标准Transformer因自注意力二次复杂度限制上下文长度而难以实现。扩展记忆机制是解决此问题的途径之一。我们提出带记忆的循环动作Transformer（RATE），这是一种用于离线RL的新型Transformer架构，集成了旨在调控信息保留的循环记忆机制。我们在多样化环境中评估RATE：记忆密集型任务（ViZDoom双色迷宫、T型迷宫、记忆迷宫、Minigrid记忆任务、POPGym）以及标准Atari和MuJoCo基准测试。综合实验表明，RATE在记忆依赖场景中显著提升性能，同时在广泛基线标准任务中保持竞争力。这些发现凸显了集成记忆机制在离线RL中的关键作用，并将RATE确立为适用于长时程有效决策的统一高容量架构。代码：https://sites.google.com/view/rate-model/。

Memex(RL): Scaling Long-Horizon LLM Agents via Indexed Experience Memory
Authors: Zhenting Wang, Huancheng Chen, Jiayun Wang, Wei Wei
First: 2026-03-04T16:45:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T16:45:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents are fundamentally bottlenecked by finite context windows on long-horizon tasks. As trajectories grow, retaining tool outputs and intermediate reasoning in-context quickly becomes infeasible: the working context becomes prohibitively long, eventually exceeds the context budget, and makes distant evidence harder to use even when it is still present. Existing solutions typically shorten context through truncation or running summaries, but these methods are fundamentally lossy because they compress or discard past evidence itself. We introduce Memex, an indexed experience memory mechanism that instead compresses context without discarding evidence. Memex maintains a compact working context consisting of concise structured summaries and stable indices, while storing full-fidelity underlying interactions in an external experience database under those indices. The agent can then decide when to dereference an index and recover the exact past evidence needed for the current subgoal. We optimize both write and read behaviors with our reinforcement learning framework MemexRL, using reward shaping tailored to indexed memory usage under a context budget, so the agent learns what to summarize, what to archive, how to index it, and when to retrieve it. This yields a substantially less lossy form of long-horizon memory than summary-only approaches. We further provide a theoretical analysis showing the potential of the Memex loop to preserve decision quality with bounded dereferencing while keeping effective in-context computation bounded as history grows. Empirically, on challenging long-horizon tasks, Memex agent trained with MemexRL improves task success while using a significantly smaller working context.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Memex(RL)：通过索引化经验记忆扩展长视野LLM智能体
大语言模型（LLM）智能体在长视野任务中受限于有限的上下文窗口。随着任务轨迹增长，在上下文中保留工具输出和中间推理会迅速变得不可行：工作上下文过长最终会超出预算，且即使早期证据仍存在也难以有效利用。现有方案通常通过截断或运行摘要来缩短上下文，但这些方法本质上有损，因为它们压缩或丢弃了原始证据。我们提出Memex——一种索引化经验记忆机制，它能在不丢弃证据的前提下压缩上下文。Memex维护由精简结构化摘要和稳定索引组成的紧凑工作上下文，同时将完整交互记录存储于外部经验数据库。智能体可随时解引用索引以恢复当前子目标所需的精确历史证据。我们通过强化学习框架MemexRL优化读写行为，在上下文预算下针对索引化内存使用进行奖励塑形，使智能体学会总结、归档、索引及检索的时机。相比仅依赖摘要的方法，这种形式的长视野记忆显著减少了信息损失。理论分析表明Memex循环能在历史增长时保持决策质量，同时将有效上下文计算量控制在有界范围内。在挑战性长视野任务上的实验表明，经MemexRL训练的Memex智能体能以显著更小的工作上下文提升任务成功率。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is that large language model (LLM) agents are constrained by finite context windows on long-horizon tasks, where storing full interaction histories becomes infeasible, leading to lossy compression or discarding of past evidence in existing methods. The proposed method, Memex, introduces an indexed experience memory mechanism that maintains a compact working context with structured summaries and indices while storing full-fidelity interactions in an external database; this is optimized via a reinforcement learning framework, MemexRL, which trains the agent to learn summarization, archiving, indexing, and retrieval behaviors under a context budget. The main experimental results show that on challenging long-horizon tasks, the Memex agent trained with MemexRL achieves improved task success while operating with a significantly smaller working context compared to summary-only approaches.

Generalization of RLVR Using Causal Reasoning as a Testbed
Authors: Brian Lu, Hongyu Zhao, Shuo Sun, Hao Peng, Rui Ding, Hongyuan Mei
First: 2025-12-23T20:45:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T16:41:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a promising paradigm for post-training large language models (LLMs) on complex reasoning tasks. Yet, the conditions under which RLVR yields robust generalization remain underexplored. This paper provides an empirical study of RLVR generalization in the setting of probabilistic inference over causal graphical models. This setting offers two natural axes along which to examine generalization: (i) the level of the probabilistic query -- associational, interventional, or counterfactual -- and (ii) the structural complexity of the query, measured by the size of its relevant subgraph. We construct a dataset of causal graphs and queries spanning these difficulty axes and fine-tune Qwen-2.5-Instruct models using RLVR or supervised fine-tuning (SFT). We vary both the model scale (3B-32B) and the query level included in training. We find that RLVR yields stronger within-level and across-level generalization than SFT, but only for specific combinations of model size and training query level. Further analysis shows that RLVR's effectiveness depends on the model's initial reasoning competence. With sufficient initial competence, RLVR improves an LLM's marginalization strategy and reduces errors in intermediate probability calculations, producing substantial accuracy gains, particularly on more complex queries. These results show that RLVR can improve specific causal reasoning subskills, with its benefits emerging only when the model has sufficient initial competence. Our code and data is available at https://github.com/zhichul/rlcausal.

标题：基于因果推理测试平台的RLVR泛化研究
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）已成为在复杂推理任务上对大型语言模型进行后训练的有前景范式，但其实现稳健泛化的条件尚未充分探索。本文通过因果图模型的概率推断场景，对RLVR的泛化能力进行实证研究。该场景提供两个自然维度以考察泛化性能：（i）概率查询的层级——关联性、干预性或反事实性；（ii）查询的结构复杂度，以其相关子图规模衡量。我们构建了覆盖这些难度维度的因果图与查询数据集，并分别使用RLVR和监督微调对Qwen-2.5-Instruct模型进行微调。通过调整模型规模（3B-32B）和训练中包含的查询层级，发现RLVR仅在特定模型规模与训练查询层级的组合下，能比监督微调产生更强的层级内与跨层级泛化能力。进一步分析表明，RLVR的有效性取决于模型的初始推理能力：当具备足够初始能力时，RLVR能优化模型的边缘化策略，减少中间概率计算错误，从而显著提升准确率，尤其在复杂查询上效果明显。这些结果证明RLVR可改进特定的因果推理子技能，但其优势仅在模型具备足够初始能力时显现。代码与数据公开于https://github.com/zhichul/rlcausal。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the generalization capabilities of reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for improving large language models' performance on causal reasoning tasks, motivated by the need to understand when RLVR yields robust improvements beyond supervised fine-tuning. The method involves constructing a dataset of causal graphs and probabilistic queries that vary in query level and structural complexity, then fine-tuning Qwen-2.5-Instruct models of different scales using RLVR and supervised fine-tuning while controlling the query levels included in training. Experimental results show that RLVR outperforms supervised fine-tuning in both within-level and across-level generalization, but only for specific combinations of model size and training query level, with its effectiveness hinging on the model's initial reasoning competence; further analysis reveals that RLVR enhances marginalization strategies and reduces intermediate calculation errors, leading to significant accuracy gains on complex queries when the model starts with sufficient competence.

Offline-to-Online Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning with Offline Value Function Memory and Sequential Exploration
Authors: Hai Zhong, Xun Wang, Zhuoran Li, Longbo Huang
First: 2024-10-25T10:24:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T16:33:38+00:00
Comments: Include detailed hyperparameter configurations
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning has emerged as a powerful paradigm, leveraging offline data for initialization and online fine-tuning to enhance both sample efficiency and performance. However, most existing research has focused on single-agent settings, with limited exploration of the multi-agent extension, i.e., Offline-to-Online Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (O2O MARL). In O2O MARL, two critical challenges become more prominent as the number of agents increases: (i) the risk of unlearning pre-trained Q-values due to distributional shifts during the transition from offline-to-online phases, and (ii) the difficulty of efficient exploration in the large joint state-action space. To tackle these challenges, we propose a novel O2O MARL framework called Offline Value Function Memory with Sequential Exploration (OVMSE). First, we introduce the Offline Value Function Memory (OVM) mechanism to compute target Q-values, preserving knowledge gained during offline training, ensuring smoother transitions, and enabling efficient fine-tuning. Second, we propose a decentralized Sequential Exploration (SE) strategy tailored for O2O MARL, which effectively utilizes the pre-trained offline policy for exploration, thereby significantly reducing the joint state-action space to be explored. Extensive experiments on the StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge (SMAC) demonstrate that OVMSE significantly outperforms existing baselines, achieving superior sample efficiency and overall performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于离线价值函数记忆与序列化探索的离线至在线多智能体强化学习
离线至在线强化学习已成为一种强大范式，通过利用离线数据进行初始化并在线微调，以提升样本效率与性能。然而现有研究多集中于单智能体场景，对多智能体扩展——即离线至在线多智能体强化学习（O2O MARL）的探索仍显不足。在O2O MARL中，随着智能体数量增加，两大挑战尤为突出：（1）因离线至在线阶段分布偏移导致预训练Q值被遗忘的风险；（2）在庞大的联合状态-动作空间中实现高效探索的困难。为此，我们提出名为“离线价值函数记忆与序列化探索”（OVMSE）的新型O2O MARL框架。首先，引入离线价值函数记忆（OVM）机制计算目标Q值，保留离线训练获得的知识，确保平稳过渡并实现高效微调。其次，提出专为O2O MARL设计的去中心化序列化探索（SE）策略，有效利用预训练离线策略进行探索，从而显著缩减待探索的联合状态-动作空间。在《星际争霸》多智能体挑战（SMAC）上的大量实验表明，OVMSE显著优于现有基线方法，实现了卓越的样本效率与整体性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenges of Offline-to-Online Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (O2O MARL), where directly extending single-agent methods risks unlearning pre-trained policies and faces inefficient exploration in large joint action spaces. The proposed solution, OVMSE, introduces an Offline Value Function Memory to stabilize Q-values against distributional shift during online fine-tuning and a decentralized Sequential Exploration strategy that leverages the offline policy to reduce the exploration space. Experimental results on the StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge show that OVMSE outperforms existing baselines in both sample efficiency and final performance.
本文针对离线到在线多智能体强化学习中的挑战展开研究，即直接扩展单智能体方法会导致预训练策略遗忘，并在大规模联合动作空间中探索低效。提出的OVMSE框架引入了离线价值函数记忆机制，以稳定在线微调期间的Q值并防止分布偏移，同时采用一种分散式顺序探索策略，利用离线策略来缩减探索空间。在星际争霸多智能体挑战上的实验结果表明，OVMSE在样本效率和最终性能上均显著优于现有基线方法。
Learning Hip Exoskeleton Control Policy via Predictive Neuromusculoskeletal Simulation
Authors: Ilseung Park, Changseob Song, Inseung Kang
First: 2026-03-04T15:23:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T15:23:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Developing exoskeleton controllers that generalize across diverse locomotor conditions typically requires extensive motion-capture data and biomechanical labeling, limiting scalability beyond instrumented laboratory settings. Here, we present a physics-based neuromusculoskeletal learning framework that trains a hip-exoskeleton control policy entirely in simulation, without motion-capture demonstrations, and deploys it on hardware via policy distillation. A reinforcement learning teacher policy is trained using a muscle-synergy action prior over a wide range of walking speeds and slopes through a two-stage curriculum, enabling direct comparison between assisted and no-exoskeleton conditions. In simulation, exoskeleton assistance reduces mean muscle activation by up to 3.4% and mean positive joint power by up to 7.0% on level ground and ramp ascent, with benefits increasing systematically with walking speed. On hardware, the assistance profiles learned in simulation are preserved across matched speed-slope conditions (r: 0.82, RMSE: 0.03 Nm/kg), providing quantitative evidence of sim-to-real transfer without additional hardware tuning. These results demonstrate that physics-based neuromusculoskeletal simulation can serve as a practical and scalable foundation for exoskeleton controller development, substantially reducing experimental burden during the design phase.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于预测性神经肌肉骨骼模拟的髋关节外骨骼控制策略学习
开发适用于多种运动条件的外骨骼控制器通常需要大量运动捕捉数据和生物力学标注，这限制了其在仪器化实验室环境之外的可扩展性。本文提出一种基于物理的神经肌肉骨骼学习框架，该框架完全在模拟环境中训练髋关节外骨骼控制策略，无需运动捕捉演示，并通过策略蒸馏将其部署到硬件上。强化学习教师策略采用肌肉协同作用先验，通过两阶段课程在多种步行速度和坡度上进行训练，从而实现对有外骨骼辅助和无外骨骼条件的直接比较。在模拟中，外骨骼辅助使平地与斜坡上行时的平均肌肉激活降低达3.4%，平均正向关节功率降低达7.0%，且效益随步行速度提升而系统性增加。在硬件测试中，模拟学习得到的辅助特性在匹配的速度-坡度条件下保持稳定（相关系数：0.82，均方根误差：0.03 Nm/kg），为无需额外硬件调优的模拟到现实迁移提供了量化证据。这些结果表明，基于物理的神经肌肉骨骼模拟可作为外骨骼控制器开发实用且可扩展的基础，显著降低设计阶段的实验负担。

The method uses a reinforcement learning teacher policy with a muscle-synergy action prior, trained over varied walking speeds and slopes via a two-stage curriculum, and transfers it to hardware through policy distillation. Experimental results in simulation show the exoskeleton reduces mean muscle activation by up to 3.4% and mean positive joint power by up to 7.0% on level ground and ramp ascent, with benefits increasing at higher speeds; on hardware, the learned assistance profiles transfer effectively across matched conditions (correlation 0.82, RMSE 0.03 Nm/kg), demonstrating successful sim-to-real transfer without additional tuning.

InstMeter: An Instruction-Level Method to Predict Energy and Latency of DL Model Inference on MCUs
Authors: Hao Liu, Qing Wang, Marco Zuniga
First: 2026-03-04T14:48:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T14:48:29+00:00
Comments: 17 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep learning (DL) models can now run on microcontrollers (MCUs). Through neural architecture search (NAS), we can search DL models that meet the constraints of MCUs. Among various constraints, energy and latency costs of the model inference are critical metrics. To predict them, existing research relies on coarse proxies such as multiply-accumulations (MACs) and model's input parameters, often resulting in inaccurate predictions or requiring extensive data collection. In this paper, we propose InstMeter, a predictor leveraging MCUs' clock cycles to accurately estimate the energy and latency of DL models. Clock cycles are fundamental metrics reflecting MCU operations, directly determining energy and latency costs. Furthermore, a unique property of our predictor is its strong linearity, allowing it to be simple and accurate. We thoroughly evaluate InstMeter under different scenarios, MCUs, and software settings. Compared with state-of-the-art studies, InstMeter can reduce the energy and latency prediction errors by $3\times$ and $6.5\times$, respectively, while requiring $100\times$ and $10\times$ less training data. In the NAS scenario, InstMeter can fully exploit the energy budget, identifying optimal DL models with higher inference accuracy. We also evaluate InstMeter's generalization performance through various experiments on three ARM MCUs (Cortex-M4, M7, M33) and one RISC-V-based MCU (ESP32-C3), different compilation options (-Os, -O2), GCC versions (v7.3, v10.3), application scenarios (keyword spotting, image recognition), dynamic voltage and frequency scaling, temperatures (21°C, 43°C), and software settings (TFLMv2.4, TFLMvCI). We will open our source codes and the MCU-specific benchmark datasets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：InstMeter：一种基于指令级的深度学习模型在微控制器上推理能耗与延迟预测方法
深度学习模型现已能在微控制器上运行。通过神经架构搜索，我们可以找到满足MCU约束的DL模型。在众多约束中，模型推理的能耗与延迟是关键指标。现有研究依赖乘加运算次数和模型输入参数等粗略代理指标进行预测，常导致结果不准确或需要大量数据收集。本文提出InstMeter，一种利用MCU时钟周期精确预测DL模型能耗与延迟的方法。时钟周期是反映MCU运行状态的基础指标，直接决定能耗与延迟成本。该预测器具有独特的强线性特性，使其兼具简洁性与准确性。我们在不同场景、MCU和软件设置下全面评估InstMeter。与前沿研究相比，InstMeter能将能耗与延迟预测误差分别降低3倍和6.5倍，同时减少100倍和10倍的训练数据需求。在NAS场景中，InstMeter能充分利用能耗预算，识别出具有更高推理精度的最优DL模型。我们通过在三种ARM MCU（Cortex-M4、M7、M33）和一款RISC-V架构MCU（ESP32-C3）上开展实验，验证了方法在编译选项（-Os、-O2）、GCC版本（v7.3、v10.3）、应用场景（关键词识别、图像识别）、动态电压频率调节、温度（21°C、43°C）及软件框架（TFLMv2.4、TFLMvCI）等多种条件下的泛化性能。我们将公开源代码及MCU专用基准数据集。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for accurate energy and latency prediction for deep learning model inference on microcontrollers, which is crucial for neural architecture search under hardware constraints, this paper introduces InstMeter, a method that uses clock cycles as a fundamental metric to estimate these costs with high linearity and simplicity. The method involves leveraging clock cycles to directly model energy and latency, avoiding reliance on coarse proxies like multiply-accumulations, and it is evaluated across various MCUs, software settings, and scenarios. Experimental results show that InstMeter reduces prediction errors for energy and latency by 3x and 6.5x respectively while requiring significantly less training data, and it effectively identifies optimal models in NAS, with validation on multiple ARM and RISC-V MCUs under different conditions.
本文针对在微控制器上运行深度学习模型推理时，需要准确预测能耗和延迟以支持神经架构搜索的需求，提出了InstMeter方法，该方法利用时钟周期作为基本指标，通过其强线性特性来简单而精确地估计这些成本。方法核心是使用时钟周期直接建模能耗和延迟，避免依赖如乘加运算等粗略代理指标，并在多种MCU、软件设置和场景下进行了全面评估。实验结果表明，InstMeter将能耗和延迟的预测误差分别降低了3倍和6.5倍，同时所需训练数据大幅减少，在神经架构搜索中能充分利用能耗预算找到更优模型，并在多种ARM和RISC-V MCU上通过不同条件验证了其泛化性能。
BeamPERL: Parameter-Efficient RL with Verifiable Rewards Specializes Compact LLMs for Structured Beam Mechanics Reasoning
Authors: Tarjei Paule Hage, Markus J. Buehler
First: 2026-03-04T14:42:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T14:42:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Can reinforcement learning with hard, verifiable rewards teach a compact language model to reason about physics, or does it primarily learn to pattern-match toward correct answers? We study this question by training a 1.5B-parameter reasoning model on beam statics, a classic engineering problem, using parameter-efficient RLVR with binary correctness rewards from symbolic solvers, without teacher-generated reasoning traces. The best BeamPERL checkpoint achieves a 66.7% improvement in Pass@1 over the base model. However, the learned competence is anisotropic: the model generalizes compositionally (more loads) but fails under topological shifts (moved supports) that require the same equilibrium equations. Intermediate checkpoints yield the strongest reasoning, while continued optimization degrades robustness while maintaining reward. These findings reveal a key limitation of outcome-level alignment: reinforcement learning with exact physics rewards induces procedural solution templates rather than internalization of governing equations. The precision of the reward signal - even when analytically exact - does not by itself guarantee transferable physical reasoning. Our results suggest that verifiable rewards may need to be paired with structured reasoning scaffolding to move beyond template matching toward robust scientific reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BeamPERL：基于可验证奖励的参数高效强化学习专用于结构化梁力学推理的紧凑型大语言模型
采用严格可验证奖励的强化学习能否教会紧凑语言模型进行物理推理，还是主要使其学会对正确答案的模式匹配？我们通过训练一个15亿参数推理模型研究该问题，该模型基于经典工程问题——梁静力学，采用参数高效的RLVR方法，利用符号求解器提供的二元正确性奖励进行训练，且无需教师生成的推理轨迹。最佳BeamPERL检查点在Pass@1指标上较基础模型提升66.7%。然而习得能力呈现各向异性：模型能实现组合泛化（更多载荷），却在需要相同平衡方程处理的拓扑变化（支座位移）场景中失效。中间检查点展现出最强推理能力，而持续优化在保持奖励的同时降低了鲁棒性。这些发现揭示了结果层面对齐的关键局限：基于精确物理奖励的强化学习仅诱导程序化解题模板，而非对控制方程的内化。即使奖励信号在解析层面完全精确，其本身也无法保证可迁移的物理推理能力。我们的结果表明，可验证奖励可能需要与结构化推理框架结合，才能超越模板匹配，实现稳健的科学推理。
Summary / 总结
This study investigates whether reinforcement learning with verifiable, binary rewards can teach a compact language model to perform genuine physics reasoning rather than merely pattern-matching correct answers. The authors introduce BeamPERL, a parameter-efficient RL method that trains a 1.5B-parameter model on beam statics problems using only correctness rewards from symbolic solvers, without relying on human-provided reasoning traces. Experimental results show the best checkpoint achieves a 66.7% improvement in Pass@1 over the base model, but the learned competence is anisotropic: it generalizes to compositional variations like additional loads yet fails under topological shifts such as moved supports, which require the same underlying physics. Notably, intermediate training checkpoints yield the strongest reasoning performance, while further optimization degrades robustness despite maintaining high reward, revealing that outcome-level alignment with exact rewards can induce procedural solution templates rather than an internalized understanding of the governing equations.
本研究探讨了使用可验证的二元奖励进行强化学习，能否教会一个紧凑的语言模型进行真正的物理推理，而非仅仅对正确答案进行模式匹配。作者提出了BeamPERL，一种参数高效的强化学习方法，仅使用符号求解器提供的正确性奖励来训练一个15亿参数的模型解决梁静力学问题，无需人类提供的推理轨迹。实验结果表明，最佳检查点在Pass@1指标上比基础模型提高了66.7%，但习得的能力是各向异性的：它能泛化到组合性变化（如增加载荷），却在需要相同物理方程支持的拓扑结构变化（如移动支座）上失败。值得注意的是，中间训练检查点产生了最强的推理性能，而进一步优化尽管保持了高奖励，却损害了鲁棒性，这表明基于精确奖励的结果层面对齐可能诱导出程序化的解决方案模板，而非对控制方程的内在理解。
Learning in Markov Decision Processes with Exogenous Dynamics
Authors: Davide Maran, Davide Salaorni, Marcello Restelli
First: 2026-03-03T11:10:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T14:42:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning algorithms are typically designed for generic Markov Decision Processes (MDPs), where any state-action pair can lead to an arbitrary transition distribution. In many practical systems, however, only a subset of the state variables is directly influenced by the agent's actions, while the remaining components evolve according to exogenous dynamics and account for most of the stochasticity. In this work, we study a structured class of MDPs characterized by exogenous state components whose transitions are independent of the agent's actions. We show that exploiting this structure yields significantly improved learning guarantees, with only the size of the exogenous state space appearing in the leading terms of the regret bounds. We further establish a matching lower bound, showing that this dependence is information-theoretically optimal. Finally, we empirically validate our approach across classical toy settings and real-world-inspired environments, demonstrating substantial gains in sample efficiency compared to standard reinforcement learning methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：具有外生动态的马尔可夫决策过程学习
强化学习算法通常为通用马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）设计，其中任意状态-动作对可导致任意转移分布。然而，在许多实际系统中，仅部分状态变量直接受智能体动作影响，其余部分则按外生动态演化并构成随机性的主要来源。本研究针对一类具有外生状态分量的结构化MDP展开分析，其转移过程独立于智能体动作。我们证明利用该结构可显著提升学习保证，仅外生状态空间规模出现在遗憾边界的主导项中。进一步建立匹配下界，表明该依赖关系在信息论意义下最优。最后，通过在经典玩具场景和现实启发环境中进行实证验证，相比标准强化学习方法，本方法在样本效率上展现出显著优势。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the observation that many real-world systems have state variables with exogenous dynamics unaffected by the agent's actions, a structure not exploited by standard reinforcement learning methods for general Markov Decision Processes. The authors propose a learning framework that explicitly leverages this exogenous structure, deriving regret bounds that depend primarily on the size of the exogenous state space rather than the full state space, and prove these bounds are information-theoretically optimal via a matching lower bound. Experimental results on toy problems and real-world-inspired environments confirm that the method achieves substantially improved sample efficiency over standard reinforcement learning algorithms.
本文的动机是观察到许多现实世界系统中的部分状态变量具有外生动态，不受智能体行动影响，而标准的强化学习方法并未利用这种一般马尔可夫决策过程之外的结构。作者提出了一种显式利用此外生结构的学习框架，推导出的遗憾边界主要依赖于外生状态空间的规模而非完整状态空间，并通过匹配的下界证明该依赖在信息论意义下是最优的。在经典玩具设置和现实世界启发环境上的实验结果表明，该方法相比标准强化学习算法显著提高了样本效率。
Knowledge Graphs are Implicit Reward Models: Path-Derived Signals Enable Compositional Reasoning
Authors: Yuval Kansal, Niraj K. Jha
First: 2026-01-21T16:38:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T14:21:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models have achieved near-expert performance in structured reasoning domains like mathematics and programming, yet their ability to perform compositional multi-hop reasoning in specialized scientific fields remains limited. We propose a bottom-up learning paradigm in which models are grounded in axiomatic domain facts and compose them to solve complex, unseen tasks. To this end, we present a post-training pipeline, based on a combination of supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning (RL), in which knowledge graphs act as implicit reward models. By deriving novel reward signals from knowledge graph paths, we provide verifiable, scalable, and grounded supervision that encourages models to compose intermediate axioms rather than optimize only final answers during RL. We validate this approach in the medical domain, training a 14B model on short-hop reasoning paths (1-3 hops) and evaluating its zero-shot generalization to complex multi-hop queries (4-5 hops). Our experiments show that path-derived rewards act as a "compositional bridge", enabling our model to significantly outperform much larger models and frontier systems like GPT-5.2 and Gemini 3 Pro, on the most difficult reasoning tasks. Furthermore, we demonstrate the robustness of our approach to adversarial perturbations against option-shuffling stress tests. This work suggests that grounding the reasoning process in structured knowledge is a scalable and efficient path toward intelligent reasoning.

标题：知识图谱作为隐式奖励模型：路径衍生信号赋能组合推理
大型语言模型在数学与编程等结构化推理领域已接近专家水平，但其在专业科学领域进行组合式多跳推理的能力仍有限。我们提出一种自底向上的学习范式，使模型基于公理化领域事实进行组合以解决复杂未知任务。为此，我们提出一种结合监督微调与强化学习的后训练流程，其中知识图谱充当隐式奖励模型。通过从知识图谱路径中衍生新颖奖励信号，我们提供可验证、可扩展且具基础性的监督，促使模型在强化学习中组合中间公理而非仅优化最终答案。我们在医学领域验证该方法，使用短跳推理路径（1-3跳）训练140亿参数模型，并评估其对复杂多跳查询（4-5跳）的零样本泛化能力。实验表明，路径衍生奖励作为“组合桥梁”，使我们的模型在最困难推理任务上显著超越更大规模模型及GPT-5.2、Gemini 3 Pro等前沿系统。此外，我们验证了该方法在选项重排压力测试中对对抗性扰动的鲁棒性。这项工作表明，将推理过程锚定于结构化知识是实现智能推理的可扩展高效路径。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limitation of large language models in performing compositional multi-hop reasoning within specialized scientific fields, despite their proficiency in structured domains like mathematics. The method introduces a bottom-up learning paradigm that grounds models in axiomatic domain facts, employing a post-training pipeline combining supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning, where knowledge graphs serve as implicit reward models by providing path-derived reward signals to encourage compositional reasoning rather than just final answer optimization. The main experimental results, validated in the medical domain with a 14B model trained on short-hop paths, demonstrate zero-shot generalization to complex multi-hop queries, significantly outperforming larger models and frontier systems like GPT-5.2 and Gemini 3 Pro on difficult reasoning tasks, while also showing robustness to adversarial perturbations in option-shuffling stress tests.

SaFeR: Safety-Critical Scenario Generation for Autonomous Driving Test via Feasibility-Constrained Token Resampling
Authors: Jinlong Cui, Fenghua Liang, Guo Yang, Chengcheng Tang, Jianxun Cui
First: 2026-03-04T13:46:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T13:46:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety-critical scenario generation is crucial for evaluating autonomous driving systems. However, existing approaches often struggle to balance three conflicting objectives: adversarial criticality, physical feasibility, and behavioral realism. To bridge this gap, we propose SaFeR: safety-critical scenario generation for autonomous driving test via feasibility-constrained token resampling. We first formulate traffic generation as a discrete next token prediction problem, employing a Transformer-based model as a realism prior to capture naturalistic driving distributions. To capture complex interactions while effectively mitigating attention noise, we propose a novel differential attention mechanism within the realism prior. Building on this prior, SaFeR implements a novel resampling strategy that induces adversarial behaviors within a high-probability trust region to maintain naturalism, while enforcing a feasibility constraint derived from the Largest Feasible Region (LFR). By approximating the LFR via offline reinforcement learning, SaFeR effectively prevents the generation of theoretically inevitable collisions. Closed-loop experiments on the Waymo Open Motion Dataset and nuPlan demonstrate that SaFeR significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving a higher solution rate and superior kinematic realism while maintaining strong adversarial effectiveness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SaFeR：基于可行性约束令牌重采样的自动驾驶测试安全关键场景生成
安全关键场景生成对自动驾驶系统评估至关重要，但现有方法常难以平衡对抗关键性、物理可行性与行为真实性这三个冲突目标。为此，我们提出SaFeR：通过可行性约束令牌重采样实现自动驾驶测试的安全关键场景生成。我们首先将交通场景生成建模为离散的下一令牌预测问题，采用基于Transformer的模型作为真实性先验以捕捉自然驾驶分布。为在捕获复杂交互的同时有效抑制注意力噪声，我们在真实性先验中提出一种新颖的差分注意力机制。基于此先验，SaFeR实施一种创新的重采样策略：在高概率信任区域内诱导对抗行为以保持自然性，同时强制执行源自最大可行区域（LFR）的可行性约束。通过离线强化学习近似LFR，SaFeR有效避免了理论上必然碰撞的生成。在Waymo开放运动数据集和nuPlan上的闭环实验表明，SaFeR显著优于现有基线方法，在保持强对抗有效性的同时，实现了更高的求解率和更优的运动学真实性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the challenge of generating safety-critical scenarios for autonomous driving tests that must simultaneously satisfy adversarial criticality, physical feasibility, and behavioral realism, objectives which are often in conflict. The proposed method, SaFeR, formulates traffic generation as a discrete token prediction problem using a Transformer-based model as a realism prior, enhanced with a novel differential attention mechanism to capture interactions and reduce noise. It then employs a feasibility-constrained token resampling strategy, guided by an offline RL-approximated Largest Feasible Region, to induce adversarial behaviors within a realistic trust region while avoiding inevitable collisions. Experimental results on the Waymo Open Motion Dataset and nuPlan show that SaFeR outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving higher solution rates, superior kinematic realism, and strong adversarial effectiveness.
本研究的动机是解决自动驾驶测试中安全关键场景生成的难题，该场景需同时满足对抗关键性、物理可行性和行为真实性这三个常相互冲突的目标。所提出的SaFeR方法将交通生成构建为离散令牌预测问题，采用基于Transformer的模型作为真实性先验，并引入一种新颖的差分注意力机制以捕捉交互并降低噪声。在此基础上，SaFeR实施了一种可行性约束的令牌重采样策略，该策略通过离线强化学习近似最大可行区域来引导，从而在保持自然主义的可信区域内诱导对抗行为，同时避免理论上的必然碰撞。在Waymo Open Motion数据集和nuPlan上的闭环实验表明，SaFeR显著优于现有先进基线，实现了更高的解决率、更优的运动学真实性，并保持了强大的对抗有效性。
A Review of Reward Functions for Reinforcement Learning in the context of Autonomous Driving
Authors: Ahmed Abouelazm, Jonas Michel, J. Marius Zoellner
First: 2024-04-12T08:32:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T13:43:15+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the 35th IEEE Intelligent Vehicles Symposium (IV 2024)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has emerged as an important approach for autonomous driving. A reward function is used in reinforcement learning to establish the learned skill objectives and guide the agent toward the optimal policy. Since autonomous driving is a complex domain with partly conflicting objectives with varying degrees of priority, developing a suitable reward function represents a fundamental challenge. This paper aims to highlight the gap in such function design by assessing different proposed formulations in the literature and dividing individual objectives into Safety, Comfort, Progress, and Traffic Rules compliance categories. Additionally, the limitations of the reviewed reward functions are discussed, such as objectives aggregation and indifference to driving context. Furthermore, the reward categories are frequently inadequately formulated and lack standardization. This paper concludes by proposing future research that potentially addresses the observed shortcomings in rewards, including a reward validation framework and structured rewards that are context-aware and able to resolve conflicts.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自动驾驶强化学习中奖励函数研究综述
强化学习已成为自动驾驶领域的重要方法。奖励函数在强化学习中用于设定学习目标并引导智能体获得最优策略。由于自动驾驶领域复杂且存在部分冲突的多优先级目标，设计合适的奖励函数是一项根本性挑战。本文通过评估文献中提出的不同奖励函数形式，将具体目标划分为安全性、舒适性、行进效率和交通规则遵守四大类别，旨在揭示该领域的设计空白。同时讨论了现有奖励函数的局限性，如目标聚合方式单一、对驾驶场景缺乏敏感性等问题。此外，当前奖励函数类别常存在定义不充分且缺乏标准化的问题。最后提出未来研究方向，包括建立奖励函数验证框架，以及设计具有场景感知能力和冲突解决机制的结构化奖励函数，以解决现有缺陷。
Summary / 总结
This review paper is motivated by the critical role of reward functions in reinforcement learning for autonomous driving, where designing effective rewards is challenging due to the domain's complexity and conflicting objectives. The method involves assessing existing reward formulations from the literature and categorizing them into Safety, Comfort, Progress, and Traffic Rules compliance. The main experimental results highlight that current reward functions suffer from limitations such as inadequate formulation of categories, lack of standardization, issues with objective aggregation, and context indifference, leading to a proposed future research direction focusing on context-aware, structured rewards and a validation framework.
本文的动机在于奖励函数在自动驾驶强化学习中的关键作用，由于该领域目标复杂且存在冲突，设计有效的奖励函数是一大挑战。方法上，论文通过评估文献中已有的奖励函数公式，将其目标归类为安全性、舒适性、行进效率和交通规则遵守四大类别。主要分析结果表明，现有奖励函数存在诸多局限，如类别构建不充分、缺乏标准化、目标聚合问题以及对驾驶情境不敏感，因此文末提出了未来研究方向，包括开发情境感知的结构化奖励和验证框架以解决这些缺陷。
Self-adapting Robotic Agents through Online Continual Reinforcement Learning with World Model Feedback
Authors: Fabian Domberg, Georg Schildbach
Venue: IROS 2026
First: 2026-03-04T13:07:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T13:07:42+00:00
Comments: submitted to IROS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As learning-based robotic controllers are typically trained offline and deployed with fixed parameters, their ability to cope with unforeseen changes during operation is limited. Biologically inspired, this work presents a framework for online Continual Reinforcement Learning that enables automated adaptation during deployment. Building on DreamerV3, a model-based Reinforcement Learning algorithm, the proposed method leverages world model prediction residuals to detect out-of-distribution events and automatically trigger finetuning. Adaptation progress is monitored using both task-level performance signals and internal training metrics, allowing convergence to be assessed without external supervision and domain knowledge. The approach is validated on a variety of contemporary continuous control problems, including a quadruped robot in high-fidelity simulation, and a real-world model vehicle. Relevant metrics and their interpretation are presented and discussed, as well as resulting trade-offs described. The results sketch out how autonomous robotic agents could once move beyond static training regimes toward adaptive systems capable of self-reflection and -improvement during operation, just like their biological counterparts.

标题：基于世界模型反馈的在线持续强化学习实现自适应机器人智能体
基于学习的机器人控制器通常在离线状态下训练并以固定参数部署，其应对运行中突发变化的能力有限。受生物学启发，本研究提出一种在线持续强化学习框架，可在部署期间实现自动适应。该方法以基于模型的强化学习算法DreamerV3为基础，利用世界模型预测残差检测分布外事件并自动触发微调。通过任务级性能信号与内部训练指标双重监控适应进程，无需外部监督与领域知识即可评估收敛性。该框架在多种现代连续控制问题上得到验证，包括高保真仿真四足机器人与真实世界模型车辆。研究详细呈现了相关指标及其解读，并阐述了由此产生的权衡关系。实验结果初步勾勒出自主机器人智能体如何突破静态训练范式，向具备运行中自我反思与改进能力的自适应系统演进，正如其生物对应物一般。
