Discriminative Perception via Anchored Description for Reasoning Segmentation
Authors: Tao Yang, Qing Zhou, Yanliang Li, Qi Wang
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-04T12:46:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T12:46:27+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reasoning segmentation increasingly employs reinforcement learning to generate explanatory reasoning chains that guide Multimodal Large Language Models. While these geometric rewards are primarily confined to guiding the final localization, they are incapable of discriminating whether the reasoning process remains anchored on the referred region or strays into irrelevant context. Lacking this discriminative guidance, the model's reasoning often devolves into unfocused and verbose chains that ultimately fail to disambiguate and perceive the target in complex scenes. This suggests a need to complement the RL objective with Discriminative Perception, an ability to actively distinguish a target from its context. To realize this, we propose DPAD to compel the model to generate a descriptive caption of the referred object, which is then used to explicitly discriminate by contrasting the caption's semantic relevance to the referred object against the wider context. By optimizing for this discriminative capability, the model is forced to focus on the unique attributes of the target, leading to a more converged and efficient reasoning chain. The descriptive caption also serves as an interpretability rationale that aligns with the segmentation. Experiments on the benchmarks confirm the validity of our approach, delivering substantial performance gains, with the cIoU on ReasonSeg increasing by 3.09% and the reasoning chain length decreasing by approximately 42%. Code is available at https://github.com/mrazhou/DPAD
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于锚定描述的判别感知用于推理分割
推理分割领域日益采用强化学习生成解释性推理链以指导多模态大语言模型。然而，这类几何奖励主要局限于引导最终定位，无法判别推理过程是否始终锚定于所指区域或偏离至无关上下文。缺乏此类判别性引导时，模型的推理常退化为散漫冗长的链条，最终难以在复杂场景中消歧并感知目标。这表明需要以判别感知能力补充强化学习目标——即主动区分目标与其上下文的能力。为此，我们提出DPAD方法，强制模型生成所指对象的描述性标题，并通过对比该标题与所指对象及更广上下文的语义相关性实现显式判别。通过优化此判别能力，模型被迫聚焦于目标的独特属性，从而产生更收敛高效的推理链。描述性标题同时可作为与分割结果对齐的可解释性依据。基准测试实验证实了方法的有效性：ReasonSeg数据集上的cIoU提升3.09%，推理链长度减少约42%。代码发布于https://github.com/mrazhou/DPAD
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the observation that existing reinforcement learning approaches for reasoning segmentation, which use geometric rewards to guide Multimodal Large Language Models, lack the ability to discriminate whether the reasoning process remains anchored on the target region or drifts into irrelevant context, leading to verbose and unfocused chains. To address this, the method proposes DPAD (Discriminative Perception via Anchored Description), which compels the model to generate a descriptive caption of the referred object and then explicitly discriminates the target by contrasting the caption's semantic relevance to the object against the wider context. The main experimental results on the ReasonSeg benchmark show substantial performance gains, with a 3.09% increase in cIoU and an approximately 42% decrease in reasoning chain length, confirming the approach's validity in producing more converged and efficient reasoning.
本研究的动机源于观察到，现有用于推理分割的强化学习方法使用几何奖励来指导多模态大语言模型，但缺乏区分推理过程是锚定在目标区域还是漂移到无关上下文的能力，导致推理链冗长且不聚焦。为解决此问题，该方法提出了DPAD（基于锚定描述的判别性感知），通过迫使模型生成所指对象的描述性标题，然后通过对比该标题与目标对象及更广泛上下文的语义相关性来进行显式判别。在ReasonSeg基准上的主要实验结果表明性能有显著提升，cIoU提高了3.09%，推理链长度减少了约42%，证实了该方法在产生更收敛、高效推理方面的有效性。
Training High-Level Schedulers with Execution-Feedback Reinforcement Learning for Long-Horizon GUI Automation
Authors: Zehao Deng, Tianjie Ju, Zheng Wu, Zhuosheng Zhang, Gongshen Liu
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2025-11-27T09:01:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T12:15:06+00:00
Comments: Accepted to CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The rapid development of large vision-language model (VLM) has greatly promoted the research of GUI agent. However, GUI agents still face significant challenges in handling long-horizon tasks. First, single-agent models struggle to balance high-level capabilities and low-level execution capability, facing prevalent issues of responsibility coupling and capability conflicts. Second, agents lack awareness of the task state, leading to progress loss in long-horizon tasks. To address these challenges, we propose a staged execution-feedback reinforcement learning algorithm. Unlike training a unified policy model, we focus on training high-level scheduling models. Specifically, we propose and train two agents: a Coordinator, responsible for the strategic planning and task decomposition; and a State Tracker, responsible for context compression and information management to maintain the task's state and coherence. Based on this, we built the Coordinator-Executor-State Tracker (CES) multi-agent framework, which can be integrated with any low-level Executor model, assisting the Executor in solving long-horizon tasks through task scheduling and state management. Experiments on long-horizon task benchmarks demonstrate that CES significantly enhances the system's planning and state management capabilities. Furthermore, analysis confirms that our trained high-level scheduling module is a generalizable, plug-and-play module that significantly enhances the long-horizon capabilities of various Executors. Code can be available at https://github.com/hehehahi4/CES.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于执行反馈强化学习训练高层调度器以实现长程GUI自动化
大规模视觉语言模型（VLM）的快速发展极大地推动了GUI智能体的研究。然而，GUI智能体在处理长程任务时仍面临重大挑战：其一，单智能体模型难以平衡高层规划能力与底层执行能力，普遍存在职责耦合与能力冲突问题；其二，智能体缺乏任务状态感知能力，导致长程任务中的进度丢失。为应对这些挑战，我们提出了一种分阶段的执行反馈强化学习算法。区别于训练统一的策略模型，我们专注于训练高层调度模型。具体而言，我们提出并训练了两个智能体：负责战略规划与任务分解的协调器（Coordinator），以及负责上下文压缩与信息管理以维持任务状态与连贯性的状态追踪器（State Tracker）。在此基础上，我们构建了协调器-执行器-状态追踪器（CES）多智能体框架，该框架可与任何底层执行器（Executor）模型集成，通过任务调度与状态管理协助执行器解决长程任务。在长程任务基准测试上的实验表明，CES显著提升了系统的规划与状态管理能力。进一步分析证实，我们训练的高层调度模块是一个可泛化、即插即用的模块，能显著增强各类执行器的长程任务处理能力。代码发布于：https://github.com/hehehahi4/CES。

The method develops a multi-agent framework called CES, comprising a Coordinator for strategic planning and task decomposition and a State Tracker for context compression and information management, which works alongside any low-level Executor model. Black Box Meta-Learning Intrinsic Rewards
Authors: Octavio Pappalardo, Rodrigo Ramele, Juan Miguel Santos
First: 2024-07-31T12:09:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T11:49:12+00:00
Comments: Improved exposition; no technical changes to content
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The broader application of reinforcement learning (RL) is limited by challenges including data efficiency, generalization capability, and ability to learn in sparse-reward environments. Meta-learning has emerged as a promising approach to address these issues by optimizing components of the learning algorithm to meet desired characteristics. Additionally, a different line of work has extensively studied the use of intrinsic rewards to enhance the exploration capabilities of algorithms. This work investigates how meta-learning can improve the training signal received by RL agents. We introduce a method to learn intrinsic rewards within a reinforcement learning framework that bypasses the typical computation of meta-gradients through an optimization process by treating policy updates as black boxes. We validate our approach against training with extrinsic rewards, demonstrating its effectiveness, and additionally compare it to the use of a meta-learned advantage function. Experiments are carried out on distributions of continuous control tasks with both parametric and non-parametric variations. Furthermore, only sparse rewards are used during evaluation. Code is available at: https: //github.com/Octavio-Pappalardo/Meta-learning-rewards
中文标题/摘要
标题：黑盒元学习内在奖励机制
强化学习（RL）的广泛应用受限于数据效率、泛化能力及稀疏奖励环境下的学习能力等挑战。元学习通过优化学习算法的组件以满足期望特性，已成为解决这些问题的有效途径。与此同时，另一研究方向深入探索了利用内在奖励增强算法探索能力的方法。本研究探讨元学习如何改进RL智能体接收的训练信号，提出一种在强化学习框架内学习内在奖励的方法：将策略更新视为黑盒，通过优化过程规避元梯度的典型计算流程。实验通过对比外在奖励训练验证了该方法的有效性，并与元学习优势函数的使用进行了比较。研究在参数化与非参数化变体的连续控制任务分布上进行测试，且评估阶段仅使用稀疏奖励。代码已开源：https://github.com/Octavio-Pappalardo/Meta-learning-rewards
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitations of reinforcement learning (RL) in data efficiency, generalization, and sparse-reward environments by meta-learning intrinsic rewards to enhance the training signal. The method treats policy updates as black boxes, avoiding direct meta-gradient computation, to learn intrinsic rewards within an RL framework. Experimental results on continuous control task distributions, using only sparse rewards for evaluation, demonstrate the approach's effectiveness over extrinsic reward training and a meta-learned advantage function baseline.
本文针对强化学习在数据效率、泛化能力和稀疏奖励环境中的局限性，提出通过元学习内在奖励来增强训练信号。该方法将策略更新视为黑箱，避免直接计算元梯度，从而在强化学习框架内学习内在奖励。在连续控制任务分布上的实验结果表明，仅使用稀疏奖励进行评估时，该方法优于外在奖励训练和元学习优势函数基线，验证了其有效性。
GIPO: Gaussian Importance Sampling Policy Optimization
Authors: Chengxuan Lu, Zhenquan Zhang, Shukuan Wang, Qunzhi Lin, Baigui Sun, Yang Liu
First: 2026-03-04T11:34:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T11:34:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Post-training with reinforcement learning (RL) has recently shown strong promise for advancing multimodal agents beyond supervised imitation. However, RL remains limited by poor data efficiency, particularly in settings where interaction data are scarce and quickly become outdated. To address this challenge, GIPO (Gaussian Importance sampling Policy Optimization) is proposed as a policy optimization objective based on truncated importance sampling, replacing hard clipping with a log-ratio-based Gaussian trust weight to softly damp extreme importance ratios while maintaining non-zero gradients. Theoretical analysis shows that GIPO introduces an implicit, tunable constraint on the update magnitude, while concentration bounds guarantee robustness and stability under finite-sample estimation. Experimental results show that GIPO achieves state-of-the-art performance among clipping-based baselines across a wide range of replay buffer sizes, from near on-policy to highly stale data, while exhibiting superior bias--variance trade-off, high training stability and improved sample efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GIPO：高斯重要性采样策略优化
强化学习（RL）的后训练近期展现出推动多模态智能体超越监督式模仿学习的巨大潜力。然而，RL仍受限于数据效率低下，尤其在交互数据稀缺且快速过时的场景中。为应对这一挑战，本文提出GIPO（高斯重要性采样策略优化），这是一种基于截断重要性采样的策略优化目标，通过基于对数比的高斯信任权重替代硬截断，以软阻尼极端重要性比率，同时保持非零梯度。理论分析表明，GIPO对更新幅度引入了隐式可调约束，而集中性界限保证了有限样本估计下的鲁棒性与稳定性。实验结果显示，在从近同策略到高度陈旧数据的广泛经验回放缓冲区规模中，GIPO在基于截断的基线方法中实现了最优性能，同时展现出更优的偏差-方差权衡、更高的训练稳定性及改进的样本效率。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the poor data efficiency of reinforcement learning in post-training, especially when interaction data are scarce and quickly become outdated. To address this, the authors propose GIPO, a policy optimization method that uses truncated importance sampling with a log-ratio-based Gaussian trust weight to softly damp extreme importance ratios while preserving non-zero gradients, theoretically ensuring robust and stable updates. Experimental results demonstrate that GIPO achieves state-of-the-art performance among clipping-based methods across various replay buffer sizes, from near on-policy to stale data, showing superior bias-variance trade-off, training stability, and sample efficiency.
本文的动机在于强化学习在训练后阶段数据效率低下，特别是在交互数据稀缺且迅速过时的场景中。为解决这一问题，作者提出了GIPO方法，它基于截断重要性采样，采用对数比高斯信任权重来柔和地抑制极端重要性比率，同时保持非零梯度，理论分析表明该方法引入了可调的隐式更新幅度约束，并保证了有限样本估计下的鲁棒性和稳定性。实验结果显示，GIPO在从近在线到高度陈旧数据的不同回放缓冲区大小下，均优于基于裁剪的基线方法，实现了最佳的偏差-方差权衡、高训练稳定性和改进的样本效率。
RVN-Bench: A Benchmark for Reactive Visual Navigation
Authors: Jaewon Lee, Jaeseok Heo, Gunmin Lee, Howoong Jun, Jeongwoo Oh, Songhwai Oh
First: 2026-03-04T11:26:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T11:26:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Safe visual navigation is critical for indoor mobile robots operating in cluttered environments. Existing benchmarks, however, often neglect collisions or are designed for outdoor scenarios, making them unsuitable for indoor visual navigation. To address this limitation, we introduce the reactive visual navigation benchmark (RVN-Bench), a collision-aware benchmark for indoor mobile robots. In RVN-Bench, an agent must reach sequential goal positions in previously unseen environments using only visual observations and no prior map, while avoiding collisions. Built on the Habitat 2.0 simulator and leveraging high-fidelity HM3D scenes, RVN-Bench provides large-scale, diverse indoor environments, defines a collision-aware navigation task and evaluation metrics, and offers tools for standardized training and benchmarking. RVN-Bench supports both online and offline learning by offering an environment for online reinforcement learning, a trajectory image dataset generator, and tools for producing negative trajectory image datasets that capture collision events. Experiments show that policies trained on RVN-Bench generalize effectively to unseen environments, demonstrating its value as a standardized benchmark for safe and robust visual navigation. Code and additional materials are available at: https://rvn-bench.github.io/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RVN-Bench：反应式视觉导航基准
安全视觉导航对于在杂乱室内环境中运行的移动机器人至关重要。然而，现有基准常忽略碰撞问题或专为户外场景设计，不适用于室内视觉导航。为弥补这一不足，我们提出了反应式视觉导航基准（RVN-Bench），这是一个面向室内移动机器人的碰撞感知基准。在RVN-Bench中，智能体需仅凭视觉观测、无需先验地图，在未知环境中依次抵达目标位置并规避碰撞。该基准基于Habitat 2.0模拟器，利用高保真HM3D场景，提供大规模多样化室内环境，定义了碰撞感知导航任务与评估指标，并配备标准化训练与基准测试工具。通过提供在线强化学习环境、轨迹图像数据集生成器，以及记录碰撞事件的负轨迹图像数据集制作工具，RVN-Bench同时支持在线与离线学习。实验表明，基于RVN-Bench训练的策略能有效泛化至未知环境，验证了其作为安全鲁棒视觉导航标准化基准的价值。代码与补充材料详见：https://rvn-bench.github.io/。

The method involves creating a benchmark built on the Habitat 2.0 simulator with high-fidelity HM3D scenes, which defines a task where an agent must navigate to sequential goals using only visual observations without a prior map while avoiding collisions, and provides tools for standardized training including online reinforcement learning and trajectory dataset generation. The main experimental results demonstrate that policies trained using RVN-Bench effectively generalize to unseen environments, validating its utility as a benchmark for safe and robust visual navigation.
RVN-Bench的提出动机是解决室内视觉导航领域缺乏碰撞感知基准的问题，因为现有基准常忽略碰撞或专为户外设计。该方法基于Habitat 2.0模拟器和高保真HM3D场景构建了一个基准，定义了智能体在无先验地图情况下仅凭视觉观察导航至连续目标点并避免碰撞的任务，并提供了标准化训练工具，包括在线强化学习和轨迹数据集生成器。主要实验结果表明，使用RVN-Bench训练的策略能有效泛化到未见环境，证实了其作为安全、鲁棒视觉导航标准化基准的价值。
Dynamic Adversarial Reinforcement Learning for Robust Multimodal Large Language Models
Authors: Yicheng Bao, Xuhong Wang, Qiaosheng Zhang, Chaochao Lu, Xia Hu, Xin Tan
First: 2026-01-24T03:47:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T11:04:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite their impressive capabilities, Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) exhibit perceptual fragility when confronted with visually complex scenes. This weakness stems from a reliance on finite training datasets, which are prohibitively expensive to scale and impose a ceiling on model robustness. We introduce \textbf{AOT-SFT}, a large-scale adversarial dataset for bootstrapping MLLM robustness. Building on this, we propose \textbf{AOT (Adversarial Opponent Training)}, a self-play framework that forges MLLM robustness by creating its own training data. Our method orchestrates a co-evolution between an image-editing Attacker and a Defender MLLM, where the Attacker generates a diverse and dynamic curriculum of image manipulations, forcing the Defender to adapt and improve. Extensive experiments demonstrate that AOT enhances the Defender's perceptual robustness and reduces hallucinations, establishing a scalable paradigm for training more reliable MLLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：动态对抗强化学习：构建鲁棒的多模态大语言模型
尽管多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）展现出卓越能力，但在面对视觉复杂场景时仍表现出感知脆弱性。这一弱点源于对有限训练数据的依赖，此类数据扩展成本极高且限制了模型鲁棒性的上限。本文提出\textbf{AOT-SFT}，一个用于引导MLLM鲁棒性的大规模对抗数据集。在此基础上，我们提出\textbf{AOT（对抗对手训练）}——一种通过自主生成训练数据来锻造MLLM鲁棒性的自我博弈框架。该方法构建了图像编辑攻击者与防御者MLLM的协同进化机制：攻击者生成多样化动态的图像操作课程，迫使防御者持续适应与改进。大量实验表明，AOT能显著提升防御者的感知鲁棒性并减少幻觉，为训练更可靠的MLLM建立了可扩展的范式。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the perceptual fragility of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) in complex visual scenes due to limited and costly training data, this paper introduces AOT-SFT, a large-scale adversarial dataset, and AOT (Adversarial Opponent Training), a self-play framework. The method employs a co-evolutionary process between an image-editing Attacker and a Defender MLLM, where the Attacker dynamically generates manipulated images to create a challenging training curriculum, thereby forcing the Defender to adapt. Experimental results show that AOT significantly improves the Defender's perceptual robustness and reduces hallucination, offering a scalable approach for developing more reliable MLLMs.
本文针对多模态大语言模型在复杂视觉场景中因训练数据有限且扩展成本高昂而表现出的感知脆弱性问题，提出了大规模对抗数据集AOT-SFT和对抗对手训练框架AOT。该方法通过图像编辑攻击者与防御者模型之间的协同进化，使攻击者动态生成多样化的图像篡改以构建挑战性训练课程，从而迫使防御者不断适应与改进。大量实验表明，AOT能有效提升防御者的感知鲁棒性并减少幻觉，为训练更可靠的多模态大语言模型提供了一种可扩展的范式。
Selecting Offline Reinforcement Learning Algorithms for Stochastic Network Control
Authors: Nicolas Helson, Pegah Alizadeh, Anastasios Giovanidis
First: 2026-03-04T10:41:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T10:41:10+00:00
Comments: Long version 12 pages, double column including Appendix. Short version accepted at NOMS2026-IPSN, Rome, Italy
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline Reinforcement Learning (RL) is a promising approach for next-generation wireless networks, where online exploration is unsafe and large amounts of operational data can be reused across the model lifecycle. However, the behavior of offline RL algorithms under genuinely stochastic dynamics -- inherent to wireless systems due to fading, noise, and traffic mobility -- remains insufficiently understood. We address this gap by evaluating Bellman-based (Conservative Q-Learning), sequence-based (Decision Transformers), and hybrid (Critic-Guided Decision Transformers) offline RL methods in an open-access stochastic telecom environment (mobile-env). Our results show that Conservative Q-Learning consistently produces more robust policies across different sources of stochasticity, making it a reliable default choice in lifecycle-driven AI management frameworks. Sequence-based methods remain competitive and can outperform Bellman-based approaches when sufficient high-return trajectories are available. These findings provide practical guidance for offline RL algorithm selection in AI-driven network control pipelines, such as O-RAN and future 6G functions, where robustness and data availability are key operational constraints.
中文标题/摘要
标题：随机网络控制中离线强化学习算法的选择
离线强化学习是下一代无线网络的一种有前景的方法，其中在线探索不安全，且大量运营数据可在模型生命周期中重复使用。然而，在真实的随机动态环境下——由于衰落、噪声和流量移动性，这是无线系统固有的特性——离线强化学习算法的行为仍未得到充分理解。我们通过在开放访问的随机电信环境（mobile-env）中评估基于贝尔曼的（保守Q学习）、基于序列的（决策变换器）和混合（评论家引导决策变换器）离线强化学习方法来解决这一差距。我们的结果表明，保守Q学习在不同随机性来源下始终产生更稳健的策略，使其成为生命周期驱动的AI管理框架中可靠的默认选择。当有足够的高回报轨迹可用时，基于序列的方法仍具有竞争力，并能超越基于贝尔曼的方法。这些发现为AI驱动的网络控制管道（如O-RAN和未来6G功能）中的离线强化学习算法选择提供了实用指导，其中稳健性和数据可用性是关键的运营约束。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the need to understand how offline reinforcement learning algorithms perform under the genuinely stochastic dynamics inherent to wireless networks, such as fading and traffic mobility, where online exploration is unsafe. The authors evaluate three types of offline RL methods—Bellman-based (Conservative Q-Learning), sequence-based (Decision Transformers), and hybrid approaches—using an open-access stochastic telecom simulation environment. Their main experimental results show that Conservative Q-Learning consistently produces the most robust policies across different stochasticity sources, making it a reliable default choice, while sequence-based methods can outperform it when sufficient high-return trajectory data is available, offering practical guidance for algorithm selection in AI-driven network control systems like O-RAN and 6G.
本文旨在解决无线网络中固有的随机动态（如衰落和流量移动性）下离线强化学习算法的性能理解问题，因为在这些环境中在线探索是不安全的。作者使用一个开源的随机电信仿真环境，评估了三种离线强化学习方法：基于贝尔曼的（保守Q学习）、基于序列的（决策变换器）以及混合方法。主要实验结果表明，保守Q学习在不同随机性来源下始终能产生最稳健的策略，是可靠的默认选择；而当有足够的高回报轨迹数据时，基于序列的方法可以超越它，这为O-RAN和6G等人工智能驱动的网络控制系统中的算法选择提供了实用指导。
Joint Hardware-Workload Co-Optimization for In-Memory Computing Accelerators
Authors: Olga Krestinskaya, Mohammed E. Fouda, Ahmed Eltawil, Khaled N. Salama
First: 2026-03-04T09:32:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T09:32:06+00:00
Comments: Accepted to IEEE Access
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Software-hardware co-design is essential for optimizing in-memory computing (IMC) hardware accelerators for neural networks. However, most existing optimization frameworks target a single workload, leading to highly specialized hardware designs that do not generalize well across models and applications. In contrast, practical deployment scenarios require a single IMC platform that can efficiently support multiple neural network workloads. This work presents a joint hardware-workload co-optimization framework based on an optimized evolutionary algorithm for designing generalized IMC accelerator architectures. By explicitly capturing cross-workload trade-offs rather than optimizing for a single model, the proposed approach significantly reduces the performance gap between workload-specific and generalized IMC designs. The framework is evaluated on both RRAM- and SRAM-based IMC architectures, demonstrating strong robustness and adaptability across diverse design scenarios. Compared to baseline methods, the optimized designs achieve energy-delay-area product (EDAP) reductions of up to 76.2% and 95.5% when optimizing across a small set (4 workloads) and a large set (9 workloads), respectively. The source code of the framework is available at https://github.com/OlgaKrestinskaya/JointHardwareWorkloadOptimizationIMC.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向存内计算加速器的硬件-负载联合协同优化
软硬件协同设计对于优化面向神经网络的存内计算硬件加速器至关重要。然而，现有优化框架大多针对单一负载，导致硬件设计高度专用化，难以在不同模型与应用间泛化。实际部署场景则要求单一存内计算平台能高效支持多种神经网络负载。本研究提出一种基于优化进化算法的硬件-负载联合协同优化框架，用于设计通用化存内计算加速器架构。该方法通过显式捕获跨负载权衡而非针对单一模型优化，显著缩小了专用化与通用化存内计算设计间的性能差距。该框架在基于RRAM和SRAM的存内计算架构上均得到验证，展现出跨多样设计场景的强大鲁棒性与适应性。相较于基线方法，在小型负载集（4种负载）和大型负载集（9种负载）的优化中，所得设计分别实现了高达76.2%和95.5%的能耗-延迟-面积积降低。框架源代码发布于https://github.com/OlgaKrestinskaya/JointHardwareWorkloadOptimizationIMC。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for in-memory computing (IMC) accelerators that generalize across multiple neural network workloads rather than being specialized for a single model, this work introduces a joint hardware-workload co-optimization framework. The method employs an optimized evolutionary algorithm to design generalized IMC architectures by explicitly capturing cross-workload trade-offs. Experimental results on RRAM- and SRAM-based IMC platforms show the framework's robustness, achieving energy-delay-area product reductions of up to 76.2% for 4 workloads and 95.5% for 9 workloads compared to baselines.
本研究旨在解决存内计算加速器通常针对单一工作负载优化而泛化能力不足的问题，提出了一种联合硬件-工作负载协同优化框架。该方法采用优化的进化算法，通过显式捕获跨工作负载的权衡来设计通用加速器架构。在基于RRAM和SRAM的存内计算架构上的实验结果表明，该框架具有强鲁棒性和适应性，与基线方法相比，在优化4个和9个工作负载时，能量-延迟-面积积分别降低了76.2%和95.5%。
QFlowNet: Fast, Diverse, and Efficient Unitary Synthesis with Generative Flow Networks
Authors: Inhoe Koo, Hyunho Cha, Jungwoo Lee
First: 2026-03-03T14:38:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T09:29:40+00:00
Comments: 7 pages, 6 figures, IEEE International Conference on Quantum Communications, Networking, and Computing (QCNC 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unitary Synthesis, the decomposition of a unitary matrix into a sequence of quantum gates, is a fundamental challenge in quantum compilation. Prevailing reinforcement learning (RL) approaches are often hampered by sparse reward signals, which necessitate complex reward shaping or long training times, and typically converge to a single policy, lacking solution diversity. In this work, we propose QFlowNet, a novel framework that learns efficiently from sparse signals by pairing a Generative Flow Network (GFlowNet) with Transformers. Our approach addresses two key challenges. First, the GFlowNet framework is fundamentally designed to learn a diverse policy that samples solutions proportional to their reward, overcoming the single-solution limitation of RL while offering faster inference than other generative models like diffusion. Second, the Transformers act as a powerful encoder, capturing the non-local structure of unitary matrices and compressing a high-dimensional state into a dense latent representation for the policy network. Our agent achieves an overall success rate of 99.7% on a 3-qubit benchmark(lengths 1-12) and discovers a diverse set of compact circuits, establishing QFlowNet as an efficient and diverse paradigm for unitary synthesis.
中文标题/摘要
标题：QFlowNet：基于生成流网络实现快速、多样且高效的酉矩阵合成
酉矩阵合成——将酉矩阵分解为量子门序列——是量子编译领域的核心挑战。主流强化学习方法常受稀疏奖励信号制约，需复杂奖励塑形或长时训练，且通常收敛至单一策略，缺乏解多样性。本研究提出QFlowNet框架，通过将生成流网络与Transformer结合，实现从稀疏信号的高效学习。该方案解决两大关键问题：其一，生成流网络框架本质设计为学习按奖励比例采样解的多样化策略，克服强化学习的单解局限，同时比扩散模型等生成方法具有更快推理速度；其二，Transformer作为强大编码器，捕捉酉矩阵的非局部结构，将高维状态压缩为策略网络的稠密隐表示。智能体在3量子比特基准测试（长度1-12）中达成99.7%总成功率，并发现多样化紧凑电路，确立QFlowNet作为高效且多样化的酉矩阵合成范式。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces QFlowNet, a novel framework for unitary synthesis in quantum compilation, motivated by the limitations of existing reinforcement learning methods which suffer from sparse rewards, require extensive training, and lack solution diversity. The method pairs a Generative Flow Network (GFlowNet) with Transformers, where the GFlowNet enables efficient learning from sparse signals to sample diverse solutions proportional to reward, and Transformers encode the non-local structure of unitary matrices into dense latent representations. Experimental results show that QFlowNet achieves a 99.7% success rate on a 3-qubit benchmark with circuit lengths from 1 to 12, discovering a diverse set of compact circuits, thus establishing it as an efficient and diverse paradigm for unitary synthesis.

Generative Recommendation for Large-Scale Advertising
Authors: Ben Xue, Dan Liu, Lixiang Wang, Mingjie Sun, Peng Wang, Pengfei Zhang, Shaoyun Shi, Tianyu Xu, Yunhao Sha, Zhiqiang Liu, Bo Kong, Bo Wang, Hang Yang, Jieting Xue, Junhao Wang, Shengyu Wang, Shuping Hui, Wencai Ye, Xiao Lin, Yongzhi Li, Yuhang Chen, Zhihui Yin, Quan Chen, Shiyang Wen, Wenjin Wu, Han Li, Guorui Zhou, Changcheng Li, Peng Jiang
First: 2026-02-26T08:15:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T09:28:17+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 6 figures, under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative recommendation has recently attracted widespread attention in industry due to its potential for scaling and stronger model capacity. However, deploying real-time generative recommendation in large-scale advertising requires designs beyond large-language-model (LLM)-style training and serving recipes. We present a production-oriented generative recommender co-designed across architecture, learning, and serving, named GR4AD (Generative Recommendation for ADdvertising). As for tokenization, GR4AD proposes UA-SID (Unified Advertisement Semantic ID) to capture complicated business information. Furthermore, GR4AD introduces LazyAR, a lazy autoregressive decoder that relaxes layer-wise dependencies for short, multi-candidate generation, preserving effectiveness while reducing inference cost, which facilitates scaling under fixed serving budgets. To align optimization with business value, GR4AD employs VSL (Value-Aware Supervised Learning) and proposes RSPO (Ranking-Guided Softmax Preference Optimization), a ranking-aware, list-wise reinforcement learning algorithm that optimizes value-based rewards under list-level metrics for continual online updates. For online inference, we further propose dynamic beam serving, which adapts beam width across generation levels and online load to control compute. Large-scale online A/B tests show up to 4.2% ad revenue improvement over an existing DLRM-based stack, with consistent gains from both model scaling and inference-time scaling. GR4AD has been fully deployed in Kuaishou advertising system with over 400 million users and achieves high-throughput real-time serving.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向大规模广告的生成式推荐系统
生成式推荐因其可扩展性和更强的模型能力，近期在工业界受到广泛关注。然而，在大规模广告中部署实时生成式推荐需要超越大语言模型（LLM）式训练与服务方案的设计。我们提出了一种面向生产的生成式推荐系统GR4AD（面向广告的生成式推荐），其在架构、学习与服务层面进行了协同设计。在分词方面，GR4AD提出了UA-SID（统一广告语义ID）以捕捉复杂的业务信息。此外，GR4AD引入了LazyAR，一种惰性自回归解码器，通过放宽层间依赖关系来生成简短的多候选结果，在保持效果的同时降低推理成本，从而有助于在固定服务预算下实现扩展。为使优化与业务价值对齐，GR4AD采用VSL（价值感知监督学习）并提出了RSPO（排序引导的Softmax偏好优化），这是一种排序感知的列表式强化学习算法，可在列表级指标下优化基于价值的奖励，以支持持续在线更新。对于在线推理，我们进一步提出了动态束搜索服务，通过在不同生成层级和在线负载间自适应调整束宽来控制计算量。大规模在线A/B测试显示，相较于现有的基于DLRM的架构，广告收入提升最高达4.2%，模型扩展和推理时扩展均带来持续收益。GR4AD已在拥有超过4亿用户的快手广告系统中全面部署，实现了高吞吐的实时服务。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to deploy real-time generative recommendation in large-scale advertising beyond standard LLM approaches, this paper introduces GR4AD, a production-oriented system co-designed across architecture, learning, and serving. The method features a Unified Advertisement Semantic ID (UA-SID) for tokenization, a Lazy Autoregressive (LazyAR) decoder for efficient multi-candidate generation, and employs Value-Aware Supervised Learning (VSL) with a novel Ranking-Guided Softmax Preference Optimization (RSPO) algorithm for business-value alignment and online updates, complemented by dynamic beam serving for adaptive inference. Large-scale online A/B tests demonstrate up to a 4.2% improvement in ad revenue compared to a DLRM-based baseline, with gains from both model and inference scaling, and the system is fully deployed serving over 400 million users on Kuaishou's platform.
本文旨在解决大规模广告中实时生成式推荐部署的挑战，超越传统大语言模型方案，提出了一个面向生产的系统GR4AD，其在架构、学习和服务端协同设计。方法上，采用统一广告语义ID（UA-SID）进行分词，引入惰性自回归解码器（LazyAR）以实现高效的多候选生成，并利用价值感知监督学习（VSL）和新型排序引导的Softmax偏好优化（RSPO）算法来对齐业务价值与在线更新，辅以动态束搜索服务进行自适应推理。大规模在线A/B测试显示，相比基于DLRM的现有系统，广告收入提升最高达4.2%，收益来自模型和推理扩展，该系统已在快手广告平台全面部署，服务超4亿用户。
Fairness Begins with State: Purifying Latent Preferences for Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning in Interactive Recommendation
Authors: Yun Lu, Xiaoyu Shi, Hong Xie, Xiangyu Zhao, Mingsheng Shang
First: 2026-03-04T08:14:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T08:14:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Interactive recommender systems (IRS) are increasingly optimized with Reinforcement Learning (RL) to capture the sequential nature of user-system dynamics. However, existing fairness-aware methods often suffer from a fundamental oversight: they assume the observed user state is a faithful representation of true preferences. In reality, implicit feedback is contaminated by popularity-driven noise and exposure bias, creating a distorted state that misleads the RL agent. We argue that the persistent conflict between accuracy and fairness is not merely a reward-shaping issue, but a state estimation failure. In this work, we propose \textbf{DSRM-HRL}, a framework that reformulates fairness-aware recommendation as a latent state purification problem followed by decoupled hierarchical decision-making. We introduce a Denoising State Representation Module (DSRM) based on diffusion models to recover the low-entropy latent preference manifold from high-entropy, noisy interaction histories. Built upon this purified state, a Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning (HRL) agent is employed to decouple conflicting objectives: a high-level policy regulates long-term fairness trajectories, while a low-level policy optimizes short-term engagement under these dynamic constraints. Extensive experiments on high-fidelity simulators (KuaiRec, KuaiRand) demonstrate that DSRM-HRL effectively breaks the "rich-get-richer" feedback loop, achieving a superior Pareto frontier between recommendation utility and exposure equity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：公平始于状态：交互推荐中层次强化学习的潜在偏好净化
交互式推荐系统（IRS）日益采用强化学习（RL）进行优化，以捕捉用户-系统交互的序列特性。然而，现有公平性方法常存在根本性疏漏：假定观测到的用户状态能忠实反映真实偏好。现实中，隐式反馈受流行度噪声和曝光偏差污染，形成误导RL智能体的失真状态。我们认为，准确性与公平性间的持续冲突不仅是奖励塑造问题，更是状态估计失效。本文提出\textbf{DSRM-HRL}框架，将公平感知推荐重构为潜在状态净化问题，继而进行解耦的层次化决策。我们引入基于扩散模型的去噪状态表示模块（DSRM），从高熵噪声交互历史中恢复低熵潜在偏好流形。在此净化状态基础上，采用层次强化学习（HRL）智能体解耦冲突目标：高层策略调控长期公平轨迹，低层策略在动态约束下优化短期参与度。在高保真模拟器（KuaiRec、KuaiRand）上的大量实验表明，DSRM-HRL能有效打破“富者愈富”反馈循环，在推荐效用与曝光公平性间实现更优的帕累托前沿。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the persistent accuracy-fairness trade-off in interactive recommender systems by arguing that the conflict stems from state estimation failure, not just reward shaping, as observed user states are contaminated by popularity bias and noise. The proposed DSRM-HRL framework first purifies latent user preferences using a Denoising State Representation Module based on diffusion models to recover a low-entropy preference manifold from noisy interactions, then employs a hierarchical RL agent where a high-level policy manages long-term fairness trajectories and a low-level policy optimizes short-term engagement under those constraints. Experiments on KuaiRec and KuaiRand simulators show the method effectively breaks the "rich-get-richer" feedback loop, achieving a superior Pareto frontier between recommendation utility and exposure equity.
本文针对交互式推荐系统中长期存在的准确性与公平性权衡问题，提出冲突根源在于状态估计失败而非仅奖励塑造，因为观测到的用户状态受流行度偏差和噪声污染。所提出的DSRM-HRL框架首先基于扩散模型去噪状态表示模块，从噪声交互中恢复低熵潜在偏好流形以净化用户偏好，随后采用分层强化学习代理，其中高层策略管理长期公平轨迹，低层策略在这些动态约束下优化短期参与度。在KuaiRec和KuaiRand模拟器上的实验表明，该方法有效打破了“富者愈富”的反馈循环，在推荐效用和曝光公平性之间实现了更优的帕累托前沿。
When Silence Is Golden: Can LLMs Learn to Abstain in Temporal QA and Beyond?
Authors: Xinyu Zhou, Chang Jin, Carsten Eickhoff, Zhijiang Guo, Seyed Ali Bahrainian
First: 2026-02-04T16:54:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T06:39:07+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) rarely admit uncertainty, often producing fluent but misleading answers, rather than abstaining (i.e., refusing to answer). This weakness is even evident in temporal question answering, where models frequently ignore time-sensitive evidence and conflate facts across different time-periods. In this paper, we present the first empirical study of training LLMs with an abstention ability while reasoning about temporal QA. Existing approaches such as calibration might be unreliable in capturing uncertainty in complex reasoning. We instead frame abstention as a teachable skill and introduce a pipeline that couples Chain-of-Thought (CoT) supervision with Reinforcement Learning (RL) guided by abstention-aware rewards. Our goal is to systematically analyze how different information types and training techniques affect temporal reasoning with abstention behavior in LLMs. Through extensive experiments studying various methods, we find that RL yields strong empirical gains on reasoning: a model initialized by Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct surpasses GPT-4o by $3.46\%$ and $5.80\%$ in Exact Match on TimeQA-Easy and Hard, respectively. Moreover, it improves the True Positive rate on unanswerable questions by $20\%$ over a pure supervised fine-tuned (SFT) variant. Beyond performance, our analysis shows that SFT induces overconfidence and harms reliability, while RL improves prediction accuracy but exhibits similar risks. Finally, by comparing implicit reasoning cues (e.g., original context, temporal sub-context, knowledge graphs) with explicit CoT supervision, we find that implicit information provides limited benefit for reasoning with abstention. Our study provides new insights into how abstention and reasoning can be jointly optimized, providing a foundation for building more reliable LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：沉默是金：大语言模型能否在时序问答及其他任务中学会弃答？
大语言模型（LLMs）很少承认不确定性，常生成流畅但具有误导性的答案，而非选择弃答（即拒绝回答）。这一缺陷在时序问答中尤为明显，模型常忽略时效性证据并混淆不同时期的事实。本文首次实证研究了在时序问答推理中训练LLMs弃答能力的方法。现有方法（如校准）在捕捉复杂推理中的不确定性时可能不可靠。我们将弃答构建为可教授的技能，提出一种结合思维链监督与弃答感知奖励强化学习的训练框架。目标是系统分析不同信息类型和训练技术如何影响LLMs的时序推理与弃答行为。通过大量实验发现：强化学习显著提升推理性能——基于Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct初始化的模型在TimeQA-Easy和Hard数据集上的精确匹配率分别超越GPT-4o达3.46%和5.80%；对不可答问题的真阳性率较纯监督微调模型提升20%。分析表明：监督微调会引发过度自信损害可靠性，强化学习虽提升预测精度但存在类似风险。通过对比隐式推理线索（原始上下文、时序子语境、知识图谱）与显式思维链监督，发现隐式信息对弃答推理的助益有限。本研究为联合优化弃答与推理提供了新见解，为构建更可靠的LLMs奠定基础。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the problem that large language models (LLMs) often produce confidently wrong answers instead of abstaining when uncertain, particularly in temporal question answering where they conflate facts across different time periods. The authors frame abstention as a teachable skill and introduce a training pipeline that combines Chain-of-Thought supervision with Reinforcement Learning using abstention-aware rewards to jointly optimize reasoning and abstention behavior. Experimental results show that their RL-trained model, based on Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct, outperforms GPT-4o on TimeQA benchmarks and improves the true positive rate on unanswerable questions by 20% compared to a supervised fine-tuning baseline, though analysis reveals that both SFT and RL can induce overconfidence, and implicit reasoning cues provide limited benefit for abstention.
本文针对大语言模型在不确定时经常产生自信但错误的答案而非选择弃答的问题展开研究，特别是在时序问答中，模型容易混淆不同时期的事实。作者将弃答能力构建为一种可学习的技能，提出了一种结合思维链监督与基于弃答感知奖励的强化学习的训练框架，以联合优化推理和弃答行为。实验结果表明，基于Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct的强化学习模型在TimeQA基准上超越了GPT-4o，并在不可回答问题上的真阳性率比纯监督微调基线提高了20%，但分析也表明监督微调和强化学习都可能引发过度自信，且隐式推理线索对弃答的帮助有限。
Learning Approximate Nash Equilibria in Cooperative Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning via Mean-Field Subsampling
Authors: Emile Anand, Ishani Karmarkar
First: 2026-03-04T06:14:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T06:14:24+00:00
Comments: 48 pages, 4 figures, 2 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many large-scale platforms and networked control systems have a centralized decision maker interacting with a massive population of agents under strict observability constraints. Motivated by such applications, we study a cooperative Markov game with a global agent and $n$ homogeneous local agents in a communication-constrained regime, where the global agent only observes a subset of $k$ local agent states per time step. We propose an alternating learning framework $(\texttt{ALTERNATING-MARL})$, where the global agent performs subsampled mean-field $Q$-learning against a fixed local policy, and local agents update by optimizing in an induced MDP. We prove that these approximate best-response dynamics converge to an $\widetilde{O}(1/\sqrt{k})$-approximate Nash Equilibrium, while yielding a separation in the sample complexities between the joint state space and action space. Finally, we validate our results in numerical simulations for multi-robot control and federated optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过均值场子采样在合作多智能体强化学习中学习近似纳什均衡
许多大规模平台和网络控制系统存在集中决策者与海量智能体在严格可观测性约束下交互的场景。受此类应用驱动，本研究在通信受限机制下探讨包含全局智能体与$n$个同质局部智能体的合作马尔可夫博弈，其中全局智能体每时间步仅能观测$k$个局部智能体状态的子集。我们提出交替学习框架$(\texttt{ALTERNATING-MARL})$：全局智能体针对固定局部策略执行子采样均值场$Q$学习，局部智能体通过在诱导MDP中优化进行更新。理论证明该近似最优响应动态可收敛至$\widetilde{O}(1/\sqrt{k})$近似纳什均衡，同时在联合状态空间与动作空间之间产生样本复杂度分离。最后通过多机器人控制与联邦优化的数值仿真验证了理论结果。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by large-scale systems with centralized control and limited observability, this paper studies cooperative Markov games where a global agent can only observe a subset of local agents. The method introduces ALTERNATING-MARL, an alternating learning framework where the global agent performs subsampled mean-field Q-learning against a fixed local policy, and local agents optimize within an induced Markov Decision Process. The main experimental results prove that this approach converges to an approximate Nash equilibrium with an error bound scaling as the inverse square root of the observation subset size, and numerical simulations in multi-robot control and federated optimization validate the theoretical findings, demonstrating a separation in sample complexity between joint state and action spaces.
本文的动机源于具有集中控制但可观测性受限的大规模系统，研究了一个全局智能体仅能观测部分局部智能体状态的合作马尔可夫博弈。方法上提出了ALTERNATING-MARL交替学习框架，其中全局智能体对固定局部策略执行子采样均值场Q学习，而局部智能体则在诱导的马尔可夫决策过程中进行优化。主要实验结果证明该方法能收敛到一个近似纳什均衡，其误差界与观测子集大小的平方根倒数相关，并在多机器人控制和联邦优化的数值模拟中验证了理论结果，显示了联合状态空间与动作空间在样本复杂度上的分离。
Confidence-Calibrated Small-Large Language Model Collaboration for Cost-Efficient Reasoning
Authors: Chuang Zhang, Zizhen Zhu, Yihao Wei, Bing Tian, Junyi Liu, Henan Wang, Xavier Wang, Yaxiao Liu
First: 2026-03-04T05:55:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T05:55:20+00:00
Comments: Accepted to EACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) demonstrate superior reasoning capabilities compared to small language models (SLMs), but incur substantially higher costs. We propose COllaborative REAsoner (COREA), a system that cascades an SLM with an LLM to achieve a balance between accuracy and cost in complex reasoning tasks. COREA first attempts to answer questions using the SLM, which outputs both an answer and a verbalized confidence score. Questions with confidence below a predefined threshold are deferred to the LLM for more accurate resolution. We introduce a reinforcement learning-based training algorithm that aligns the SLM's confidence through an additional confidence calibration reward. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method jointly improves the SLM's reasoning ability and confidence calibration across diverse datasets and model backbones. Compared to using the LLM alone, COREA reduces cost by 21.5% and 16.8% on out-of-domain math and non-math datasets, respectively, with only an absolute pass@1 drop within 2%.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于置信度校准的大小语言模型协作实现高性价比推理
大语言模型（LLM）相比小语言模型（SLM）具有更优的推理能力，但成本显著更高。我们提出协作推理器（COREA），该系统通过级联SLM与LLM，在复杂推理任务中实现准确性与成本的平衡。COREA首先尝试用SLM回答问题，SLM会同时输出答案和语言化置信度分数。置信度低于预设阈值的问题将交由LLM进行更精确求解。我们引入基于强化学习的训练算法，通过额外的置信度校准奖励来对齐SLM的置信度。大量实验表明，该方法能协同提升SLM在不同数据集和模型架构下的推理能力与置信度校准效果。与单独使用LLM相比，COREA在域外数学和非数学数据集上分别降低21.5%和16.8%的成本，而绝对pass@1指标下降幅度控制在2%以内。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high cost of large language models (LLMs) despite their strong reasoning, this paper introduces COREA, a collaborative system that cascades a small language model (SLM) with an LLM to balance accuracy and expense. The method first uses the SLM to answer questions and provide a verbalized confidence score; questions with low confidence are deferred to the LLM, and a reinforcement learning algorithm aligns the SLM's confidence via a calibration reward. Experimental results show the approach improves the SLM's reasoning and calibration across datasets, reducing costs by 21.5% and 16.8% on out-of-domain math and non-math tasks with minimal accuracy loss.
本文的动机在于大型语言模型（LLM）虽然推理能力强但成本高昂，因此提出了COREA系统，通过级联小型语言模型（SLM）和LLM来平衡准确性与开销。方法首先使用SLM回答问题并输出言语化的置信度分数，置信度低于阈值的问题则交由LLM处理，并采用基于强化学习的训练算法通过置信度校准奖励来对齐SLM的置信度。实验结果表明，该方法在不同数据集和模型骨干上提升了SLM的推理能力和置信度校准，在域外数学和非数学数据集上分别降低了21.5%和16.8%的成本，且准确率下降幅度很小。
Interaction-Aware Whole-Body Control for Compliant Object Transport
Authors: Hao Zhang, Yves Tseng, Ding Zhao, H. Eric Tseng
First: 2026-03-04T05:50:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T05:50:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Cooperative object transport in unstructured environments remains challenging for assistive humanoids because strong, time-varying interaction forces can make tracking-centric whole-body control unreliable, especially in close-contact support tasks. This paper proposes a bio-inspired, interaction-oriented whole-body control (IO-WBC) that functions as an artificial cerebellum - an adaptive motor agent that translates upstream (skill-level) commands into stable, physically consistent whole-body behavior under contact. This work structurally separates upper-body interaction execution from lower-body support control, enabling the robot to maintain balance while shaping force exchange in a tightly coupled robot-object system. A trajectory-optimized reference generator (RG) provides a kinematic prior, while a reinforcement learning (RL) policy governs body responses under heavy-load interactions and disturbances. The policy is trained in simulation with randomized payload mass/inertia and external perturbations, and deployed via asymmetric teacher-student distillation so that the student relies only on proprioceptive histories at runtime. Extensive experiments demonstrate that IO-WBC maintains stable whole-body behavior and physical interaction even when precise velocity tracking becomes infeasible, enabling compliant object transport across a wide range of scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向顺应性物体搬运的交互感知全身控制
非结构化环境中的协作物体搬运对辅助人形机器人仍具挑战性，因为强烈且时变的交互力会使以轨迹跟踪为核心的全身控制变得不可靠，尤其在紧密接触的支撑任务中。本文提出一种受生物启发的、面向交互的全身控制方法，其功能类似于人工小脑——一个能将上游技能级指令转化为接触条件下稳定、物理一致的全身行为的自适应运动代理。该工作在结构上将上半身交互执行与下半身支撑控制分离，使机器人在紧密耦合的机器人-物体系统中保持平衡的同时调控力交换。轨迹优化的参考生成器提供运动学先验，而强化学习策略则负责管理重载交互和扰动下的身体响应。该策略在仿真环境中通过随机化负载质量/惯性和外部扰动进行训练，并通过非对称师生蒸馏进行部署，使学生策略在运行时仅依赖本体感知历史数据。大量实验表明，即使在精确速度跟踪不可行的情况下，该方法仍能维持稳定的全身行为与物理交互，实现广泛场景下的顺应性物体搬运。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of reliable whole-body control for humanoid robots during compliant object transport, where strong interaction forces can destabilize traditional tracking-based controllers. The authors propose an interaction-oriented whole-body control (IO-WBC) framework inspired by biological motor control, which structurally separates upper-body interaction execution from lower-body support to maintain balance while managing force exchange. A trajectory-optimized reference generator provides kinematic guidance, while a reinforcement learning policy trained in simulation with randomized payloads and disturbances handles body responses, deployed via teacher-student distillation for runtime efficiency. Experimental results show that IO-WBC maintains stable whole-body behavior and physical interaction even when precise velocity tracking is infeasible, enabling robust transport across diverse scenarios.
本文针对人形机器人在柔顺物体搬运过程中，强交互力易导致传统基于跟踪的全身控制失稳的挑战，提出了一种受生物运动控制启发的交互导向全身控制框架。该方法在结构上将上半身的交互执行与下半身的支撑控制分离，以在管理力交换的同时保持平衡；轨迹优化的参考生成器提供运动学先验，而通过模拟中随机化负载与扰动训练的强化学习策略则处理身体响应，并借助师生蒸馏部署以实现运行时高效性。实验结果表明，即使在精确速度跟踪不可行时，该控制框架也能维持稳定的全身行为与物理交互，从而在各种场景下实现鲁棒的物体搬运。
HALyPO: Heterogeneous-Agent Lyapunov Policy Optimization for Human-Robot Collaboration
Authors: Hao Zhang, Yaru Niu, Yikai Wang, Ding Zhao, H. Eric Tseng
First: 2026-03-04T05:26:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T05:26:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
To improve generalization and resilience in human-robot collaboration (HRC), robots must handle the combinatorial diversity of human behaviors and contexts, motivating multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL). However, inherent heterogeneity between robots and humans creates a rationality gap (RG) in the learning process-a variational mismatch between decentralized best-response dynamics and centralized cooperative ascent. The resulting learning problem is a general-sum differentiable game, so independent policy-gradient updates can oscillate or diverge without added structure. We propose heterogeneous-agent Lyapunov policy optimization (HALyPO), which establishes formal stability directly in the policy-parameter space by enforcing a per-step Lyapunov decrease condition on a parameter-space disagreement metric. Unlike Lyapunov-based safe RL, which targets state/trajectory constraints in constrained Markov decision processes, HALyPO uses Lyapunov certification to stabilize decentralized policy learning. HALyPO rectifies decentralized gradients via optimal quadratic projections, ensuring monotonic contraction of RG and enabling effective exploration of open-ended interaction spaces. Extensive simulations and real-world humanoid-robot experiments show that this certified stability improves generalization and robustness in collaborative corner cases.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HALyPO：面向人机协作的异构智能体李雅普诺夫策略优化
为提升人机协作的泛化性与鲁棒性，机器人需应对人类行为与情境的组合多样性，这推动了多智能体强化学习的应用。然而，机器人与人类间的内在异质性会在学习过程中产生理性鸿沟——即分散式最优响应动态与集中式协同上升间的变分失配。该学习问题本质上是广义和可微博弈，若无额外结构约束，独立策略梯度更新易出现振荡或发散。本文提出异构智能体李雅普诺夫策略优化方法，通过在参数空间分歧度量上强制实施步进式李雅普诺夫递减条件，直接在策略参数空间建立形式化稳定性。与基于李雅普诺夫的安全强化学习（针对约束马尔可夫决策过程的状态/轨迹约束）不同，HALyPO运用李雅普诺夫证明来稳定分散式策略学习。该方法通过最优二次投影修正分散式梯度，确保理性鸿沟的单调收缩，并支持对开放式交互空间的有效探索。大量仿真与真实人形机器人实验表明，这种经证明的稳定性显著提升了协作边缘场景中的泛化能力与鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need for robots to generalize and remain resilient in human-robot collaboration despite the diversity of human behaviors, which leads to a rationality gap in multi-agent reinforcement learning due to heterogeneity between agents. The method, Heterogeneous-Agent Lyapunov Policy Optimization (HALyPO), addresses this by enforcing a Lyapunov decrease condition on a parameter-space disagreement metric to stabilize decentralized policy learning, using optimal quadratic projections to rectify gradients and ensure monotonic contraction of the rationality gap. Experimental results from simulations and real-world humanoid-robot tests demonstrate that this certified stability enhances generalization and robustness in challenging collaborative scenarios.
本文的动机是，尽管人类行为具有多样性，机器人仍需在人机协作中实现泛化与鲁棒性，这因智能体间的异质性导致多智能体强化学习中出现理性差距。所提出的方法——异构智能体李雅普诺夫策略优化（HALyPO），通过在参数空间的不一致度量上强制李雅普诺夫递减条件来稳定分散策略学习，并利用最优二次投影修正梯度以确保理性差距的单调收缩。仿真和真实人形机器人实验结果表明，这种经认证的稳定性在具有挑战性的协作场景中提高了泛化能力和鲁棒性。
AutoQD: Automatic Discovery of Diverse Behaviors with Quality-Diversity Optimization
Authors: Saeed Hedayatian, Stefanos Nikolaidis
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-06-05T23:34:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T05:24:53+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Quality-Diversity (QD) algorithms have shown remarkable success in discovering diverse, high-performing solutions, but rely heavily on hand-crafted behavioral descriptors that constrain exploration to predefined notions of diversity. Leveraging the equivalence between policies and occupancy measures, we present a theoretically grounded approach to automatically generate behavioral descriptors by embedding the occupancy measures of policies in Markov Decision Processes. Our method, AutoQD, leverages random Fourier features to approximate the Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD) between policy occupancy measures, creating embeddings whose distances reflect meaningful behavioral differences. A low-dimensional projection of these embeddings that captures the most behaviorally significant dimensions can then be used as behavioral descriptors for CMA-MAE, a state of the art blackbox QD method, to discover diverse policies. We prove that our embeddings converge to true MMD distances between occupancy measures as the number of sampled trajectories and embedding dimensions increase. Through experiments in multiple continuous control tasks we demonstrate AutoQD's ability in discovering diverse policies without predefined behavioral descriptors, presenting a well-motivated alternative to prior methods in unsupervised Reinforcement Learning and QD optimization. Our approach opens new possibilities for open-ended learning and automated behavior discovery in sequential decision making settings without requiring domain-specific knowledge. Source code is available at https://github.com/conflictednerd/autoqd-code.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AutoQD：基于质量多样性优化的多样化行为自动发现方法
质量多样性算法在发现多样化高性能解决方案方面成效显著，但其严重依赖人工设计的行为描述符，将探索范围限制在预设的多样性概念中。基于策略与占用测度的等价性，我们提出一种理论完备的方法，通过嵌入马尔可夫决策过程中策略的占用测度来自动生成行为描述符。我们的方法AutoQD利用随机傅里叶特征逼近策略占用测度间的最大均值差异，构建能反映行为差异的嵌入表示。通过提取最具行为区分度的低维投影作为行为描述符，可将其应用于前沿黑箱质量多样性方法CMA-MAE，从而发现多样化策略。我们证明随着轨迹采样数与嵌入维度的增加，该嵌入表示将收敛至占用测度的真实最大均值差异距离。在多个连续控制任务中的实验表明，AutoQD无需预定义行为描述符即可发现多样化策略，为无监督强化学习与质量多样性优化提供了理论完备的替代方案。该方法为序列决策场景中的开放式学习与自动化行为发现开辟了新路径，且无需领域先验知识。源代码发布于https://github.com/conflictednerd/autoqd-code。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of Quality-Diversity (QD) algorithms, which depend on hand-crafted behavioral descriptors that restrict exploration to predefined diversity notions. The method, AutoQD, automatically generates behavioral descriptors by embedding policy occupancy measures in Markov Decision Processes using random Fourier features to approximate Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD), creating embeddings where distances reflect meaningful behavioral differences; these are then projected into a low-dimensional space for use with the CMA-MAE QD algorithm. Experimental results in continuous control tasks demonstrate AutoQD's ability to discover diverse policies without predefined descriptors, offering a theoretically grounded alternative for unsupervised reinforcement learning and QD optimization, thereby enabling open-ended learning without domain-specific knowledge.
本文针对质量多样性（QD）算法依赖手工设计行为描述符、限制探索预定义多样性概念的局限性，提出了一种自动生成行为描述符的方法。该方法名为AutoQD，通过嵌入马尔可夫决策过程中策略的占用测度，利用随机傅里叶特征近似最大均值差异（MMD），创建能反映行为差异的嵌入表示，并将其投影到低维空间以用于CMA-MAE QD算法。在连续控制任务中的实验结果表明，AutoQD能够在无需预定义描述符的情况下发现多样化策略，为无监督强化学习和QD优化提供了理论依据充分的替代方案，从而实现了无需领域知识的开放式学习。
SHE: Stepwise Hybrid Examination Reinforcement Learning Framework for E-commerce Search Relevance
Authors: Pengkun Jiao, Yiming Jin, Jianhui Yang, Chenhe Dong, Zerui Huang, Shaowei Yao, Xiaojiang Zhou, Dan Ou, Haihong Tang
First: 2025-10-09T09:03:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T05:15:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Query-product relevance prediction is a foundational technology in e-commerce search engines and has become increasingly important in AI-driven e-commerce. The recent emergence of LLMs, particularly their CoT reasoning capabilities, offers promising opportunities for developing relevance systems that are both more interpretable and more robust. However, existing training paradigms have notable limitations: SFT and DPO suffer from poor generalization on long-tail queries and from a lack of fine-grained, stepwise supervision to enforce rule-aligned reasoning. In contrast, reinforcement learning with verification rewards (RLVR) suffers from sparse feedback, which provides insufficient signal to correct erroneous intermediate steps, thereby undermining logical consistency and limiting performance in complex inference scenarios. To address these challenges, we introduce the Stepwise Hybrid Examination Reinforcement Learning framework for search relevance (SHE). At its core is Stepwise Reward Policy Optimization (SRPO), a reinforcement learning algorithm that leverages step-level rewards generated by a hybrid of a high-quality generative stepwise reward model and a human-annotated offline verifier, prioritizing learning from critical correct and incorrect reasoning steps. To bolster robustness and generalization, SHE further integrates a dual-strategy optimization: diversified data filtering, which broadens the exploration of reasoning trajectories to preempt policy entropy collapse, and a multi-stage curriculum learning protocol that systematically orchestrates progressive capability acquisition. Extensive experiments on real-world search benchmarks show that SHE improves both reasoning quality and relevance-prediction accuracy in large-scale e-commerce settings, outperforming SFT, DPO, GRPO, and other baselines, while also enhancing interpretability and robustness.

标题：SHE：面向电商搜索相关性的渐进式混合检验强化学习框架
查询-商品相关性预测是电商搜索引擎的基础技术，在AI驱动的电商领域日益重要。近期大语言模型（LLM）的出现，特别是其思维链推理能力，为开发兼具更强可解释性与鲁棒性的相关性系统提供了新机遇。然而，现有训练范式存在明显局限：监督微调（SFT）和直接偏好优化（DPO）对长尾查询泛化能力不足，且缺乏细粒度、渐进式的监督来确保规则对齐的推理；而基于验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）则受限于稀疏反馈，难以纠正错误中间步骤，损害逻辑一致性并限制复杂推理场景的性能。为应对这些挑战，我们提出面向搜索相关性的渐进式混合检验强化学习框架（SHE）。其核心是渐进式奖励策略优化算法（SRPO），该强化学习算法融合高质量生成式渐进奖励模型与人工标注离线验证器产生的步骤级奖励，优先从关键正误推理步骤中学习。为增强鲁棒性与泛化能力，SHE进一步集成双策略优化：多样化数据过滤通过扩展推理轨迹探索防止策略熵崩溃，多阶段课程学习协议系统化协调渐进能力习得。在真实搜索基准上的大量实验表明，SHE在大规模电商场景中同步提升推理质量与相关性预测准确率，优于SFT、DPO、GRPO等基线方法，同时增强可解释性与鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing training paradigms like SFT, DPO, and RLVR for query-product relevance prediction—which suffer from poor generalization, lack of stepwise supervision, and sparse feedback—this paper introduces the Stepwise Hybrid Examination Reinforcement Learning framework (SHE). The method centers on Stepwise Reward Policy Optimization (SRPO), which uses step-level rewards from a hybrid generative model and human-annotated verifier to prioritize critical reasoning steps, combined with diversified data filtering and multi-stage curriculum learning for robustness. Experimental results on real-world e-commerce benchmarks demonstrate that SHE outperforms SFT, DPO, GRPO, and other baselines in both reasoning quality and relevance-prediction accuracy, while also improving interpretability and robustness.

OASI: Objective-Aware Surrogate Initialization for Multi-Objective Bayesian Optimization in TinyML Keyword Spotting
Authors: Soumen Garai, Danilo Pau, Suman Samui
First: 2025-12-17T17:32:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T04:50:18+00:00
Comments: Updated version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Voice-triggered interfaces rely on keyword spotting (KWS) models that must operate continuously under strict memory, latency, and energy constraints on microcontroller-class hardware. Designing such models therefore requires not only high recognition accuracy but also predictable deployability within limited Flash and SRAM budgets. Bayesian optimization is known to handle accuracy-efficiency trade-offs effectively in multi-objective optimization; however, it is highly sensitive to initialization, particularly in the low-budget regimes of TinyML model optimization. We propose Objective-Aware Surrogate Initialization (OASI), which seeds surrogate optimization with Pareto-biased solutions generated via multi-objective simulated annealing. Unlike space-filling or heuristic warm-start methods, OASI initializes the surrogate conditioning process with a bias toward feasible accuracy-memory trade-offs, thus avoiding SRAM-violating configurations. OASI improves hypervolume and convergence robustness over Latin hypercube, Sobol, and random initializations under the same budget constraints on a TinyML KWS problem. Hardware-in-the-loop experiments on STM32 microcontrollers verify the existence of deployable and memory-feasible models without incurring extra optimization costs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OASI：面向TinyML关键词检测中多目标贝叶斯优化的目标感知代理初始化方法
语音触发接口依赖关键词检测模型，此类模型必须在微控制器级硬件的严格内存、延迟和能耗约束下持续运行。因此设计这类模型不仅需要高识别准确率，还需确保在有限的Flash和SRAM资源内可部署。贝叶斯优化虽能有效处理多目标优化中的精度-效率权衡，但其对初始化极为敏感，在TinyML模型优化的低预算场景中尤为突出。本文提出目标感知代理初始化方法，通过多目标模拟退火生成的帕累托偏置解来初始化代理优化。与空间填充或启发式热启动方法不同，OASI使代理条件化过程初始偏向可行的精度-内存权衡，从而避免违反SRAM约束的配置。在相同预算约束下，OASI在TinyML关键词检测问题上相比拉丁超立方、Sobol序列及随机初始化，显著提升了超体积指标与收敛鲁棒性。基于STM32微控制器的硬件在环实验证实，该方法可在不增加优化成本的前提下获得可部署且内存可行的模型。

Subsampling Factorization Machine Annealing
Authors: Yusuke Hama, Tadashi Kadowaki
Venue: Phys. Rev. Research 8, 013187 (2026)
First: 2025-08-12T09:25:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T04:09:43+00:00
Comments: 29 pages and 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Quantum computing and machine learning are state-of-the-art technologies that have been investigated intensively in both academia and industry. The hybrid technology of these two ingredients is expected to be a powerful tool to solve complex problems in many branches of science and engineering such as combinatorial optimization problems and accelerate the creation of next-generation technologies. In this work, we develop an algorithm to solve a black-box optimization problem by improving Factorization Machine Annealing (FMA) such that the training of a machine learning model called Factorization Machine is performed not by a full dataset but by a subdataset that is sampled from a full dataset: Subsampling Factorization Machine Annealing (SFMA). According to such a probabilistic training process, the performance of FMA on exploring a solution space gets enhanced. As a result, SFMA exhibits balanced performance of exploration and exploitation, which we call exploitation-exploration functionality. We conduct numerical benchmarking tests to compare the performance of SFMA with that of FMA. Consequently, SFMA certainly exhibits the exploration-exploitation functionality and outperforms FMA in speed and accuracy. In addition, the performance of SFMA can be further improved by sequentially using two subsampling datasets with different sizes such that the size of the latter dataset is substantially smaller than the former. Such a substantial reduction not only enhances the exploration performance of SFMA but also enables us to run it with correspondingly low computational cost even for a large-scale problem. These results indicate the effectiveness of SFMA in a certain class of black-box optimization problems of significant size: the potential scalability of SFMA in solving large-scale problems with correspondingly low computational cost.
中文标题/摘要
标题：子采样因子分解机退火算法
量子计算与机器学习是学术界和工业界广泛研究的前沿技术。两者的融合技术有望成为解决组合优化等科学与工程领域复杂问题的强大工具，并推动下一代技术的快速发展。本研究通过改进因子分解机退火算法，提出一种黑盒优化算法：子采样因子分解机退火算法。该算法采用从全数据集中采样的子数据集训练因子分解机模型，而非使用完整数据集。这种概率化训练过程增强了算法在解空间的探索性能，实现了探索与利用的平衡，即“利用-探索功能”。数值基准测试表明，SFMA在速度与精度上均优于FMA，并展现出明确的探索-利用功能。此外，通过先后使用两个规模递减的子数据集（后者规模显著小于前者），可进一步提升SFMA性能。这种大幅度的规模缩减不仅增强了探索能力，还能以较低计算成本处理大规模问题。这些结果证明了SFMA在特定类别大规模黑盒优化问题中的有效性，以及其在保持低计算成本前提下解决大规模问题的潜在可扩展性。

Motivated by the need to enhance the efficiency of quantum-inspired machine learning for large-scale black-box optimization, this paper introduces Subsampling Factorization Machine Annealing (SFMA), an improved variant of Factorization Machine Annealing (FMA) that trains the Factorization Machine model using probabilistically sampled subsets of data rather than the full dataset. UrbanHuRo: A Two-Layer Human-Robot Collaboration Framework for the Joint Optimization of Heterogeneous Urban Services
Authors: Tonmoy Dey, Lin Jiang, Zheng Dong, Guang Wang
Venue: ICRA
First: 2026-03-04T04:02:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T04:02:28+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 15 figures. This paper has been accepted by ICRA'26 as a regular paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In the vision of smart cities, technologies are being developed to enhance the efficiency of urban services and improve residents' quality of life. However, most existing research focuses on optimizing individual services in isolation, without adequately considering reciprocal interactions among heterogeneous urban services that could yield higher efficiency and improved resource utilization. For example, human couriers could collect traffic and air quality data along their delivery routes, while sensing robots could assist with on-demand delivery during peak hours, enhancing both sensing coverage and delivery efficiency. However, the joint optimization of different urban services is challenging due to potentially conflicting objectives and the need for real-time coordination in dynamic environments. In this paper, we propose UrbanHuRo, a two-layer human-robot collaboration framework for joint optimization of heterogeneous urban services, demonstrated through crowdsourced delivery and urban sensing. UrbanHuRo includes two key designs: (i) a scalable distributed MapReduce-based K-submodular maximization module for efficient order dispatch, and (ii) a deep submodular reward reinforcement learning algorithm for sensing route planning. Experimental evaluations on real-world datasets from a food delivery platform demonstrate that UrbanHuRo improves sensing coverage by 29.7% and courier income by 39.2% on average in most settings, while also significantly reducing the number of overdue orders.

标题：UrbanHuRo：面向异构城市服务联合优化的双层人机协作框架

Vision-Zero: Scalable VLM Self-Improvement via Strategic Gamified Self-Play
Authors: Qinsi Wang, Bo Liu, Tianyi Zhou, Jing Shi, Yueqian Lin, Yiran Chen, Hai Helen Li, Kun Wan, Wentian Zhao
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-29T21:55:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T03:35:17+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Although reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a promising approach for improving vision-language models (VLMs) and multimodal large language models (MLLMs), current methods rely heavily on manually curated datasets and costly human verification, which limits scalable self-improvement in multimodal systems. To address this challenge, we propose Vision-Zero, a label-free, domain-agnostic multi-agent self-play framework for self-evolving VLMs through competitive visual games generated from arbitrary image inputs. Specifically, Vision-Zero encompasses three main attributes: (1) Strategic Self-Play Framework: Vision-Zero trains VLMs in "Who Is the Spy"-style games, where the models engage in strategic reasoning and actions across multiple roles. Through interactive gameplay, models autonomously generate their training data without human annotation. (2) Gameplay from Arbitrary Images: Unlike existing gamified frameworks, Vision-Zero can generate games from arbitrary images, thereby enhancing the model's reasoning ability across diverse domains and showing strong generalization to different tasks. We demonstrate this versatility using three distinct types of image datasets: CLEVR-based synthetic scenes, charts, and real-world images. (3) Sustainable Performance Gain: We introduce Iterative Self-Play Policy Optimization (Iterative-SPO), a novel training algorithm that alternates between Self-Play and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), mitigating the performance plateau often seen in self-play-only training and achieving sustained long-term improvements. Despite using label-free data, Vision-Zero achieves state-of-the-art performance on reasoning, chart question answering, and vision-centric understanding tasks, surpassing other annotation-based methods. Models and code have been released at https://github.com/wangqinsi1/Vision-Zero.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Vision-Zero：通过策略性游戏化自我博弈实现可扩展的视觉语言模型自我改进
尽管强化学习已成为改进视觉语言模型和多模态大语言模型的有前景方法，但现有方法严重依赖人工标注数据集和昂贵的人工验证，限制了多模态系统的可扩展自我改进。为应对这一挑战，我们提出Vision-Zero——一种无需标注、领域无关的多智能体自我博弈框架，通过任意图像输入生成的竞争性视觉游戏实现视觉语言模型的自主进化。该框架具备三大特性：（1）策略性自我博弈框架：通过“谁是卧底”式游戏训练模型进行跨角色策略推理与行动，在交互游戏中自主生成训练数据；（2）任意图像生成游戏：突破现有游戏化框架限制，利用任意图像生成游戏，提升模型跨领域推理能力，在合成场景、图表和真实图像三类数据集上均展现强大泛化性；（3）可持续性能增益：提出迭代自我博弈策略优化算法，交替进行自我博弈与可验证奖励的强化学习，突破纯自我博弈的性能瓶颈，实现长期持续改进。实验表明，Vision-Zero在推理、图表问答和视觉理解任务上达到最先进性能，超越基于标注的方法。代码与模型已开源。

本文针对当前基于强化学习的视觉语言模型改进方法依赖人工标注数据和验证、可扩展性受限的问题，提出了一种无需标注、领域无关的多智能体自博弈框架Vision-Zero。该方法通过从任意图像生成竞争性视觉游戏，让模型在类似“谁是卧底”的策略游戏中自主推理并产生训练数据，无需人工干预。实验结果表明，使用合成场景、图表和真实世界图像时，结合迭代自博弈策略优化算法，Vision-Zero在推理、图表问答和视觉中心理解任务上取得了最先进的性能，超越了基于标注的方法，并展现出强大的跨领域泛化能力。
MAGE: Meta-Reinforcement Learning for Language Agents toward Strategic Exploration and Exploitation
Authors: Lu Yang, Zelai Xu, Minyang Xie, Jiaxuan Gao, Zhao Shok, Yu Wang, Yi Wu
First: 2026-03-04T03:14:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T03:14:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Language Model (LLM) agents have demonstrated remarkable proficiency in learned tasks, yet they often struggle to adapt to non-stationary environments with feedback. While In-Context Learning and external memory offer some flexibility, they fail to internalize the adaptive ability required for long-term improvement. Meta-Reinforcement Learning (meta-RL) provides an alternative by embedding the learning process directly within the model. However, existing meta-RL approaches for LLMs focus primarily on exploration in single-agent settings, neglecting the strategic exploitation necessary for multi-agent environments. We propose MAGE, a meta-RL framework that empowers LLM agents for strategic exploration and exploitation. MAGE utilizes a multi-episode training regime where interaction histories and reflections are integrated into the context window. By using the final episode reward as the objective, MAGE incentivizes the agent to refine its strategy based on past experiences. We further combine population-based training with an agent-specific advantage normalization technique to enrich agent diversity and ensure stable learning. Experiment results show that MAGE outperforms existing baselines in both exploration and exploitation tasks. Furthermore, MAGE exhibits strong generalization to unseen opponents, suggesting it has internalized the ability for strategic exploration and exploitation. Code is available at https://github.com/Lu-Yang666/MAGE.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MAGE：面向语言智能体的元强化学习框架，实现策略性探索与利用
大语言模型智能体在已学习任务中展现出卓越能力，但常难以适应带反馈的非平稳环境。尽管上下文学习和外部记忆提供了一定灵活性，却未能内化长期改进所需的适应能力。元强化学习通过将学习过程直接嵌入模型提供了一种替代方案，但现有面向大语言模型的元强化学习方法主要关注单智能体环境中的探索，忽视了多智能体环境所需的策略性利用。我们提出MAGE——一个赋能大语言模型智能体进行策略性探索与利用的元强化学习框架。该框架采用多轮次训练机制，将交互历史与反思整合至上下文窗口，并以最终轮次奖励为目标激励智能体基于历史经验优化策略。我们进一步将群体训练与智能体特定优势归一化技术相结合，以增强智能体多样性并确保稳定学习。实验结果表明，MAGE在探索与利用任务中均优于现有基线方法，且对未见过的对手表现出强大泛化能力，表明其已内化策略性探索与利用的能力。代码发布于https://github.com/Lu-Yang666/MAGE。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the limitation of current LLM agents in adapting to non-stationary environments, as existing methods like In-Context Learning lack internalized long-term adaptive ability, and prior meta-RL approaches overlook strategic exploitation in multi-agent settings. To address this, the authors propose MAGE, a meta-RL framework that trains agents through a multi-episode regime, integrating interaction histories and reflections into the context window and optimizing for final episode reward to refine strategies based on past experiences, while also employing population-based training with advantage normalization to enhance diversity and stability. Experimental results demonstrate that MAGE outperforms baselines in both exploration and exploitation tasks and shows strong generalization to unseen opponents, indicating successful internalization of strategic adaptation.
本文的动机在于现有大型语言模型智能体难以适应非平稳环境，因为上下文学习等方法缺乏内在的长期适应能力，且先前的元强化学习方法在多智能体环境中忽略了战略利用。为此，作者提出了MAGE，一个元强化学习框架，通过多轮训练机制，将交互历史和反思整合到上下文窗口中，并以最终轮次奖励为目标优化策略，同时结合群体训练和优势归一化技术以增强智能体多样性和学习稳定性。实验结果表明，MAGE在探索和利用任务上均优于现有基线，并能很好地泛化到未见过的对手，表明其成功内化了战略探索与利用的能力。
MIND: Unified Inquiry and Diagnosis RL with Criteria Grounded Clinical Supports for Psychiatric Consultation
Authors: Guoyi Li, Shihao Xu, Jiatong Ma, Yunyun Han, Jianhua Chen, Yafeng Deng
First: 2026-03-04T03:05:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T03:05:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have advanced medical dialogue systems, yet psychiatric consultation poses substantially higher demands due to subjective ambiguity and comorbidity complexity: an agent must continuously extract psychopathological cues from incomplete and inconsistent patient reports in multi-turn interactions and perform rigorous differential diagnostic reasoning. However, existing methods face two fundamental challenges. First, without criteria-grounded clinical supports, they are prone to unsupported clinical assertions when symptoms are atypical or underspecified. Second, in multi-turn interactions, they struggle to mitigate inquiry drift (off-topic or low-yield questioning) and optimize questioning strategies. To address these challenges, we propose MIND, a unified inquiry--diagnosis reinforcement learning framework for psychiatric consultation. Specifically, we build a Criteria-Grounded Psychiatric Reasoning Bank (PRB) that summarizes dialogue context into clinical retrieval states, retrieves semantically similar reference consultations, and distills reusable criteria-grounded clinical supports to guide criteria-aligned inquiry and reasoning. Building on this foundation, MIND enforces explicit clinical reasoning with rubric-based process rewards to provide fine-grained supervision over intermediate decision steps, and incorporates a value-aware trajectory rectification mechanism to jointly improve information acquisition and diagnostic decision-making across turns. Extensive experiments demonstrate that MIND consistently outperforms strong baselines in diagnostic accuracy, empathetic interaction quality, interpretability, and generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MIND：基于标准锚定临床支持的统一问诊与诊断强化学习框架用于精神科会诊
大语言模型虽已推动医疗对话系统发展，但精神科会诊因主观模糊性与共病复杂性面临更高要求：智能体需在多轮交互中持续从不完整且矛盾的病患陈述中提取精神病理线索，并进行严谨的鉴别诊断推理。现有方法存在两大根本挑战：其一，缺乏标准锚定的临床支持，易在症状非典型或描述不明确时做出无依据的临床断言；其二，在多轮交互中难以抑制问诊偏移（偏离主题或低效提问）并优化提问策略。为此，我们提出MIND——面向精神科会诊的统一问诊-诊断强化学习框架。具体而言，我们构建了标准锚定精神科推理库，将对话语境归纳为临床检索状态，检索语义相似的参考会诊记录，并提炼可复用的标准锚定临床支持，以指导符合诊断标准的问诊推理。在此基础上，MIND通过基于量规的过程奖励机制强化显性临床推理，对中间决策步骤实施细粒度监督，并引入价值感知轨迹校正机制，协同优化多轮交互中的信息获取与诊断决策。大量实验表明，MIND在诊断准确性、共情交互质量、可解释性及泛化能力方面均持续优于现有基线模型。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the heightened challenges in psychiatric consultation, where large language models struggle with subjective ambiguity and comorbidity, often making unsupported clinical claims and experiencing inquiry drift in multi-turn dialogues. To overcome this, the authors propose MIND, a unified reinforcement learning framework that integrates a Criteria-Grounded Psychiatric Reasoning Bank to distill clinical supports from reference consultations, guiding criteria-aligned inquiry and reasoning. Experimental results show that MIND outperforms baselines in diagnostic accuracy, empathetic interaction quality, interpretability, and generalization.
该论文针对精神科咨询中主观模糊性和共病复杂性带来的挑战，现有大型语言模型易产生无依据的临床断言并在多轮对话中出现询问偏离。为此，作者提出MIND框架，通过构建标准依据的精神科推理库，从参考咨询中提炼临床支持信息，以指导符合标准的询问和推理。实验结果表明，MIND在诊断准确性、共情交互质量、可解释性和泛化能力上均优于基线方法。
Rewards as Labels: Revisiting RLVR from a Classification Perspective
Authors: Zepeng Zhai, Meilin Chen, Jiaxuan Zhao, Junlang Qian, Lei Shen, Yuan Lu
First: 2026-02-05T13:11:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T03:01:17+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 5 figures, 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards has recently advanced the capabilities of Large Language Models in complex reasoning tasks by providing explicit rule-based supervision. Among RLVR methods, GRPO and its variants have achieved strong empirical performance. Despite their success, we identify that they suffer from Gradient Misassignment in Positives and Gradient Domination in Negatives, which lead to inefficient and suboptimal policy updates. To address these issues, we propose Rewards as Labels (REAL), a novel framework that revisits verifiable rewards as categorical labels rather than scalar weights, thereby reformulating policy optimization as a classification problem. Building on this, we further introduce anchor logits to enhance policy learning. Our analysis reveals that REAL induces a monotonic and bounded gradient weighting, enabling balanced gradient allocation across rollouts and effectively mitigating the identified mismatches. Extensive experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that REAL improves training stability and consistently outperforms GRPO and strong variants such as DAPO. On the 1.5B model, REAL improves average Pass@1 over DAPO by 6.7%. These gains further scale to 7B model, REAL continues to outperform DAPO and GSPO by 6.2% and 1.7%, respectively. Notably, even with a vanilla binary cross-entropy, REAL remains stable and exceeds DAPO by 4.5% on average.
中文标题/摘要
标题：奖励作为标签：从分类视角重审RLVR
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）近期通过提供显式的基于规则的监督，显著提升了大型语言模型在复杂推理任务中的能力。在RLVR方法中，GRPO及其变体取得了优异的实证性能。尽管成果显著，我们发现这些方法存在正样本梯度错配与负样本梯度主导问题，导致策略更新效率低下且非最优。为解决这些问题，我们提出奖励作为标签（REAL）框架，将可验证奖励重新定义为分类标签而非标量权重，从而将策略优化重构为分类问题。在此基础上，我们进一步引入锚定逻辑值以增强策略学习。分析表明，REAL能产生单调有界的梯度加权，实现回合间梯度分配的平衡，有效缓解已识别的错配问题。在数学推理基准上的大量实验表明，REAL提升了训练稳定性，并持续超越GRPO及DAPO等强效变体。在15亿参数模型上，REAL的Pass@1平均指标较DAPO提升6.7%。该优势进一步扩展至70亿参数模型，REAL分别以6.2%和1.7%的优势持续超越DAPO与GSPO。值得注意的是，即使采用基础二元交叉熵损失，REAL仍保持稳定，平均性能超越DAPO达4.5%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by identified inefficiencies in existing RLVR methods, specifically Gradient Misassignment in Positives and Gradient Domination in Negatives, this paper proposes the Rewards as Labels (REAL) framework, which reformulates policy optimization as a classification problem by treating verifiable rewards as categorical labels and incorporates anchor logits to enhance learning. The method's analysis shows it enables balanced gradient allocation. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that REAL improves training stability and outperforms strong baselines like GRPO and DAPO, with significant performance gains scaling from 1.5B to 7B parameter models.
本文的动机是解决现有RLVR方法中存在的梯度错配与主导问题，提出了名为REAL的新框架，其核心方法是将可验证奖励视为分类标签而非标量权重，从而将策略优化重构为分类问题，并引入锚定逻辑值以增强学习。分析表明该方法能实现平衡的梯度分配。在数学推理基准上的主要实验结果表明，REAL提升了训练稳定性，并在1.5B和7B参数模型上持续超越了GRPO、DAPO等强基线方法，取得了显著的性能提升。
